## Tiruppavai - 23  
Author: Subramanian.R       Date: January 07, 2010, 11:10:36 AM  
---  
The 23rd song of Tiruppavai, is sung today, the 23rd day of Dhanur,   
Margazhi, month. This is again a simple narrative song, continuing   
the them of waking up Narayana for the early morning bathing.   
The lion in the rainy season, comes out from its sleep, from out   
of the mountain-cave. It makes a roar and looks at the surroundings   
with its fire emitting eyes. O Narayana, the god with hue of blue   
lily, you too come out from your bed and ask us for what purpose,   
we have come to your doorstep, and then bless us.   
The Sri Vaishnava scholars say that the imagery to the lion is indicative of  
Narasimha avatara. Since AndaL has been referring   
to Vamana Avatara, Sri Ramaavatara and Sri Krishnavatara in the next song,  
they say that this song is a discreet reference to Narasimha Avatara.   
Arunachala Siva.
 ---  
Source:[http://web.archive.org/web/20100707061610/http://www.arunachala-ramana.org/forum/index.php?topic=4336.msg10932](http://web.archive.org/web/20100707061610/http://www.arunachala-ramana.org/forum/index.php?topic=4336.msg10932)   
---  

## Tiruppavai - 22  
Author: Subramanian.R       Date: January 06, 2010, 09:32:21 AM  
---  
The 22nd song of Tiruppavai, is sung on this day, the 22nd day   
of Margazhi (Dhanur month). This again is a simple narrative song,   
perhaps with a discreet reference to Duryodana and Arjuna going   
to Krishna while the latter was lying on the bed, for support for   
their war at Gurukshetra.   
We are all coming to you Krishna, leaving all our ego, like the   
great kings who came to you leaving all their self respect, and   
stood beside your bed. Will you not, please direct towards us your lotus like  
eyes full of grace and it will be like sun and moon rising   
together. If you could show your gaze once towards us, all our   
sins will vanish and we shall merge at your lotus feet!   
Arunachala Siva.
 ---  
Source:[http://web.archive.org/web/20100707061547/http://www.arunachala-ramana.org/forum/index.php?topic=4336.0;prev_next=next](http://web.archive.org/web/20100707061547/http://www.arunachala-ramana.org/forum/index.php?topic=4336.0;prev_next=next)   
---  

## Tiruppavai - 24  
Author: Subramanian.R       Date: January 09, 2010, 05:10:39 AM  
---  
Tiruppavai song no. 24 is sung on 24th day of Dhanur, Margazhi   
month, i.e. this year, on 8th Jan 2010. Here AndaL, the saint   
poetess describes the various avataras of Vishnu.   
O Narayana, the One who measured all the worlds with your feet*,   
glory to your feet! O the One who crossed over the ocean to Lanka   
and destroyed the demons**, glory to your valour! O the One who   
killed Sakatasura, glory to your fame! O the One who who killed   
demon who came as a calf and also killed the demon who came in the form of  
a Indian apple tree. O the One who raised   
the Govardhan mountain as an umbrella (to protect the cowherds   
and cows from torrential rains caused by Indra.). Glory to your   
features of courage. Glory to the Spear that is on your hand which   
is a nightmare to your enemies. We have come this early morning   
to sing your glory and attain your grace. Please take pity on us.   
* Vamana-Trivikarama Avatara.   
 Sri Rama Avatara   
 Krishna as a child killed Sakatasura who came in the form of   
 a fast moving cart-wheel.   
 One demon came as a calf to hit Krishna. He lifted that   
 calf and threw it on an Indian apple tree, which was also a   
 form taken by another demon. Both were killed.   
The lifting of Govardhana mountain as an umbrella to protect   
the cows and cowherds, is again in Krishna Avatara. Indra causes   
torrential rains, since puja was denied to him and instead offered   
to Govardhana mountain. Krishna lifted the Govardhana mountain   
with his little finger and raised it so that in the space below cows   
and cowherds rested without affected by rains. It lasted for 7 days.   
Srimad Bhagavatam says that Krishna also made the cows and cowherds to have no  
appetite or thirst or nature calls during these   
seven days!   
Arunachala Siva.
 ---  
Source:[http://web.archive.org/web/20100706101615/http://www.arunachala-ramana.org/forum/index.php?topic=4336.0;prev_next=prev](http://web.archive.org/web/20100706101615/http://www.arunachala-ramana.org/forum/index.php?topic=4336.0;prev_next=prev)

## How to watch the sense 'I am'  
Author: snow                Date: January 07, 2010, 03:06:33 PM  
---  
Nisargadatta Maharaj said that it is very important to watch "I-am-ness" all  
the time. I don't however understand what this sense "I Am" contains. Does it  
include seeing, smelling, hearing etc.? Should I be mindful of these also? Or  
is it enough if I just do like Maharshi said: "Get rid of your present  
thoughts, that is all."   
This however seems a little difficult (atleast when I'm not meditating). But  
would you say that just letting go of thinking is basically all that is  
necessary.
 ---  
Source:[http://web.archive.org/web/20100707040658/http://www.arunachala-ramana.org/forum/index.php?topic=4337.msg10955](http://web.archive.org/web/20100707040658/http://www.arunachala-ramana.org/forum/index.php?topic=4337.msg10955)   
---  

## Re:[1] How to watch the sense 'I am'  
Author: silentgreen         Date: January 08, 2010, 03:54:19 AM  
---  
Dear Snow,   
Good question.   
It is the natural feeling of the sense of "I am" which Nisargadatta Maharaj is  
pointing to.   
This feeling is there even if we shut out our senses. For example: We can close our eyes and shut out the sense of vision. "I am" is still there.   
We can close our ears with our fingers and shut out the sense of hearing. "I  
am" is still there.   
We can close our mouth and shut out the sense of taste. "I am" is still there.   
So what is this "I am" which seems to be independent of senses etc.   
How far can we go towards its source?   
Bhagavan Ramana says to find out, "from where this 'I' arises".   
In the process attention will go towards the pure consciousness within.   
Nisargadatta Maharaj says to remain with the sense of "I am" at its root (as  
far as possible) without allowing thoughts to extend "I am" as "I am this or  
that" (like "I am Henry", "I am a teacher", "I am feeling hot" etc.). The  
effect of this is also to take one towards the pure consciousness within.
 ---  
Source:[http://web.archive.org/web/20100707040658/http://www.arunachala-ramana.org/forum/index.php?topic=4337.msg10955](http://web.archive.org/web/20100707040658/http://www.arunachala-ramana.org/forum/index.php?topic=4337.msg10955)   
---  

## Re:[2] How to watch the sense 'I am'  
Author: Subramanian.R       Date: January 08, 2010, 05:06:31 AM  
---  
The state of I AM is simply I AM.   
It is defintely not I am this or I am that.   
I AM is the state of Existence/Witness.   
Dear snow, it is ver difficult to remain in that I AM. That is why   
Bhagavan Ramana said: Ask for whom this thought? It is for me.   
Who am I? Keep on killing the soldiers coming out of the enemy   
fortress. It is difficult, so Bhagavan said Atma Vidya is very easy.   
It is because, we are carrying huge dirt of thoughts and vasanas,   
from many previous births. Guru's Grace alone will remove it one   
stroke, like the Sun removes the darkness of a room, closed and kept in  
darkness for years.   
Arunachala Siva.
 ---  
Source:[http://web.archive.org/web/20100707040658/http://www.arunachala-ramana.org/forum/index.php?topic=4337.msg10955](http://web.archive.org/web/20100707040658/http://www.arunachala-ramana.org/forum/index.php?topic=4337.msg10955)

## Re:[4] How to watch the sense 'I am'  
Author: Subramanian.R       Date: January 08, 2010, 01:20:24 PM  
---  
Dear snow,   
"I find this one as not powerful question..." \- I am not clear   
as to what this question, which is not powerful, that you refer.   
Kindly let me know.   
Should Bhagavan Ramana be only living in a body, to be our Guru?   
He remained in body for some years. One cannot live for ever in   
body. Further, why do you associate a body, for selecting a guru?   
Only those who are body conscious should worry about the guru being   
in body. Is not His Presence, powerful enough, to be your Guru?   
His Presence is all pervading but the power is felt at its highest   
in His Samadhi as well as in Old Hall, where He sat for 23 years   
and guided devotees. If you visit T'malai next time, kindly sit   
in the Samadhi Hall or Old Hall, for about an hour. You shall   
definitely feel the Power of Presence, engulfing you.   
Arunachala Siva.

## Re:[6] How to watch the sense 'I am'  
Author: Subramanian.R       Date: January 08, 2010, 02:41:04 PM  
---  
Dear snow,   
Yes. Letting go of all thoughts about the objective world - is   
the thoughtless state, that is essential for self enquiry. Thought   
about God within, Bhagavan Ramana says, Atma Nishtaparan, in   
Who am I? is the greatest devotion. Hence this thought should   
be retained till it matures into surrender. Once the total surrender   
becomes your nature, there is no need even for thought of God, since   
there is only God within you and not any more of you.   
The question, for whom this thought arises? is necessary and must   
be continued, till worldly thoughts keep bothering you. At one stage, for  
whom this thought arises? - will not arise at all. That   
is abidance in Self. If this abidance in Self becomes permanent,   
then it is Sahaja Stithi. Thereafter every worldly activity of yours   
will be done by That, as Ribhu Gita, Ch.26 Verse 25 states.   
Arunachala Siva.
 ---  
Source:[http://web.archive.org/web/20100707040658/http://www.arunachala-ramana.org/forum/index.php?topic=4337.msg10955](http://web.archive.org/web/20100707040658/http://www.arunachala-ramana.org/forum/index.php?topic=4337.msg10955)

is just I am, and then one step further. .. which cannot be described.

## Re:[9] How to watch the sense 'I am'  
Author: matthias            Date: January 09, 2010, 06:38:35 PM  
---  
dear snow I would like to anwer your first questions..   
the sense of "Iam" is effortless, so making effort to reach it is  
impossible..you can try but hte more oyu try the more you will be hard in the  
chest, the energy will move to your head and you will find meditaitng is very  
exhausting...   
this is a misstake that I do and others do...so maybe this could save some  
time   
noone has ever seen this "Iam"...it is not an object to meditate about, infact  
the more we try to reach it the more we are in ignorance of our true nature   
warding of thoughts cna be missunderstood, beeing thougtless is nice but  
temporary what we look for is ever present conciousness...wich does not care  
aout our thoughts...so best thing is to be that wich does not care wether  
thoughts are there or not...   
hope I could be of help   
matthias

## Re:[12] How to watch the sense 'I am'  
Author: Nagaraj             Date: January 11, 2010, 05:58:47 PM  
---  
Dear I,   
It takes a mammoth effort to do something, to think and it takes absolutely no  
effort at all to simply be. This is the greatest irony that 'mind' thinks  
other wise and never rests! This is the essence of 'I am'   
Just cast of the very need to understand this and simply be. do not attempt to  
know or even bother to answer your question, cast of your very question  
itself, relax and just be. You do not need to know anything about "I am" that  
is really being 'I am'   
Salutations to Sri Ramana
 ---  
Source:[http://web.archive.org/web/20100707040658/http://www.arunachala-ramana.org/forum/index.php?topic=4337.msg10955](http://web.archive.org/web/20100707040658/http://www.arunachala-ramana.org/forum/index.php?topic=4337.msg10955)

## Re:[13]TAT TVAM ASI  How to watch the sense 'I am'  
Author: srkudai             Date: January 12, 2010, 10:45:22 AM  
---  
Dear Nagaraj,   
This. .. "Cast off everything and just be". .. when you say it, someone takes  
it into the mind. And then, its a memory.   
But moments of anger, jealousy, lust, fear, worry, guilt. .. they come  
automatically. .. very fast. So fast that the person does not get time to  
remember your statement until some time!   
how to cast off everything and just be ?   
If the person is already JUST IS, this is redundant to say.   
if the person is not already JUST IS, this statement does not help him. .. coz  
his mind wont allow him to just be! he has no choice.   
You tell me... you told this. .. just be. .. but do u really remain like that?  
The point is simple. .. anger just comes in a moment's time! IT wont give you  
time enough to refer to your memory and find "who am i sentence" and do it!   
Love!   
Silence

## Re:[14] How to watch the sense 'I am'  
Author: Nagaraj             Date: January 12, 2010, 12:49:09 PM  
---  
Dear I,   
The moment you responded, you are not just being. You - 'I' \- Thoughts just  
don't want to be. see it wants to continue.   
Quote  
But moments of anger, jealousy, lust, fear, worry, guilt. .. they come  
automatically. .. very fast. So fast that the person does not get time to  
remember your statement until some time!   
they don't come automatically, it comes because there is a need for all these  
emotions. To put it more clearly, these emotions arise because when any  
thought which arises and questions the very foundation of you - 'I' \- your  
thoughts, then it responds frantically, anger, fear, etc.. comes because it  
itself is under threat, its place is under question. hence these emotions  
arise.   
And at the same time, if any emotions such as comforting or happiness arises,  
it is nothing but anything that is conforming to what it already knows, it  
feels stronger, its place is assured, hence such emotions.   
emotions such as lust arise because of its inherent need of security to exist  
permanently. Lust need not necessarily be physical, money, material etc.. are  
all accumulated because of insecurity or incmpleteness.   
Quote  
If the person is already JUST IS, this is redundant to say.   
if the person is not already JUST IS, this statement does not help him. .. coz  
his mind wont allow him to just be! he has no choice.   
If the person is already as you say Just Is, then he would not have posted it  
here. and as you say "if the person is not already JUST IS, this statement  
does not help him. .. coz his mind wont allow him to just be! he has no  
choice." is because, thoughts have to die, Manonasham is this. Thoughts - you  
- 'I' need thoughts to survive.   
The very moment you read this post you have already put effort. Just Be is  
zero effort. zero thinking, where you can't see that you are not thinking for  
if you begin to see that you are not thinking, you have put an effort there.  
Just Be.   
Salutations to Sri Ramana

## How to watch the sense 'I am'  
Author: snow                Date: January 07, 2010, 03:06:33 PM  
---  
Nisargadatta Maharaj said that it is very important to watch "I-am-ness" all  
the time. I don't however understand what this sense "I Am" contains. Does it  
include seeing, smelling, hearing etc.? Should I be mindful of these also? Or  
is it enough if I just do like Maharshi said: "Get rid of your present  
thoughts, that is all."   
This however seems a little difficult (atleast when I'm not meditating). But  
would you say that just letting go of thinking is basically all that is  
necessary.
 ---  
Source:[http://web.archive.org/web/20100707040954/http://www.arunachala-ramana.org/forum/index.php?topic=4337.msg10961](http://web.archive.org/web/20100707040954/http://www.arunachala-ramana.org/forum/index.php?topic=4337.msg10961)   
---  

## Re:[1] How to watch the sense 'I am'  
Author: silentgreen         Date: January 08, 2010, 03:54:19 AM  
---  
Dear Snow,   
Good question.   
It is the natural feeling of the sense of "I am" which Nisargadatta Maharaj is  
pointing to.   
This feeling is there even if we shut out our senses. For example: We can close our eyes and shut out the sense of vision. "I am" is still there.   
We can close our ears with our fingers and shut out the sense of hearing. "I  
am" is still there.   
We can close our mouth and shut out the sense of taste. "I am" is still there.   
So what is this "I am" which seems to be independent of senses etc.   
How far can we go towards its source?   
Bhagavan Ramana says to find out, "from where this 'I' arises".   
In the process attention will go towards the pure consciousness within.   
Nisargadatta Maharaj says to remain with the sense of "I am" at its root (as  
far as possible) without allowing thoughts to extend "I am" as "I am this or  
that" (like "I am Henry", "I am a teacher", "I am feeling hot" etc.). The  
effect of this is also to take one towards the pure consciousness within.
 ---  
Source:[http://web.archive.org/web/20100707040954/http://www.arunachala-ramana.org/forum/index.php?topic=4337.msg10961](http://web.archive.org/web/20100707040954/http://www.arunachala-ramana.org/forum/index.php?topic=4337.msg10961)   
---  

## Re:[2] How to watch the sense 'I am'  
Author: Subramanian.R       Date: January 08, 2010, 05:06:31 AM  
---  
The state of I AM is simply I AM.   
It is defintely not I am this or I am that.   
I AM is the state of Existence/Witness.   
Dear snow, it is ver difficult to remain in that I AM. That is why   
Bhagavan Ramana said: Ask for whom this thought? It is for me.   
Who am I? Keep on killing the soldiers coming out of the enemy   
fortress. It is difficult, so Bhagavan said Atma Vidya is very easy.   
It is because, we are carrying huge dirt of thoughts and vasanas,   
from many previous births. Guru's Grace alone will remove it one   
stroke, like the Sun removes the darkness of a room, closed and kept in  
darkness for years.   
Arunachala Siva.
 ---  
Source:[http://web.archive.org/web/20100707040954/http://www.arunachala-ramana.org/forum/index.php?topic=4337.msg10961](http://web.archive.org/web/20100707040954/http://www.arunachala-ramana.org/forum/index.php?topic=4337.msg10961)   
---

## Re:[4] How to watch the sense 'I am'  
Author: Subramanian.R       Date: January 08, 2010, 01:20:24 PM  
---  
Dear snow,   
"I find this one as not powerful question..." \- I am not clear   
as to what this question, which is not powerful, that you refer.   
Kindly let me know.   
Should Bhagavan Ramana be only living in a body, to be our Guru?   
He remained in body for some years. One cannot live for ever in   
body. Further, why do you associate a body, for selecting a guru?   
Only those who are body conscious should worry about the guru being   
in body. Is not His Presence, powerful enough, to be your Guru?   
His Presence is all pervading but the power is felt at its highest   
in His Samadhi as well as in Old Hall, where He sat for 23 years   
and guided devotees. If you visit T'malai next time, kindly sit   
in the Samadhi Hall or Old Hall, for about an hour. You shall   
definitely feel the Power of Presence, engulfing you.   
Arunachala Siva.
 ---

## Re:[6] How to watch the sense 'I am'  
Author: Subramanian.R       Date: January 08, 2010, 02:41:04 PM  
---  
Dear snow,   
Yes. Letting go of all thoughts about the objective world - is   
the thoughtless state, that is essential for self enquiry. Thought   
about God within, Bhagavan Ramana says, Atma Nishtaparan, in   
Who am I? is the greatest devotion. Hence this thought should   
be retained till it matures into surrender. Once the total surrender   
becomes your nature, there is no need even for thought of God, since   
there is only God within you and not any more of you.   
The question, for whom this thought arises? is necessary and must   
be continued, till worldly thoughts keep bothering you. At one stage, for  
whom this thought arises? - will not arise at all. That   
is abidance in Self. If this abidance in Self becomes permanent,   
then it is Sahaja Stithi. Thereafter every worldly activity of yours   
will be done by That, as Ribhu Gita, Ch.26 Verse 25 states.   
Arunachala Siva.
 ---  
Source:[http://web.archive.org/web/20100707040954/http://www.arunachala-ramana.org/forum/index.php?topic=4337.msg10961](http://web.archive.org/web/20100707040954/http://www.arunachala-ramana.org/forum/index.php?topic=4337.msg10961)

dear snow I would like to anwer your first questions..   
the sense of "Iam" is effortless, so making effort to reach it is  
impossible..you can try but hte more oyu try the more you will be hard in the  
chest, the energy will move to your head and you will find meditaitng is very  
exhausting...   
this is a misstake that I do and others do...so maybe this could save some  
time   
noone has ever seen this "Iam"...it is not an object to meditate about, infact  
the more we try to reach it the more we are in ignorance of our true nature   
warding of thoughts cna be missunderstood, beeing thougtless is nice but  
temporary what we look for is ever present conciousness...wich does not care  
aout our thoughts...so best thing is to be that wich does not care wether  
thoughts are there or not...   
hope I could be of help   
matthias

## Re:[12] How to watch the sense 'I am'  
Author: Nagaraj             Date: January 11, 2010, 05:58:47 PM  
---  
Dear I,   
It takes a mammoth effort to do something, to think and it takes absolutely no  
effort at all to simply be. This is the greatest irony that 'mind' thinks  
other wise and never rests! This is the essence of 'I am'   
Just cast of the very need to understand this and simply be. do not attempt to  
know or even bother to answer your question, cast of your very question  
itself, relax and just be. You do not need to know anything about "I am" that  
is really being 'I am'   
Salutations to Sri Ramana
 ---  
Source:[http://web.archive.org/web/20100707040954/http://www.arunachala-ramana.org/forum/index.php?topic=4337.msg10961](http://web.archive.org/web/20100707040954/http://www.arunachala-ramana.org/forum/index.php?topic=4337.msg10961)

## Re:[13]TAT TVAM ASI  How to watch the sense 'I am'  
Author: srkudai             Date: January 12, 2010, 10:45:22 AM  
---  
Dear Nagaraj,   
This. .. "Cast off everything and just be". .. when you say it, someone takes  
it into the mind. And then, its a memory.   
But moments of anger, jealousy, lust, fear, worry, guilt. .. they come  
automatically. .. very fast. So fast that the person does not get time to  
remember your statement until some time!   
how to cast off everything and just be ?   
If the person is already JUST IS, this is redundant to say.   
if the person is not already JUST IS, this statement does not help him. .. coz  
his mind wont allow him to just be! he has no choice.   
You tell me... you told this. .. just be. .. but do u really remain like that?  
The point is simple. .. anger just comes in a moment's time! IT wont give you  
time enough to refer to your memory and find "who am i sentence" and do it!   
Love!   
Silence

## Re:[14] How to watch the sense 'I am'  
Author: Nagaraj             Date: January 12, 2010, 12:49:09 PM  
---  
Dear I,   
The moment you responded, you are not just being. You - 'I' \- Thoughts just  
don't want to be. see it wants to continue.   
Quote  
But moments of anger, jealousy, lust, fear, worry, guilt. .. they come  
automatically. .. very fast. So fast that the person does not get time to  
remember your statement until some time!   
they don't come automatically, it comes because there is a need for all these  
emotions. To put it more clearly, these emotions arise because when any  
thought which arises and questions the very foundation of you - 'I' \- your  
thoughts, then it responds frantically, anger, fear, etc.. comes because it  
itself is under threat, its place is under question. hence these emotions  
arise.   
And at the same time, if any emotions such as comforting or happiness arises,  
it is nothing but anything that is conforming to what it already knows, it  
feels stronger, its place is assured, hence such emotions.   
emotions such as lust arise because of its inherent need of security to exist  
permanently. Lust need not necessarily be physical, money, material etc.. are  
all accumulated because of insecurity or incmpleteness.   
Quote  
If the person is already JUST IS, this is redundant to say.   
if the person is not already JUST IS, this statement does not help him. .. coz  
his mind wont allow him to just be! he has no choice.   
If the person is already as you say Just Is, then he would not have posted it  
here. and as you say "if the person is not already JUST IS, this statement  
does not help him. .. coz his mind wont allow him to just be! he has no  
choice." is because, thoughts have to die, Manonasham is this. Thoughts - you  
- 'I' need thoughts to survive.   
The very moment you read this post you have already put effort. Just Be is  
zero effort. zero thinking, where you can't see that you are not thinking for  
if you begin to see that you are not thinking, you have put an effort there.  
Just Be.   
Salutations to Sri Ramana

## How to watch the sense 'I am'  
Author: snow                Date: January 07, 2010, 03:06:33 PM  
---  
Nisargadatta Maharaj said that it is very important to watch "I-am-ness" all  
the time. I don't however understand what this sense "I Am" contains. Does it  
include seeing, smelling, hearing etc.? Should I be mindful of these also? Or  
is it enough if I just do like Maharshi said: "Get rid of your present  
thoughts, that is all."   
This however seems a little difficult (atleast when I'm not meditating). But  
would you say that just letting go of thinking is basically all that is  
necessary.
 ---  
Source:[http://web.archive.org/web/20100707041029/http://www.arunachala-ramana.org/forum/index.php?topic=4337.msg10962](http://web.archive.org/web/20100707041029/http://www.arunachala-ramana.org/forum/index.php?topic=4337.msg10962)   
---  

## Re:[1] How to watch the sense 'I am'  
Author: silentgreen         Date: January 08, 2010, 03:54:19 AM  
---  
Dear Snow,   
Good question.   
It is the natural feeling of the sense of "I am" which Nisargadatta Maharaj is  
pointing to.   
This feeling is there even if we shut out our senses. For example: We can close our eyes and shut out the sense of vision. "I am" is still there.   
We can close our ears with our fingers and shut out the sense of hearing. "I  
am" is still there.   
We can close our mouth and shut out the sense of taste. "I am" is still there.   
So what is this "I am" which seems to be independent of senses etc.   
How far can we go towards its source?   
Bhagavan Ramana says to find out, "from where this 'I' arises".   
In the process attention will go towards the pure consciousness within.   
Nisargadatta Maharaj says to remain with the sense of "I am" at its root (as  
far as possible) without allowing thoughts to extend "I am" as "I am this or  
that" (like "I am Henry", "I am a teacher", "I am feeling hot" etc.). The  
effect of this is also to take one towards the pure consciousness within.
 ---  
Source:[http://web.archive.org/web/20100707041029/http://www.arunachala-ramana.org/forum/index.php?topic=4337.msg10962](http://web.archive.org/web/20100707041029/http://www.arunachala-ramana.org/forum/index.php?topic=4337.msg10962)   
---  

## Re:[2] How to watch the sense 'I am'  
Author: Subramanian.R       Date: January 08, 2010, 05:06:31 AM  
---  
The state of I AM is simply I AM.   
It is defintely not I am this or I am that.   
I AM is the state of Existence/Witness.   
Dear snow, it is ver difficult to remain in that I AM. That is why   
Bhagavan Ramana said: Ask for whom this thought? It is for me.   
Who am I? Keep on killing the soldiers coming out of the enemy   
fortress. It is difficult, so Bhagavan said Atma Vidya is very easy.   
It is because, we are carrying huge dirt of thoughts and vasanas,   
from many previous births. Guru's Grace alone will remove it one   
stroke, like the Sun removes the darkness of a room, closed and kept in  
darkness for years.   
Arunachala Siva.
 ---  
Source:[http://web.archive.org/web/20100707041029/http://www.arunachala-ramana.org/forum/index.php?topic=4337.msg10962](http://web.archive.org/web/20100707041029/http://www.arunachala-ramana.org/forum/index.php?topic=4337.msg10962)

Dear snow, it is ver difficult to remain in that I AM. That is why   
 **Bhagavan Ramana said: Ask for whom this thought? It is for me.   
Who am I? Keep on killing the soldiers coming out of the enemy   
fortress.  
It is difficult, so Bhagavan said Atma Vidya is very easy.   
It is because, we are carrying huge dirt of thoughts and vasanas,   
from many previous births. **Guru 's Grace alone will remove it one   
stroke, like the Sun removes the darkness of a room, closed and kept in  
darkness for years.   
Arunachala Siva.  
Is this one necessary to say? Isn't it pretty obivious? I find this not to be  
as powerful question to the mind than "Who am I" which is (like Adyashanti  
said) an alarm clock thrown in the dream.   
And can Bhagavan be my guru even though he left his body decades ago?

## Re:[4] How to watch the sense 'I am'  
Author: Subramanian.R       Date: January 08, 2010, 01:20:24 PM  
---  
Dear snow,   
"I find this one as not powerful question..." \- I am not clear   
as to what this question, which is not powerful, that you refer.   
Kindly let me know.   
Should Bhagavan Ramana be only living in a body, to be our Guru?   
He remained in body for some years. One cannot live for ever in   
body. Further, why do you associate a body, for selecting a guru?   
Only those who are body conscious should worry about the guru being   
in body. Is not His Presence, powerful enough, to be your Guru?   
His Presence is all pervading but the power is felt at its highest   
in His Samadhi as well as in Old Hall, where He sat for 23 years   
and guided devotees. If you visit T'malai next time, kindly sit   
in the Samadhi Hall or Old Hall, for about an hour. You shall   
definitely feel the Power of Presence, engulfing you.   
Arunachala Siva.

## Re:[6] How to watch the sense 'I am'  
Author: Subramanian.R       Date: January 08, 2010, 02:41:04 PM  
---  
Dear snow,   
Yes. Letting go of all thoughts about the objective world - is   
the thoughtless state, that is essential for self enquiry. Thought   
about God within, Bhagavan Ramana says, Atma Nishtaparan, in   
Who am I? is the greatest devotion. Hence this thought should   
be retained till it matures into surrender. Once the total surrender   
becomes your nature, there is no need even for thought of God, since   
there is only God within you and not any more of you.   
The question, for whom this thought arises? is necessary and must   
be continued, till worldly thoughts keep bothering you. At one stage, for  
whom this thought arises? - will not arise at all. That   
is abidance in Self. If this abidance in Self becomes permanent,   
then it is Sahaja Stithi. Thereafter every worldly activity of yours   
will be done by That, as Ribhu Gita, Ch.26 Verse 25 states.   
Arunachala Siva.
 ---  
Source:[http://web.archive.org/web/20100707041029/http://www.arunachala-ramana.org/forum/index.php?topic=4337.msg10962](http://web.archive.org/web/20100707041029/http://www.arunachala-ramana.org/forum/index.php?topic=4337.msg10962)   
---

noone has ever seen this "Iam"...it is not an object to meditate about, infact

aout our thoughts...so best thing is to be that wich does not care wether  
thoughts are there or not...

## Re:[12] How to watch the sense 'I am'  
Author: Nagaraj             Date: January 11, 2010, 05:58:47 PM  
---  
Dear I,   
It takes a mammoth effort to do something, to think and it takes absolutely no  
effort at all to simply be. This is the greatest irony that 'mind' thinks  
other wise and never rests! This is the essence of 'I am'   
Just cast of the very need to understand this and simply be. do not attempt to  
know or even bother to answer your question, cast of your very question  
itself, relax and just be. You do not need to know anything about "I am" that  
is really being 'I am'   
Salutations to Sri Ramana
 ---  
Source:[http://web.archive.org/web/20100707041029/http://www.arunachala-ramana.org/forum/index.php?topic=4337.msg10962](http://web.archive.org/web/20100707041029/http://www.arunachala-ramana.org/forum/index.php?topic=4337.msg10962)

Dear Nagaraj,   
This. .. "Cast off everything and just be". .. when you say it, someone takes  
it into the mind. And then, its a memory.   
But moments of anger, jealousy, lust, fear, worry, guilt. .. they come  
automatically. .. very fast. So fast that the person does not get time to  
remember your statement until some time!   
how to cast off everything and just be ?   
If the person is already JUST IS, this is redundant to say.   
if the person is not already JUST IS, this statement does not help him. .. coz  
his mind wont allow him to just be! he has no choice.   
You tell me... you told this. .. just be. .. but do u really remain like that?  
The point is simple. .. anger just comes in a moment's time! IT wont give you  
time enough to refer to your memory and find "who am i sentence" and do it!   
Love!   
Silence

## Re:[14] How to watch the sense 'I am'  
Author: Nagaraj             Date: January 12, 2010, 12:49:09 PM  
---  
Dear I,   
The moment you responded, you are not just being. You - 'I' \- Thoughts just  
don't want to be. see it wants to continue.   
Quote  
But moments of anger, jealousy, lust, fear, worry, guilt. .. they come  
automatically. .. very fast. So fast that the person does not get time to  
remember your statement until some time!   
they don't come automatically, it comes because there is a need for all these  
emotions. To put it more clearly, these emotions arise because when any  
thought which arises and questions the very foundation of you - 'I' \- your  
thoughts, then it responds frantically, anger, fear, etc.. comes because it  
itself is under threat, its place is under question. hence these emotions  
arise.   
And at the same time, if any emotions such as comforting or happiness arises,  
it is nothing but anything that is conforming to what it already knows, it  
feels stronger, its place is assured, hence such emotions.   
emotions such as lust arise because of its inherent need of security to exist  
permanently. Lust need not necessarily be physical, money, material etc.. are  
all accumulated because of insecurity or incmpleteness.   
Quote  
If the person is already JUST IS, this is redundant to say.   
if the person is not already JUST IS, this statement does not help him. .. coz  
his mind wont allow him to just be! he has no choice.   
If the person is already as you say Just Is, then he would not have posted it  
here. and as you say "if the person is not already JUST IS, this statement  
does not help him. .. coz his mind wont allow him to just be! he has no  
choice." is because, thoughts have to die, Manonasham is this. Thoughts - you  
- 'I' need thoughts to survive.   
The very moment you read this post you have already put effort. Just Be is  
zero effort. zero thinking, where you can't see that you are not thinking for  
if you begin to see that you are not thinking, you have put an effort there.  
Just Be.   
Salutations to Sri Ramana

title: How to watch the sense -I am-

## How to watch the sense 'I am'  
Author: snow                Date: January 07, 2010, 03:06:33 PM  
---  
Nisargadatta Maharaj said that it is very important to watch "I-am-ness" all  
the time. I don't however understand what this sense "I Am" contains. Does it  
include seeing, smelling, hearing etc.? Should I be mindful of these also? Or  
is it enough if I just do like Maharshi said: "Get rid of your present  
thoughts, that is all."   
This however seems a little difficult (atleast when I'm not meditating). But  
would you say that just letting go of thinking is basically all that is  
necessary.
 ---  
Source:[http://web.archive.org/web/20100707040751/http://www.arunachala-ramana.org/forum/index.php?topic=4337.msg10980](http://web.archive.org/web/20100707040751/http://www.arunachala-ramana.org/forum/index.php?topic=4337.msg10980)   
---  

## Re:[1] How to watch the sense 'I am'  
Author: silentgreen         Date: January 08, 2010, 03:54:19 AM  
---  
Dear Snow,   
Good question.   
It is the natural feeling of the sense of "I am" which Nisargadatta Maharaj is  
pointing to.   
This feeling is there even if we shut out our senses. For example: We can close our eyes and shut out the sense of vision. "I am" is still there.   
We can close our ears with our fingers and shut out the sense of hearing. "I  
am" is still there.   
We can close our mouth and shut out the sense of taste. "I am" is still there.   
So what is this "I am" which seems to be independent of senses etc.   
How far can we go towards its source?   
Bhagavan Ramana says to find out, "from where this 'I' arises".   
In the process attention will go towards the pure consciousness within.   
Nisargadatta Maharaj says to remain with the sense of "I am" at its root (as  
far as possible) without allowing thoughts to extend "I am" as "I am this or  
that" (like "I am Henry", "I am a teacher", "I am feeling hot" etc.). The  
effect of this is also to take one towards the pure consciousness within.
 ---  
Source:[http://web.archive.org/web/20100707040751/http://www.arunachala-ramana.org/forum/index.php?topic=4337.msg10980](http://web.archive.org/web/20100707040751/http://www.arunachala-ramana.org/forum/index.php?topic=4337.msg10980)   
---  

## Re:[2] How to watch the sense 'I am'  
Author: Subramanian.R       Date: January 08, 2010, 05:06:31 AM  
---  
The state of I AM is simply I AM.   
It is defintely not I am this or I am that.   
I AM is the state of Existence/Witness.   
Dear snow, it is ver difficult to remain in that I AM. That is why   
Bhagavan Ramana said: Ask for whom this thought? It is for me.   
Who am I? Keep on killing the soldiers coming out of the enemy   
fortress. It is difficult, so Bhagavan said Atma Vidya is very easy.   
It is because, we are carrying huge dirt of thoughts and vasanas,   
from many previous births. Guru's Grace alone will remove it one   
stroke, like the Sun removes the darkness of a room, closed and kept in  
darkness for years.   
Arunachala Siva.
 ---  
Source:[http://web.archive.org/web/20100707040751/http://www.arunachala-ramana.org/forum/index.php?topic=4337.msg10980](http://web.archive.org/web/20100707040751/http://www.arunachala-ramana.org/forum/index.php?topic=4337.msg10980)   
---

## Re:[6] How to watch the sense 'I am'  
Author: Subramanian.R       Date: January 08, 2010, 02:41:04 PM  
---  
Dear snow,   
Yes. Letting go of all thoughts about the objective world - is   
the thoughtless state, that is essential for self enquiry. Thought   
about God within, Bhagavan Ramana says, Atma Nishtaparan, in   
Who am I? is the greatest devotion. Hence this thought should   
be retained till it matures into surrender. Once the total surrender   
becomes your nature, there is no need even for thought of God, since   
there is only God within you and not any more of you.   
The question, for whom this thought arises? is necessary and must   
be continued, till worldly thoughts keep bothering you. At one stage, for  
whom this thought arises? - will not arise at all. That   
is abidance in Self. If this abidance in Self becomes permanent,   
then it is Sahaja Stithi. Thereafter every worldly activity of yours   
will be done by That, as Ribhu Gita, Ch.26 Verse 25 states.   
Arunachala Siva.
 ---

## Re:[7] How to watch the sense 'I am'

What is the feeling of existing ? Seek within. What is the feeling on  
existing ? Now.

am, deeper and deeper into the I am you go, beyond the impressions until there  
is just I am, and then one step further. .. which cannot be described.

thoughts are there or not...

## Re:[12] How to watch the sense 'I am'  
Author: Nagaraj             Date: January 11, 2010, 05:58:47 PM  
---  
Dear I,   
It takes a mammoth effort to do something, to think and it takes absolutely no  
effort at all to simply be. This is the greatest irony that 'mind' thinks  
other wise and never rests! This is the essence of 'I am'   
Just cast of the very need to understand this and simply be. do not attempt to  
know or even bother to answer your question, cast of your very question  
itself, relax and just be. You do not need to know anything about "I am" that  
is really being 'I am'   
Salutations to Sri Ramana
 ---  
Source:[http://web.archive.org/web/20100707040751/http://www.arunachala-ramana.org/forum/index.php?topic=4337.msg10980](http://web.archive.org/web/20100707040751/http://www.arunachala-ramana.org/forum/index.php?topic=4337.msg10980)

## Re:[13]TAT TVAM ASI  How to watch the sense 'I am'  
Author: srkudai             Date: January 12, 2010, 10:45:22 AM  
---  
Dear Nagaraj,   
This. .. "Cast off everything and just be". .. when you say it, someone takes  
it into the mind. And then, its a memory.   
But moments of anger, jealousy, lust, fear, worry, guilt. .. they come  
automatically. .. very fast. So fast that the person does not get time to  
remember your statement until some time!   
how to cast off everything and just be ?   
If the person is already JUST IS, this is redundant to say.   
if the person is not already JUST IS, this statement does not help him. .. coz  
his mind wont allow him to just be! he has no choice.   
You tell me... you told this. .. just be. .. but do u really remain like that?  
The point is simple. .. anger just comes in a moment's time! IT wont give you  
time enough to refer to your memory and find "who am i sentence" and do it!   
Love!   
Silence

## Re:[14] How to watch the sense 'I am'  
Author: Nagaraj             Date: January 12, 2010, 12:49:09 PM  
---  
Dear I,   
The moment you responded, you are not just being. You - 'I' \- Thoughts just  
don't want to be. see it wants to continue.   
Quote  
But moments of anger, jealousy, lust, fear, worry, guilt. .. they come  
automatically. .. very fast. So fast that the person does not get time to  
remember your statement until some time!   
they don't come automatically, it comes because there is a need for all these  
emotions. To put it more clearly, these emotions arise because when any  
thought which arises and questions the very foundation of you - 'I' \- your  
thoughts, then it responds frantically, anger, fear, etc.. comes because it  
itself is under threat, its place is under question. hence these emotions  
arise.   
And at the same time, if any emotions such as comforting or happiness arises,  
it is nothing but anything that is conforming to what it already knows, it  
feels stronger, its place is assured, hence such emotions.   
emotions such as lust arise because of its inherent need of security to exist  
permanently. Lust need not necessarily be physical, money, material etc.. are  
all accumulated because of insecurity or incmpleteness.   
Quote  
If the person is already JUST IS, this is redundant to say.   
if the person is not already JUST IS, this statement does not help him. .. coz  
his mind wont allow him to just be! he has no choice.   
If the person is already as you say Just Is, then he would not have posted it  
here. and as you say "if the person is not already JUST IS, this statement  
does not help him. .. coz his mind wont allow him to just be! he has no  
choice." is because, thoughts have to die, Manonasham is this. Thoughts - you  
- 'I' need thoughts to survive.   
The very moment you read this post you have already put effort. Just Be is  
zero effort. zero thinking, where you can't see that you are not thinking for  
if you begin to see that you are not thinking, you have put an effort there.  
Just Be.   
Salutations to Sri Ramana

title: How to watch the sense -I am-

## How to watch the sense 'I am'  
Author: snow                Date: January 07, 2010, 03:06:33 PM  
---  
Nisargadatta Maharaj said that it is very important to watch "I-am-ness" all  
the time. I don't however understand what this sense "I Am" contains. Does it  
include seeing, smelling, hearing etc.? Should I be mindful of these also? Or  
is it enough if I just do like Maharshi said: "Get rid of your present  
thoughts, that is all."   
This however seems a little difficult (atleast when I'm not meditating). But  
would you say that just letting go of thinking is basically all that is  
necessary.
 ---  
Source:[http://web.archive.org/web/20100707040918/http://www.arunachala-ramana.org/forum/index.php?topic=4337.msg10981](http://web.archive.org/web/20100707040918/http://www.arunachala-ramana.org/forum/index.php?topic=4337.msg10981)   
---  

## Re:[1] How to watch the sense 'I am'  
Author: silentgreen         Date: January 08, 2010, 03:54:19 AM  
---  
Dear Snow,   
Good question.   
It is the natural feeling of the sense of "I am" which Nisargadatta Maharaj is  
pointing to.   
This feeling is there even if we shut out our senses. For example: We can close our eyes and shut out the sense of vision. "I am" is still there.   
We can close our ears with our fingers and shut out the sense of hearing. "I  
am" is still there.   
We can close our mouth and shut out the sense of taste. "I am" is still there.   
So what is this "I am" which seems to be independent of senses etc.   
How far can we go towards its source?   
Bhagavan Ramana says to find out, "from where this 'I' arises".   
In the process attention will go towards the pure consciousness within.   
Nisargadatta Maharaj says to remain with the sense of "I am" at its root (as  
far as possible) without allowing thoughts to extend "I am" as "I am this or  
that" (like "I am Henry", "I am a teacher", "I am feeling hot" etc.). The  
effect of this is also to take one towards the pure consciousness within.
 ---  
Source:[http://web.archive.org/web/20100707040918/http://www.arunachala-ramana.org/forum/index.php?topic=4337.msg10981](http://web.archive.org/web/20100707040918/http://www.arunachala-ramana.org/forum/index.php?topic=4337.msg10981)   
---  

## Re:[2] How to watch the sense 'I am'  
Author: Subramanian.R       Date: January 08, 2010, 05:06:31 AM  
---  
The state of I AM is simply I AM.   
It is defintely not I am this or I am that.   
I AM is the state of Existence/Witness.   
Dear snow, it is ver difficult to remain in that I AM. That is why   
Bhagavan Ramana said: Ask for whom this thought? It is for me.   
Who am I? Keep on killing the soldiers coming out of the enemy   
fortress. It is difficult, so Bhagavan said Atma Vidya is very easy.   
It is because, we are carrying huge dirt of thoughts and vasanas,   
from many previous births. Guru's Grace alone will remove it one   
stroke, like the Sun removes the darkness of a room, closed and kept in  
darkness for years.   
Arunachala Siva.
 ---  
Source:[http://web.archive.org/web/20100707040918/http://www.arunachala-ramana.org/forum/index.php?topic=4337.msg10981](http://web.archive.org/web/20100707040918/http://www.arunachala-ramana.org/forum/index.php?topic=4337.msg10981)   
---

## Re:[4] How to watch the sense 'I am'  
Author: Subramanian.R       Date: January 08, 2010, 01:20:24 PM  
---  
Dear snow,   
"I find this one as not powerful question..." \- I am not clear   
as to what this question, which is not powerful, that you refer.   
Kindly let me know.   
Should Bhagavan Ramana be only living in a body, to be our Guru?   
He remained in body for some years. One cannot live for ever in   
body. Further, why do you associate a body, for selecting a guru?   
Only those who are body conscious should worry about the guru being   
in body. Is not His Presence, powerful enough, to be your Guru?   
His Presence is all pervading but the power is felt at its highest   
in His Samadhi as well as in Old Hall, where He sat for 23 years   
and guided devotees. If you visit T'malai next time, kindly sit   
in the Samadhi Hall or Old Hall, for about an hour. You shall   
definitely feel the Power of Presence, engulfing you.   
Arunachala Siva.
 ---

## Re:[6] How to watch the sense 'I am'  
Author: Subramanian.R       Date: January 08, 2010, 02:41:04 PM  
---  
Dear snow,   
Yes. Letting go of all thoughts about the objective world - is   
the thoughtless state, that is essential for self enquiry. Thought   
about God within, Bhagavan Ramana says, Atma Nishtaparan, in   
Who am I? is the greatest devotion. Hence this thought should   
be retained till it matures into surrender. Once the total surrender   
becomes your nature, there is no need even for thought of God, since   
there is only God within you and not any more of you.   
The question, for whom this thought arises? is necessary and must   
be continued, till worldly thoughts keep bothering you. At one stage, for  
whom this thought arises? - will not arise at all. That   
is abidance in Self. If this abidance in Self becomes permanent,   
then it is Sahaja Stithi. Thereafter every worldly activity of yours   
will be done by That, as Ribhu Gita, Ch.26 Verse 25 states.   
Arunachala Siva.
 ---  
Source:[http://web.archive.org/web/20100707040918/http://www.arunachala-ramana.org/forum/index.php?topic=4337.msg10981](http://web.archive.org/web/20100707040918/http://www.arunachala-ramana.org/forum/index.php?topic=4337.msg10981)   
---

warding of thoughts cna be missunderstood, beeing thougtless is nice but  
temporary what we look for is ever present conciousness...wich does not care  
aout our thoughts...so best thing is to be that wich does not care wether  
thoughts are there or not...

## Re:[12] How to watch the sense 'I am'  
Author: Nagaraj             Date: January 11, 2010, 05:58:47 PM  
---  
Dear I,   
It takes a mammoth effort to do something, to think and it takes absolutely no  
effort at all to simply be. This is the greatest irony that 'mind' thinks  
other wise and never rests! This is the essence of 'I am'   
Just cast of the very need to understand this and simply be. do not attempt to  
know or even bother to answer your question, cast of your very question  
itself, relax and just be. You do not need to know anything about "I am" that  
is really being 'I am'   
Salutations to Sri Ramana
 ---

Author: srkudai             Date: January 12, 2010, 10:45:22 AM  
---  
Dear Nagaraj,   
This. .. "Cast off everything and just be". .. when you say it, someone takes  
it into the mind. And then, its a memory.   
But moments of anger, jealousy, lust, fear, worry, guilt. .. they come  
automatically. .. very fast. So fast that the person does not get time to  
remember your statement until some time!   
how to cast off everything and just be ?   
If the person is already JUST IS, this is redundant to say.   
if the person is not already JUST IS, this statement does not help him. .. coz  
his mind wont allow him to just be! he has no choice.   
You tell me... you told this. .. just be. .. but do u really remain like that?  
The point is simple. .. anger just comes in a moment's time! IT wont give you  
time enough to refer to your memory and find "who am i sentence" and do it!   
Love!   
Silence

## Re:[14] How to watch the sense 'I am'  
Author: Nagaraj             Date: January 12, 2010, 12:49:09 PM  
---  
Dear I,   
The moment you responded, you are not just being. You - 'I' \- Thoughts just  
don't want to be. see it wants to continue.   
Quote  
But moments of anger, jealousy, lust, fear, worry, guilt. .. they come  
automatically. .. very fast. So fast that the person does not get time to  
remember your statement until some time!   
they don't come automatically, it comes because there is a need for all these  
emotions. To put it more clearly, these emotions arise because when any  
thought which arises and questions the very foundation of you - 'I' \- your  
thoughts, then it responds frantically, anger, fear, etc.. comes because it  
itself is under threat, its place is under question. hence these emotions  
arise.   
And at the same time, if any emotions such as comforting or happiness arises,  
it is nothing but anything that is conforming to what it already knows, it  
feels stronger, its place is assured, hence such emotions.   
emotions such as lust arise because of its inherent need of security to exist  
permanently. Lust need not necessarily be physical, money, material etc.. are  
all accumulated because of insecurity or incmpleteness.   
Quote  
If the person is already JUST IS, this is redundant to say.   
if the person is not already JUST IS, this statement does not help him. .. coz  
his mind wont allow him to just be! he has no choice.   
If the person is already as you say Just Is, then he would not have posted it  
here. and as you say "if the person is not already JUST IS, this statement  
does not help him. .. coz his mind wont allow him to just be! he has no  
choice." is because, thoughts have to die, Manonasham is this. Thoughts - you  
- 'I' need thoughts to survive.   
The very moment you read this post you have already put effort. Just Be is  
zero effort. zero thinking, where you can't see that you are not thinking for  
if you begin to see that you are not thinking, you have put an effort there.  
Just Be.   
Salutations to Sri Ramana

## How to watch the sense 'I am'  
Author: snow                Date: January 07, 2010, 03:06:33 PM  
---  
Nisargadatta Maharaj said that it is very important to watch "I-am-ness" all  
the time. I don't however understand what this sense "I Am" contains. Does it  
include seeing, smelling, hearing etc.? Should I be mindful of these also? Or  
is it enough if I just do like Maharshi said: "Get rid of your present  
thoughts, that is all."   
This however seems a little difficult (atleast when I'm not meditating). But  
would you say that just letting go of thinking is basically all that is  
necessary.
 ---  
Source:[http://web.archive.org/web/20100707041123/http://www.arunachala-ramana.org/forum/index.php?topic=4337.msg10983](http://web.archive.org/web/20100707041123/http://www.arunachala-ramana.org/forum/index.php?topic=4337.msg10983)   
---  

## Re:[1] How to watch the sense 'I am'  
Author: silentgreen         Date: January 08, 2010, 03:54:19 AM  
---  
Dear Snow,   
Good question.   
It is the natural feeling of the sense of "I am" which Nisargadatta Maharaj is  
pointing to.   
This feeling is there even if we shut out our senses. For example: We can close our eyes and shut out the sense of vision. "I am" is still there.   
We can close our ears with our fingers and shut out the sense of hearing. "I  
am" is still there.   
We can close our mouth and shut out the sense of taste. "I am" is still there.   
So what is this "I am" which seems to be independent of senses etc.   
How far can we go towards its source?   
Bhagavan Ramana says to find out, "from where this 'I' arises".   
In the process attention will go towards the pure consciousness within.   
Nisargadatta Maharaj says to remain with the sense of "I am" at its root (as  
far as possible) without allowing thoughts to extend "I am" as "I am this or  
that" (like "I am Henry", "I am a teacher", "I am feeling hot" etc.). The  
effect of this is also to take one towards the pure consciousness within.
 ---  
Source:[http://web.archive.org/web/20100707041123/http://www.arunachala-ramana.org/forum/index.php?topic=4337.msg10983](http://web.archive.org/web/20100707041123/http://www.arunachala-ramana.org/forum/index.php?topic=4337.msg10983)   
---  

## Re:[2] How to watch the sense 'I am'  
Author: Subramanian.R       Date: January 08, 2010, 05:06:31 AM  
---  
The state of I AM is simply I AM.   
It is defintely not I am this or I am that.   
I AM is the state of Existence/Witness.   
Dear snow, it is ver difficult to remain in that I AM. That is why   
Bhagavan Ramana said: Ask for whom this thought? It is for me.   
Who am I? Keep on killing the soldiers coming out of the enemy   
fortress. It is difficult, so Bhagavan said Atma Vidya is very easy.   
It is because, we are carrying huge dirt of thoughts and vasanas,   
from many previous births. Guru's Grace alone will remove it one   
stroke, like the Sun removes the darkness of a room, closed and kept in  
darkness for years.   
Arunachala Siva.
 ---  
Source:[http://web.archive.org/web/20100707041123/http://www.arunachala-ramana.org/forum/index.php?topic=4337.msg10983](http://web.archive.org/web/20100707041123/http://www.arunachala-ramana.org/forum/index.php?topic=4337.msg10983)   
---

## Re:[4] How to watch the sense 'I am'  
Author: Subramanian.R       Date: January 08, 2010, 01:20:24 PM  
---  
Dear snow,   
"I find this one as not powerful question..." \- I am not clear   
as to what this question, which is not powerful, that you refer.   
Kindly let me know.   
Should Bhagavan Ramana be only living in a body, to be our Guru?   
He remained in body for some years. One cannot live for ever in   
body. Further, why do you associate a body, for selecting a guru?   
Only those who are body conscious should worry about the guru being   
in body. Is not His Presence, powerful enough, to be your Guru?   
His Presence is all pervading but the power is felt at its highest   
in His Samadhi as well as in Old Hall, where He sat for 23 years   
and guided devotees. If you visit T'malai next time, kindly sit   
in the Samadhi Hall or Old Hall, for about an hour. You shall   
definitely feel the Power of Presence, engulfing you.   
Arunachala Siva.

## Re:[6] How to watch the sense 'I am'  
Author: Subramanian.R       Date: January 08, 2010, 02:41:04 PM  
---  
Dear snow,   
Yes. Letting go of all thoughts about the objective world - is   
the thoughtless state, that is essential for self enquiry. Thought   
about God within, Bhagavan Ramana says, Atma Nishtaparan, in   
Who am I? is the greatest devotion. Hence this thought should   
be retained till it matures into surrender. Once the total surrender   
becomes your nature, there is no need even for thought of God, since   
there is only God within you and not any more of you.   
The question, for whom this thought arises? is necessary and must   
be continued, till worldly thoughts keep bothering you. At one stage, for  
whom this thought arises? - will not arise at all. That   
is abidance in Self. If this abidance in Self becomes permanent,   
then it is Sahaja Stithi. Thereafter every worldly activity of yours   
will be done by That, as Ribhu Gita, Ch.26 Verse 25 states.   
Arunachala Siva.
 ---  
Source:[http://web.archive.org/web/20100707041123/http://www.arunachala-ramana.org/forum/index.php?topic=4337.msg10983](http://web.archive.org/web/20100707041123/http://www.arunachala-ramana.org/forum/index.php?topic=4337.msg10983)

Dear I,   
It takes a mammoth effort to do something, to think and it takes absolutely no  
effort at all to simply be. This is the greatest irony that 'mind' thinks  
other wise and never rests! This is the essence of 'I am'   
Just cast of the very need to understand this and simply be. do not attempt to  
know or even bother to answer your question, cast of your very question  
itself, relax and just be. You do not need to know anything about "I am" that  
is really being 'I am'   
Salutations to Sri Ramana

## Re:[14] How to watch the sense 'I am'  
Author: Nagaraj             Date: January 12, 2010, 12:49:09 PM  
---  
Dear I,   
The moment you responded, you are not just being. You - 'I' \- Thoughts just  
don't want to be. see it wants to continue.   
Quote  
But moments of anger, jealousy, lust, fear, worry, guilt. .. they come  
automatically. .. very fast. So fast that the person does not get time to  
remember your statement until some time!   
they don't come automatically, it comes because there is a need for all these  
emotions. To put it more clearly, these emotions arise because when any  
thought which arises and questions the very foundation of you - 'I' \- your  
thoughts, then it responds frantically, anger, fear, etc.. comes because it  
itself is under threat, its place is under question. hence these emotions  
arise.   
And at the same time, if any emotions such as comforting or happiness arises,  
it is nothing but anything that is conforming to what it already knows, it  
feels stronger, its place is assured, hence such emotions.   
emotions such as lust arise because of its inherent need of security to exist  
permanently. Lust need not necessarily be physical, money, material etc.. are  
all accumulated because of insecurity or incmpleteness.   
Quote  
If the person is already JUST IS, this is redundant to say.   
if the person is not already JUST IS, this statement does not help him. .. coz  
his mind wont allow him to just be! he has no choice.   
If the person is already as you say Just Is, then he would not have posted it  
here. and as you say "if the person is not already JUST IS, this statement  
does not help him. .. coz his mind wont allow him to just be! he has no  
choice." is because, thoughts have to die, Manonasham is this. Thoughts - you  
- 'I' need thoughts to survive.   
The very moment you read this post you have already put effort. Just Be is  
zero effort. zero thinking, where you can't see that you are not thinking for  
if you begin to see that you are not thinking, you have put an effort there.  
Just Be.   
Salutations to Sri Ramana

## How to watch the sense 'I am'  
Author: snow                Date: January 07, 2010, 03:06:33 PM  
---  
Nisargadatta Maharaj said that it is very important to watch "I-am-ness" all  
the time. I don't however understand what this sense "I Am" contains. Does it  
include seeing, smelling, hearing etc.? Should I be mindful of these also? Or  
is it enough if I just do like Maharshi said: "Get rid of your present  
thoughts, that is all."   
This however seems a little difficult (atleast when I'm not meditating). But  
would you say that just letting go of thinking is basically all that is  
necessary.
 ---  
Source:[http://web.archive.org/web/20100707041106/http://www.arunachala-ramana.org/forum/index.php?topic=4337.msg10984](http://web.archive.org/web/20100707041106/http://www.arunachala-ramana.org/forum/index.php?topic=4337.msg10984)   
---  

## Re:[1] How to watch the sense 'I am'  
Author: silentgreen         Date: January 08, 2010, 03:54:19 AM  
---  
Dear Snow,   
Good question.   
It is the natural feeling of the sense of "I am" which Nisargadatta Maharaj is  
pointing to.   
This feeling is there even if we shut out our senses. For example: We can close our eyes and shut out the sense of vision. "I am" is still there.   
We can close our ears with our fingers and shut out the sense of hearing. "I  
am" is still there.   
We can close our mouth and shut out the sense of taste. "I am" is still there.   
So what is this "I am" which seems to be independent of senses etc.   
How far can we go towards its source?   
Bhagavan Ramana says to find out, "from where this 'I' arises".   
In the process attention will go towards the pure consciousness within.   
Nisargadatta Maharaj says to remain with the sense of "I am" at its root (as  
far as possible) without allowing thoughts to extend "I am" as "I am this or  
that" (like "I am Henry", "I am a teacher", "I am feeling hot" etc.). The  
effect of this is also to take one towards the pure consciousness within.
 ---  
Source:[http://web.archive.org/web/20100707041106/http://www.arunachala-ramana.org/forum/index.php?topic=4337.msg10984](http://web.archive.org/web/20100707041106/http://www.arunachala-ramana.org/forum/index.php?topic=4337.msg10984)   
---  

## Re:[2] How to watch the sense 'I am'  
Author: Subramanian.R       Date: January 08, 2010, 05:06:31 AM  
---  
The state of I AM is simply I AM.   
It is defintely not I am this or I am that.   
I AM is the state of Existence/Witness.   
Dear snow, it is ver difficult to remain in that I AM. That is why   
Bhagavan Ramana said: Ask for whom this thought? It is for me.   
Who am I? Keep on killing the soldiers coming out of the enemy   
fortress. It is difficult, so Bhagavan said Atma Vidya is very easy.   
It is because, we are carrying huge dirt of thoughts and vasanas,   
from many previous births. Guru's Grace alone will remove it one   
stroke, like the Sun removes the darkness of a room, closed and kept in  
darkness for years.   
Arunachala Siva.
 ---  
Source:[http://web.archive.org/web/20100707041106/http://www.arunachala-ramana.org/forum/index.php?topic=4337.msg10984](http://web.archive.org/web/20100707041106/http://www.arunachala-ramana.org/forum/index.php?topic=4337.msg10984)   
---

## Re:[4] How to watch the sense 'I am'  
Author: Subramanian.R       Date: January 08, 2010, 01:20:24 PM  
---  
Dear snow,   
"I find this one as not powerful question..." \- I am not clear   
as to what this question, which is not powerful, that you refer.   
Kindly let me know.   
Should Bhagavan Ramana be only living in a body, to be our Guru?   
He remained in body for some years. One cannot live for ever in   
body. Further, why do you associate a body, for selecting a guru?   
Only those who are body conscious should worry about the guru being   
in body. Is not His Presence, powerful enough, to be your Guru?   
His Presence is all pervading but the power is felt at its highest   
in His Samadhi as well as in Old Hall, where He sat for 23 years   
and guided devotees. If you visit T'malai next time, kindly sit   
in the Samadhi Hall or Old Hall, for about an hour. You shall   
definitely feel the Power of Presence, engulfing you.   
Arunachala Siva.
 ---

## Re:[6] How to watch the sense 'I am'  
Author: Subramanian.R       Date: January 08, 2010, 02:41:04 PM  
---  
Dear snow,   
Yes. Letting go of all thoughts about the objective world - is   
the thoughtless state, that is essential for self enquiry. Thought   
about God within, Bhagavan Ramana says, Atma Nishtaparan, in   
Who am I? is the greatest devotion. Hence this thought should   
be retained till it matures into surrender. Once the total surrender   
becomes your nature, there is no need even for thought of God, since   
there is only God within you and not any more of you.   
The question, for whom this thought arises? is necessary and must   
be continued, till worldly thoughts keep bothering you. At one stage, for  
whom this thought arises? - will not arise at all. That   
is abidance in Self. If this abidance in Self becomes permanent,   
then it is Sahaja Stithi. Thereafter every worldly activity of yours   
will be done by That, as Ribhu Gita, Ch.26 Verse 25 states.   
Arunachala Siva.
 ---  
Source:[http://web.archive.org/web/20100707041106/http://www.arunachala-ramana.org/forum/index.php?topic=4337.msg10984](http://web.archive.org/web/20100707041106/http://www.arunachala-ramana.org/forum/index.php?topic=4337.msg10984)

dear snow I would like to anwer your first questions..   
the sense of "Iam" is effortless, so making effort to reach it is  
impossible..you can try but hte more oyu try the more you will be hard in the  
chest, the energy will move to your head and you will find meditaitng is very  
exhausting...   
this is a misstake that I do and others do...so maybe this could save some  
time   
noone has ever seen this "Iam"...it is not an object to meditate about, infact  
the more we try to reach it the more we are in ignorance of our true nature   
warding of thoughts cna be missunderstood, beeing thougtless is nice but  
temporary what we look for is ever present conciousness...wich does not care  
aout our thoughts...so best thing is to be that wich does not care wether  
thoughts are there or not...   
hope I could be of help   
matthias

## Re:[12] How to watch the sense 'I am'  
Author: Nagaraj             Date: January 11, 2010, 05:58:47 PM  
---  
Dear I,   
It takes a mammoth effort to do something, to think and it takes absolutely no  
effort at all to simply be. This is the greatest irony that 'mind' thinks  
other wise and never rests! This is the essence of 'I am'   
Just cast of the very need to understand this and simply be. do not attempt to  
know or even bother to answer your question, cast of your very question  
itself, relax and just be. You do not need to know anything about "I am" that  
is really being 'I am'   
Salutations to Sri Ramana
 ---  
Source:[http://web.archive.org/web/20100707041106/http://www.arunachala-ramana.org/forum/index.php?topic=4337.msg10984](http://web.archive.org/web/20100707041106/http://www.arunachala-ramana.org/forum/index.php?topic=4337.msg10984)   
---  

## Re:[13]TAT TVAM ASI  How to watch the sense 'I am'  
Author: srkudai             Date: January 12, 2010, 10:45:22 AM  
---  
Dear Nagaraj,   
This. .. "Cast off everything and just be". .. when you say it, someone takes  
it into the mind. And then, its a memory.   
But moments of anger, jealousy, lust, fear, worry, guilt. .. they come  
automatically. .. very fast. So fast that the person does not get time to  
remember your statement until some time!   
how to cast off everything and just be ?   
If the person is already JUST IS, this is redundant to say.   
if the person is not already JUST IS, this statement does not help him. .. coz  
his mind wont allow him to just be! he has no choice.   
You tell me... you told this. .. just be. .. but do u really remain like that?  
The point is simple. .. anger just comes in a moment's time! IT wont give you  
time enough to refer to your memory and find "who am i sentence" and do it!   
Love!   
Silence

## Re:[14] How to watch the sense 'I am'  
Author: Nagaraj             Date: January 12, 2010, 12:49:09 PM  
---  
Dear I,   
The moment you responded, you are not just being. You - 'I' \- Thoughts just  
don't want to be. see it wants to continue.   
Quote  
But moments of anger, jealousy, lust, fear, worry, guilt. .. they come  
automatically. .. very fast. So fast that the person does not get time to  
remember your statement until some time!   
they don't come automatically, it comes because there is a need for all these  
emotions. To put it more clearly, these emotions arise because when any  
thought which arises and questions the very foundation of you - 'I' \- your  
thoughts, then it responds frantically, anger, fear, etc.. comes because it  
itself is under threat, its place is under question. hence these emotions  
arise.   
And at the same time, if any emotions such as comforting or happiness arises,  
it is nothing but anything that is conforming to what it already knows, it  
feels stronger, its place is assured, hence such emotions.   
emotions such as lust arise because of its inherent need of security to exist  
permanently. Lust need not necessarily be physical, money, material etc.. are  
all accumulated because of insecurity or incmpleteness.   
Quote  
If the person is already JUST IS, this is redundant to say.   
if the person is not already JUST IS, this statement does not help him. .. coz  
his mind wont allow him to just be! he has no choice.   
If the person is already as you say Just Is, then he would not have posted it  
here. and as you say "if the person is not already JUST IS, this statement  
does not help him. .. coz his mind wont allow him to just be! he has no  
choice." is because, thoughts have to die, Manonasham is this. Thoughts - you  
- 'I' need thoughts to survive.   
The very moment you read this post you have already put effort. Just Be is  
zero effort. zero thinking, where you can't see that you are not thinking for  
if you begin to see that you are not thinking, you have put an effort there.  
Just Be.   
Salutations to Sri Ramana

## How to watch the sense 'I am'  
Author: snow                Date: January 07, 2010, 03:06:33 PM  
---  
Nisargadatta Maharaj said that it is very important to watch "I-am-ness" all  
the time. I don't however understand what this sense "I Am" contains. Does it  
include seeing, smelling, hearing etc.? Should I be mindful of these also? Or  
is it enough if I just do like Maharshi said: "Get rid of your present  
thoughts, that is all."   
This however seems a little difficult (atleast when I'm not meditating). But  
would you say that just letting go of thinking is basically all that is  
necessary.
 ---  
Source:[http://web.archive.org/web/20100707041011/http://www.arunachala-ramana.org/forum/index.php?topic=4337.msg10993](http://web.archive.org/web/20100707041011/http://www.arunachala-ramana.org/forum/index.php?topic=4337.msg10993)   
---  

## Re:[1] How to watch the sense 'I am'  
Author: silentgreen         Date: January 08, 2010, 03:54:19 AM  
---  
Dear Snow,   
Good question.   
It is the natural feeling of the sense of "I am" which Nisargadatta Maharaj is  
pointing to.   
This feeling is there even if we shut out our senses. For example: We can close our eyes and shut out the sense of vision. "I am" is still there.   
We can close our ears with our fingers and shut out the sense of hearing. "I  
am" is still there.   
We can close our mouth and shut out the sense of taste. "I am" is still there.   
So what is this "I am" which seems to be independent of senses etc.   
How far can we go towards its source?   
Bhagavan Ramana says to find out, "from where this 'I' arises".   
In the process attention will go towards the pure consciousness within.   
Nisargadatta Maharaj says to remain with the sense of "I am" at its root (as  
far as possible) without allowing thoughts to extend "I am" as "I am this or  
that" (like "I am Henry", "I am a teacher", "I am feeling hot" etc.). The  
effect of this is also to take one towards the pure consciousness within.
 ---  
Source:[http://web.archive.org/web/20100707041011/http://www.arunachala-ramana.org/forum/index.php?topic=4337.msg10993](http://web.archive.org/web/20100707041011/http://www.arunachala-ramana.org/forum/index.php?topic=4337.msg10993)   
---  

## Re:[2] How to watch the sense 'I am'  
Author: Subramanian.R       Date: January 08, 2010, 05:06:31 AM  
---  
The state of I AM is simply I AM.   
It is defintely not I am this or I am that.   
I AM is the state of Existence/Witness.   
Dear snow, it is ver difficult to remain in that I AM. That is why   
Bhagavan Ramana said: Ask for whom this thought? It is for me.   
Who am I? Keep on killing the soldiers coming out of the enemy   
fortress. It is difficult, so Bhagavan said Atma Vidya is very easy.   
It is because, we are carrying huge dirt of thoughts and vasanas,   
from many previous births. Guru's Grace alone will remove it one   
stroke, like the Sun removes the darkness of a room, closed and kept in  
darkness for years.   
Arunachala Siva.
 ---  
Source:[http://web.archive.org/web/20100707041011/http://www.arunachala-ramana.org/forum/index.php?topic=4337.msg10993](http://web.archive.org/web/20100707041011/http://www.arunachala-ramana.org/forum/index.php?topic=4337.msg10993)

as powerful question to the mind than "Who am I" which is (like Adyashanti  
said) an alarm clock thrown in the dream.

## Re:[4] How to watch the sense 'I am'  
Author: Subramanian.R       Date: January 08, 2010, 01:20:24 PM  
---  
Dear snow,   
"I find this one as not powerful question..." \- I am not clear   
as to what this question, which is not powerful, that you refer.   
Kindly let me know.   
Should Bhagavan Ramana be only living in a body, to be our Guru?   
He remained in body for some years. One cannot live for ever in   
body. Further, why do you associate a body, for selecting a guru?   
Only those who are body conscious should worry about the guru being   
in body. Is not His Presence, powerful enough, to be your Guru?   
His Presence is all pervading but the power is felt at its highest   
in His Samadhi as well as in Old Hall, where He sat for 23 years   
and guided devotees. If you visit T'malai next time, kindly sit   
in the Samadhi Hall or Old Hall, for about an hour. You shall   
definitely feel the Power of Presence, engulfing you.   
Arunachala Siva.
 ---

## Re:[6] How to watch the sense 'I am'  
Author: Subramanian.R       Date: January 08, 2010, 02:41:04 PM  
---  
Dear snow,   
Yes. Letting go of all thoughts about the objective world - is   
the thoughtless state, that is essential for self enquiry. Thought   
about God within, Bhagavan Ramana says, Atma Nishtaparan, in   
Who am I? is the greatest devotion. Hence this thought should   
be retained till it matures into surrender. Once the total surrender   
becomes your nature, there is no need even for thought of God, since   
there is only God within you and not any more of you.   
The question, for whom this thought arises? is necessary and must   
be continued, till worldly thoughts keep bothering you. At one stage, for  
whom this thought arises? - will not arise at all. That   
is abidance in Self. If this abidance in Self becomes permanent,   
then it is Sahaja Stithi. Thereafter every worldly activity of yours   
will be done by That, as Ribhu Gita, Ch.26 Verse 25 states.   
Arunachala Siva.
 ---  
Source:[http://web.archive.org/web/20100707041011/http://www.arunachala-ramana.org/forum/index.php?topic=4337.msg10993](http://web.archive.org/web/20100707041011/http://www.arunachala-ramana.org/forum/index.php?topic=4337.msg10993)   
---  

## Re:[7] How to watch the sense 'I am'  
Author: rideforever         Date: January 08, 2010, 07:07:14 PM  
---  
What is the feeling of existing ? Seek within. What is the feeling on  
existing ? Now.   
Sometimes I call myself to find myself : Q : hello ? A : hmm ? Q: hello ?  
A:ar hmmm ? Q:hello ? A:... I am here ?   
But I am is coloured by the impressions/conditioning picked up. Holding the I  
am, deeper and deeper into the I am you go, beyond the impressions until there  
is just I am, and then one step further. .. which cannot be described.

dear snow I would like to anwer your first questions..   
the sense of "Iam" is effortless, so making effort to reach it is  
impossible..you can try but hte more oyu try the more you will be hard in the  
chest, the energy will move to your head and you will find meditaitng is very  
exhausting...   
this is a misstake that I do and others do...so maybe this could save some  
time   
noone has ever seen this "Iam"...it is not an object to meditate about, infact  
the more we try to reach it the more we are in ignorance of our true nature   
warding of thoughts cna be missunderstood, beeing thougtless is nice but  
temporary what we look for is ever present conciousness...wich does not care  
aout our thoughts...so best thing is to be that wich does not care wether  
thoughts are there or not...   
hope I could be of help   
matthias

## Re:[12] How to watch the sense 'I am'  
Author: Nagaraj             Date: January 11, 2010, 05:58:47 PM  
---  
Dear I,   
It takes a mammoth effort to do something, to think and it takes absolutely no  
effort at all to simply be. This is the greatest irony that 'mind' thinks  
other wise and never rests! This is the essence of 'I am'   
Just cast of the very need to understand this and simply be. do not attempt to  
know or even bother to answer your question, cast of your very question  
itself, relax and just be. You do not need to know anything about "I am" that  
is really being 'I am'   
Salutations to Sri Ramana
 ---  
Source:[http://web.archive.org/web/20100707041011/http://www.arunachala-ramana.org/forum/index.php?topic=4337.msg10993](http://web.archive.org/web/20100707041011/http://www.arunachala-ramana.org/forum/index.php?topic=4337.msg10993)
