## Re:[22] How to watch the sense 'I am'  
Author: Subramanian.R       Date: January 13, 2010, 05:45:58 AM  
---  
Bhagavan Ramana has said the following on the various points   
mentioned: 1. Desiring the Self is the only desire that one can have. If   
desire is meant as vasana, this is the only vasana that one can   
have.   
2. Bhagavan Ramana did write books, did have some thoughts,   
why only thoughts, He did have dreams too. He did drinking   
and sleeping. He has said that this is done by the Pure Mind   
or Suddha Manas, or Sattva Manas, which does not produce   
any prarabdha effect. It is from the Pure Mind, which is like   
the burnt rope. The burnt rope has only a form but of little   
use for any activity i.e. activity that we normally mean.   
He has also said that the Self does everything that a self realized   
jnani does. It is an advaitic paradox. Sri Sankara did all the work,   
including pilgrimages (which Bhagavan Ramana did not do) with   
this Pure Mind or the Self. It is said in Tamil - Ninaiyamal ninainthu...  
thinking without thinking, sollaamal solli. .. telling   
without telling.... kaanaamal kandu....seeing without seeing.   
It is like doing acitivity in a dream. He has said this to Maurice   
Frydman in one of His conversations.   
Arunachala Siva.
 ---  
Source:[http://web.archive.org/web/20100707045414/http://www.arunachala-ramana.org/forum/index.php?topic=4337.msg11081](http://web.archive.org/web/20100707045414/http://www.arunachala-ramana.org/forum/index.php?topic=4337.msg11081)   
---

1\. The moment one does something if its lost. .. than Ramana was doing so  
many things! what do u intend to say?   
2.what kind of self inquiry are you talking about Nagaraj?   
When a thought came. ..   
and you remembered that you have to question to whom it has come...   
the original thought is already over. the thought now is this remembrance.   
while the illusion is created as if you are killing the previous thought!!   
and if u did not remember, you cannot ask the question either.   
so u sit for just be. .. and the thought arose. .. it did not ask u permission  
to arise. it just arose.... and nothing can be done about it! u try it  
tomorrow. just sit. thought arises. when you remembered your self inquiry and  
tried to use it to "resolve that thought". .. this remembrance is slow. by  
that time the thought has already passed away.   
infact the reason u r saying this always but not doing it is. .. u r not able  
to do it. .. coz its impractical!

I am trying to understand whether it can be classified as a thoughtful or  
thoughtless activity.  
Why do you - 'I' want to know, whether eating and drinking also is part of  
effort and whether one has to refrain from them to "Just Be" \- please see,  
this very need is taking you - 'I' away from Just Being. This is what you -  
'I' \- Mind - Thought is doing. Questioning!   
Just for purposes of clarity, in a thoughtless (state) what matters to you -  
'I' ? why speculate about it now Thinking about it? what ever you think about  
it now, is going to be false as it falls in the realms of thoughts only!   
A honest answer thought can give is - "you - thought - 'I' will know answer  
for your question only in thought-less (state) {in reality you will never know  
for you - thoughts will never be there to know this answer}   
Ideally, Ramana Mahashi would say, first get to the thoughtless (state) and  
then ask this question.   
You - 'I' (as in - Thoughts) can never know Manonasham (state) what ever you  
know is just thought alone! Please see, it is you - 'I' \- Mind - thought that  
is just hungry for thinking - Thoughts, Mind just want to procreate for  
continuity for eternity.   
Please see, as I mentioned in other posts about the Sushupti (State), is there  
any hunger, thirst, life, Body, others, world, are you there? where are these  
questions about the effort and effortlessness, activity and inactivity!   
Salutations to Sri Ramana

How to watch the sense 'I am'

of it and you will not succeed. When you are defeated in such a way, you'll  
see how to watch it.

## Re:[20] How to watch the sense 'I am'

dear rideforever you said   
" Please help me understand. You say do not try. .. so you mean do nothing ?  
Or are you saying do something subtle ?"**   
try as you like, it is ok to meditate, to make effort..but know that all  
effort is contraproductive as a mental concentration activity..   
what we look for is eternal, everpresent concioussness...and it is simply the  
arising of htis moment..not a big thing..just this   
now tell me Who creates thsi moment...if you found a personality who makes  
this moment   
then tell me next who sustains this moment?   
if you can find someone then show me a person who transcends this moment...   
oyu will never find anything apart from this moment...no sustainer no creator  
no destroyer   
it simply is...and no one is there to make this...yo effor tis senseless...but  
still we need to make effort daily   
its a paradox but a very gentle and loving paradox..so make effort, hard  
effort and then more and more subtle but know deeply understand deeply that it  
is for nothing because there is no one to achive enlightment, enlightment is  
allready (primordially) the nature of htis moment...it is self arising,  
spontanious samadhi   
you cannot reach it, you cannot miss it, you can not grasp it hold it or  
whatever...so best thing is to relax...

the other side 5%.

relaxing. Stop looking. Forget it.

## Re:[22] How to watch the sense 'I am'  
Author: Subramanian.R       Date: January 13, 2010, 05:45:58 AM  
---  
Bhagavan Ramana has said the following on the various points   
mentioned: 1. Desiring the Self is the only desire that one can have. If   
desire is meant as vasana, this is the only vasana that one can   
have.   
2. Bhagavan Ramana did write books, did have some thoughts,   
why only thoughts, He did have dreams too. He did drinking   
and sleeping. He has said that this is done by the Pure Mind   
or Suddha Manas, or Sattva Manas, which does not produce   
any prarabdha effect. It is from the Pure Mind, which is like   
the burnt rope. The burnt rope has only a form but of little   
use for any activity i.e. activity that we normally mean.   
He has also said that the Self does everything that a self realized   
jnani does. It is an advaitic paradox. Sri Sankara did all the work,   
including pilgrimages (which Bhagavan Ramana did not do) with   
this Pure Mind or the Self. It is said in Tamil - Ninaiyamal ninainthu...  
thinking without thinking, sollaamal solli. .. telling   
without telling.... kaanaamal kandu....seeing without seeing.   
It is like doing acitivity in a dream. He has said this to Maurice   
Frydman in one of His conversations.   
Arunachala Siva.
 ---  
Source:[http://web.archive.org/web/20100707045310/http://www.arunachala-ramana.org/forum/index.php?topic=4337.msg11082](http://web.archive.org/web/20100707045310/http://www.arunachala-ramana.org/forum/index.php?topic=4337.msg11082)

## Re:[16]TAT TVAM ASI  How to watch the sense 'I am'  
Author: srkudai             Date: January 12, 2010, 02:32:38 PM  
---  
1\. The moment one does something if its lost. .. than Ramana was doing so  
many things! what do u intend to say?   
2.what kind of self inquiry are you talking about Nagaraj?   
When a thought came. ..   
and you remembered that you have to question to whom it has come...   
the original thought is already over. the thought now is this remembrance.   
while the illusion is created as if you are killing the previous thought!!   
and if u did not remember, you cannot ask the question either.   
so u sit for just be. .. and the thought arose. .. it did not ask u permission  
to arise. it just arose.... and nothing can be done about it! u try it  
tomorrow. just sit. thought arises. when you remembered your self inquiry and  
tried to use it to "resolve that thought". .. this remembrance is slow. by  
that time the thought has already passed away.   
infact the reason u r saying this always but not doing it is. .. u r not able  
to do it. .. coz its impractical!   
Love!   
Silence

## Re:[17] How to watch the sense 'I am'  
Author: Nagaraj             Date: January 12, 2010, 04:24:58 PM  
---  
Dear I,   
Quote from: silentgreen on January 12, 2010, 01:13:29 PM  
Is eating and drinking also part of effort and one requires to refrain from  
them to "Just Be"?   
What do you say?   
I am trying to understand whether it can be classified as a thoughtful or  
thoughtless activity.  
Why do you - 'I' want to know, whether eating and drinking also is part of  
effort and whether one has to refrain from them to "Just Be" \- please see,  
this very need is taking you - 'I' away from Just Being. This is what you -  
'I' \- Mind - Thought is doing. Questioning!   
Just for purposes of clarity, in a thoughtless (state) what matters to you -  
'I' ? why speculate about it now Thinking about it? what ever you think about  
it now, is going to be false as it falls in the realms of thoughts only!   
A honest answer thought can give is - "you - thought - 'I' will know answer  
for your question only in thought-less (state) {in reality you will never know  
for you - thoughts will never be there to know this answer}   
Ideally, Ramana Mahashi would say, first get to the thoughtless (state) and  
then ask this question.   
You - 'I' (as in - Thoughts) can never know Manonasham (state) what ever you  
know is just thought alone! Please see, it is you - 'I' \- Mind - thought that  
is just hungry for thinking - Thoughts, Mind just want to procreate for  
continuity for eternity.   
Please see, as I mentioned in other posts about the Sushupti (State), is there  
any hunger, thirst, life, Body, others, world, are you there? where are these  
questions about the effort and effortlessness, activity and inactivity!   
Salutations to Sri Ramana

## Re:[19] How to watch the sense 'I am'  
Author: Vladimir            Date: January 12, 2010, 08:19:10 PM  
---  
Quote  
How to watch the sense 'I am'  
Dear Snow,   
Sence of "I am" is what watches so called "you" all the time. Try to get rid  
of it and you will not succeed. When you are defeated in such a way, you'll  
see how to watch it.

## Re:[20] How to watch the sense 'I am'  
Author: matthias            Date: January 12, 2010, 09:52:26 PM  
---  
dear rideforever you said   
" Please help me understand. You say do not try. .. so you mean do nothing ?  
Or are you saying do something subtle ?"**   
try as you like, it is ok to meditate, to make effort..but know that all  
effort is contraproductive as a mental concentration activity..   
what we look for is eternal, everpresent concioussness...and it is simply the  
arising of htis moment..not a big thing..just this   
now tell me Who creates thsi moment...if you found a personality who makes  
this moment   
then tell me next who sustains this moment?   
if you can find someone then show me a person who transcends this moment...   
oyu will never find anything apart from this moment...no sustainer no creator  
no destroyer   
it simply is...and no one is there to make this...yo effor tis senseless...but  
still we need to make effort daily   
its a paradox but a very gentle and loving paradox..so make effort, hard  
effort and then more and more subtle but know deeply understand deeply that it  
is for nothing because there is no one to achive enlightment, enlightment is  
allready (primordially) the nature of htis moment...it is self arising,  
spontanious samadhi   
you cannot reach it, you cannot miss it, you can not grasp it hold it or  
whatever...so best thing is to relax...

## Re:[21] How to watch the sense 'I am'  
Author: rideforever         Date: January 12, 2010, 10:04:48 PM  
---  
Quote from: matthias on January 12, 2010, 09:52:26 PM  
what we look for. ..   
so best thing is to relax...   
If you are looking or if you are relaxing, you are doing something.   
"Is there any meaning in wanting to be a jnani ?", or does enlightenment just  
happen ?   
"Is it possible to make an effort to be a jnani ?"   
"Why did Sri Ramana write a book about jnana ? reading a book is gaining a  
vasana"   
Yes, I think, wanting to be a jnana might have some value. I am not saying  
definitely, I am saying there is a possibility that it would help to want to  
be a jnana.   
The instruction "hold onto the I-feeling". This is a vasana. Can it help you  
? Perhaps.   
Perhaps if you have a small amount of wanting, a small amount of doing, it can  
take you 95% on the path, and then you give that up and you are pulled from  
the other side 5%.   
If you think that any effort is against jnana, then stop being a jnana. Stop  
relaxing. Stop looking. Forget it.
 ---

## Re:[22] How to watch the sense 'I am'  
Author: Subramanian.R       Date: January 13, 2010, 05:45:58 AM  
---  
Bhagavan Ramana has said the following on the various points   
mentioned: 1. Desiring the Self is the only desire that one can have. If   
desire is meant as vasana, this is the only vasana that one can   
have.   
2. Bhagavan Ramana did write books, did have some thoughts,   
why only thoughts, He did have dreams too. He did drinking   
and sleeping. He has said that this is done by the Pure Mind   
or Suddha Manas, or Sattva Manas, which does not produce   
any prarabdha effect. It is from the Pure Mind, which is like   
the burnt rope. The burnt rope has only a form but of little   
use for any activity i.e. activity that we normally mean.   
He has also said that the Self does everything that a self realized   
jnani does. It is an advaitic paradox. Sri Sankara did all the work,   
including pilgrimages (which Bhagavan Ramana did not do) with   
this Pure Mind or the Self. It is said in Tamil - Ninaiyamal ninainthu...  
thinking without thinking, sollaamal solli. .. telling   
without telling.... kaanaamal kandu....seeing without seeing.   
It is like doing acitivity in a dream. He has said this to Maurice   
Frydman in one of His conversations.   
Arunachala Siva.
 ---  
Source:[http://web.archive.org/web/20100707045451/http://www.arunachala-ramana.org/forum/index.php?topic=4337.msg11087](http://web.archive.org/web/20100707045451/http://www.arunachala-ramana.org/forum/index.php?topic=4337.msg11087)   
---

'I' \- Mind - Thought is doing. Questioning!   
Just for purposes of clarity, in a thoughtless (state) what matters to you -  
'I' ? why speculate about it now Thinking about it? what ever you think about  
it now, is going to be false as it falls in the realms of thoughts only!   
A honest answer thought can give is - "you - thought - 'I' will know answer  
for your question only in thought-less (state) {in reality you will never know  
for you - thoughts will never be there to know this answer}   
Ideally, Ramana Mahashi would say, first get to the thoughtless (state) and  
then ask this question.   
You - 'I' (as in - Thoughts) can never know Manonasham (state) what ever you  
know is just thought alone! Please see, it is you - 'I' \- Mind - thought that  
is just hungry for thinking - Thoughts, Mind just want to procreate for  
continuity for eternity.   
Please see, as I mentioned in other posts about the Sushupti (State), is there  
any hunger, thirst, life, Body, others, world, are you there? where are these  
questions about the effort and effortlessness, activity and inactivity!   
Salutations to Sri Ramana

When a thought came. ..

the original thought is already over. the thought now is this remembrance.   
while the illusion is created as if you are killing the previous thought!!

tomorrow. just sit. thought arises. when you remembered your self inquiry and  
tried to use it to "resolve that thought". .. this remembrance is slow. by  
that time the thought has already passed away.   
infact the reason u r saying this always but not doing it is. .. u r not able

How to watch the sense 'I am'  
Dear Snow,   
Sence of "I am" is what watches so called "you" all the time. Try to get rid

see how to watch it.

## Re:[20] How to watch the sense 'I am'  
Author: matthias            Date: January 12, 2010, 09:52:26 PM  
---  
dear rideforever you said   
" Please help me understand. You say do not try. .. so you mean do nothing ?  
Or are you saying do something subtle ?"**   
try as you like, it is ok to meditate, to make effort..but know that all  
effort is contraproductive as a mental concentration activity..   
what we look for is eternal, everpresent concioussness...and it is simply the  
arising of htis moment..not a big thing..just this   
now tell me Who creates thsi moment...if you found a personality who makes  
this moment   
then tell me next who sustains this moment?   
if you can find someone then show me a person who transcends this moment...   
oyu will never find anything apart from this moment...no sustainer no creator  
no destroyer   
it simply is...and no one is there to make this...yo effor tis senseless...but  
still we need to make effort daily   
its a paradox but a very gentle and loving paradox..so make effort, hard  
effort and then more and more subtle but know deeply understand deeply that it  
is for nothing because there is no one to achive enlightment, enlightment is  
allready (primordially) the nature of htis moment...it is self arising,  
spontanious samadhi   
you cannot reach it, you cannot miss it, you can not grasp it hold it or  
whatever...so best thing is to relax...
 ---

## Re:[21] How to watch the sense 'I am'  
Author: rideforever         Date: January 12, 2010, 10:04:48 PM  
---  
Quote from: matthias on January 12, 2010, 09:52:26 PM  
what we look for. ..   
so best thing is to relax...   
If you are looking or if you are relaxing, you are doing something.   
"Is there any meaning in wanting to be a jnani ?", or does enlightenment just  
happen ?   
"Is it possible to make an effort to be a jnani ?"   
"Why did Sri Ramana write a book about jnana ? reading a book is gaining a  
vasana"   
Yes, I think, wanting to be a jnana might have some value. I am not saying  
definitely, I am saying there is a possibility that it would help to want to  
be a jnana.   
The instruction "hold onto the I-feeling". This is a vasana. Can it help you  
? Perhaps.   
Perhaps if you have a small amount of wanting, a small amount of doing, it can  
take you 95% on the path, and then you give that up and you are pulled from  
the other side 5%.   
If you think that any effort is against jnana, then stop being a jnana. Stop  
relaxing. Stop looking. Forget it.
 ---  
Source:[http://web.archive.org/web/20100707045228/http://www.arunachala-ramana.org/forum/index.php?topic=4337.msg11091](http://web.archive.org/web/20100707045228/http://www.arunachala-ramana.org/forum/index.php?topic=4337.msg11091)

## Re:[22] How to watch the sense 'I am'  
Author: Subramanian.R       Date: January 13, 2010, 05:45:58 AM  
---  
Bhagavan Ramana has said the following on the various points   
mentioned: 1. Desiring the Self is the only desire that one can have. If   
desire is meant as vasana, this is the only vasana that one can   
have.   
2. Bhagavan Ramana did write books, did have some thoughts,   
why only thoughts, He did have dreams too. He did drinking   
and sleeping. He has said that this is done by the Pure Mind   
or Suddha Manas, or Sattva Manas, which does not produce   
any prarabdha effect. It is from the Pure Mind, which is like   
the burnt rope. The burnt rope has only a form but of little   
use for any activity i.e. activity that we normally mean.   
He has also said that the Self does everything that a self realized   
jnani does. It is an advaitic paradox. Sri Sankara did all the work,   
including pilgrimages (which Bhagavan Ramana did not do) with   
this Pure Mind or the Self. It is said in Tamil - Ninaiyamal ninainthu...  
thinking without thinking, sollaamal solli. .. telling   
without telling.... kaanaamal kandu....seeing without seeing.   
It is like doing acitivity in a dream. He has said this to Maurice   
Frydman in one of His conversations.   
Arunachala Siva.
 ---  
Source:[http://web.archive.org/web/20100707045228/http://www.arunachala-ramana.org/forum/index.php?topic=4337.msg11091](http://web.archive.org/web/20100707045228/http://www.arunachala-ramana.org/forum/index.php?topic=4337.msg11091)   
---

## Re:[16]TAT TVAM ASI  How to watch the sense 'I am'  
Author: srkudai             Date: January 12, 2010, 02:32:38 PM

1\. The moment one does something if its lost. .. than Ramana was doing so  
many things! what do u intend to say?   
2.what kind of self inquiry are you talking about Nagaraj?   
When a thought came. ..   
and you remembered that you have to question to whom it has come...   
the original thought is already over. the thought now is this remembrance.   
while the illusion is created as if you are killing the previous thought!!   
and if u did not remember, you cannot ask the question either.   
so u sit for just be. .. and the thought arose. .. it did not ask u permission  
to arise. it just arose.... and nothing can be done about it! u try it  
tomorrow. just sit. thought arises. when you remembered your self inquiry and  
tried to use it to "resolve that thought". .. this remembrance is slow. by  
that time the thought has already passed away.   
infact the reason u r saying this always but not doing it is. .. u r not able  
to do it. .. coz its impractical!   
Love!

vasana"   
Yes, I think, wanting to be a jnana might have some value. I am not saying  
definitely, I am saying there is a possibility that it would help to want to  
be a jnana.   
The instruction "hold onto the I-feeling". This is a vasana. Can it help you  
? Perhaps.   
Perhaps if you have a small amount of wanting, a small amount of doing, it can  
take you 95% on the path, and then you give that up and you are pulled from  
the other side 5%.   
If you think that any effort is against jnana, then stop being a jnana. Stop  
relaxing. Stop looking. Forget it.
 ---  
Source:[http://web.archive.org/web/20100707045333/http://www.arunachala-ramana.org/forum/index.php?topic=4337.msg11093](http://web.archive.org/web/20100707045333/http://www.arunachala-ramana.org/forum/index.php?topic=4337.msg11093)   
---  

## Re:[22] How to watch the sense 'I am'  
Author: Subramanian.R       Date: January 13, 2010, 05:45:58 AM  
---  
Bhagavan Ramana has said the following on the various points   
mentioned: 1. Desiring the Self is the only desire that one can have. If   
desire is meant as vasana, this is the only vasana that one can   
have.   
2. Bhagavan Ramana did write books, did have some thoughts,   
why only thoughts, He did have dreams too. He did drinking   
and sleeping. He has said that this is done by the Pure Mind   
or Suddha Manas, or Sattva Manas, which does not produce   
any prarabdha effect. It is from the Pure Mind, which is like   
the burnt rope. The burnt rope has only a form but of little   
use for any activity i.e. activity that we normally mean.   
He has also said that the Self does everything that a self realized   
jnani does. It is an advaitic paradox. Sri Sankara did all the work,   
including pilgrimages (which Bhagavan Ramana did not do) with   
this Pure Mind or the Self. It is said in Tamil - Ninaiyamal ninainthu...  
thinking without thinking, sollaamal solli. .. telling   
without telling.... kaanaamal kandu....seeing without seeing.   
It is like doing acitivity in a dream. He has said this to Maurice   
Frydman in one of His conversations.   
Arunachala Siva.
 ---  
Source:[http://web.archive.org/web/20100707045333/http://www.arunachala-ramana.org/forum/index.php?topic=4337.msg11093](http://web.archive.org/web/20100707045333/http://www.arunachala-ramana.org/forum/index.php?topic=4337.msg11093)   
---

1\. The moment one does something if its lost. .. than Ramana was doing so  
many things! what do u intend to say?   
2.what kind of self inquiry are you talking about Nagaraj?   
When a thought came. ..   
and you remembered that you have to question to whom it has come...   
the original thought is already over. the thought now is this remembrance.   
while the illusion is created as if you are killing the previous thought!!   
and if u did not remember, you cannot ask the question either.   
so u sit for just be. .. and the thought arose. .. it did not ask u permission  
to arise. it just arose.... and nothing can be done about it! u try it  
tomorrow. just sit. thought arises. when you remembered your self inquiry and  
tried to use it to "resolve that thought". .. this remembrance is slow. by  
that time the thought has already passed away.   
infact the reason u r saying this always but not doing it is. .. u r not able  
to do it. .. coz its impractical!

Dear I,

Is eating and drinking also part of effort and one requires to refrain from

I am trying to understand whether it can be classified as a thoughtful or  
thoughtless activity.  
Why do you - 'I' want to know, whether eating and drinking also is part of  
effort and whether one has to refrain from them to "Just Be" \- please see,  
this very need is taking you - 'I' away from Just Being. This is what you -  
'I' \- Mind - Thought is doing. Questioning!   
Just for purposes of clarity, in a thoughtless (state) what matters to you -  
'I' ? why speculate about it now Thinking about it? what ever you think about  
it now, is going to be false as it falls in the realms of thoughts only!   
A honest answer thought can give is - "you - thought - 'I' will know answer  
for your question only in thought-less (state) {in reality you will never know  
for you - thoughts will never be there to know this answer}   
Ideally, Ramana Mahashi would say, first get to the thoughtless (state) and  
then ask this question.   
You - 'I' (as in - Thoughts) can never know Manonasham (state) what ever you  
know is just thought alone! Please see, it is you - 'I' \- Mind - thought that  
is just hungry for thinking - Thoughts, Mind just want to procreate for  
continuity for eternity.   
Please see, as I mentioned in other posts about the Sushupti (State), is there  
any hunger, thirst, life, Body, others, world, are you there? where are these  
questions about the effort and effortlessness, activity and inactivity!   
Salutations to Sri Ramana

Quote  
How to watch the sense 'I am'  
Dear Snow,   
Sence of "I am" is what watches so called "you" all the time. Try to get rid  
of it and you will not succeed. When you are defeated in such a way, you'll  
see how to watch it.

## Re:[20] How to watch the sense 'I am'  
Author: matthias            Date: January 12, 2010, 09:52:26 PM  
---  
dear rideforever you said   
" Please help me understand. You say do not try. .. so you mean do nothing ?  
Or are you saying do something subtle ?"**   
try as you like, it is ok to meditate, to make effort..but know that all  
effort is contraproductive as a mental concentration activity..   
what we look for is eternal, everpresent concioussness...and it is simply the  
arising of htis moment..not a big thing..just this   
now tell me Who creates thsi moment...if you found a personality who makes  
this moment   
then tell me next who sustains this moment?   
if you can find someone then show me a person who transcends this moment...   
oyu will never find anything apart from this moment...no sustainer no creator  
no destroyer   
it simply is...and no one is there to make this...yo effor tis senseless...but  
still we need to make effort daily   
its a paradox but a very gentle and loving paradox..so make effort, hard  
effort and then more and more subtle but know deeply understand deeply that it  
is for nothing because there is no one to achive enlightment, enlightment is  
allready (primordially) the nature of htis moment...it is self arising,  
spontanious samadhi   
you cannot reach it, you cannot miss it, you can not grasp it hold it or  
whatever...so best thing is to relax...

Quote from: matthias on January 12, 2010, 09:52:26 PM  
what we look for. ..   
so best thing is to relax...   
If you are looking or if you are relaxing, you are doing something.   
"Is there any meaning in wanting to be a jnani ?", or does enlightenment just  
happen ?   
"Is it possible to make an effort to be a jnani ?"   
"Why did Sri Ramana write a book about jnana ? reading a book is gaining a  
vasana"   
Yes, I think, wanting to be a jnana might have some value. I am not saying  
definitely, I am saying there is a possibility that it would help to want to  
be a jnana.   
The instruction "hold onto the I-feeling". This is a vasana. Can it help you  
? Perhaps.   
Perhaps if you have a small amount of wanting, a small amount of doing, it can  
take you 95% on the path, and then you give that up and you are pulled from  
the other side 5%.   
If you think that any effort is against jnana, then stop being a jnana. Stop  
relaxing. Stop looking. Forget it.

## Re:[22] How to watch the sense 'I am'  
Author: Subramanian.R       Date: January 13, 2010, 05:45:58 AM  
---  
Bhagavan Ramana has said the following on the various points   
mentioned: 1. Desiring the Self is the only desire that one can have. If   
desire is meant as vasana, this is the only vasana that one can   
have.   
2. Bhagavan Ramana did write books, did have some thoughts,   
why only thoughts, He did have dreams too. He did drinking   
and sleeping. He has said that this is done by the Pure Mind   
or Suddha Manas, or Sattva Manas, which does not produce   
any prarabdha effect. It is from the Pure Mind, which is like   
the burnt rope. The burnt rope has only a form but of little   
use for any activity i.e. activity that we normally mean.   
He has also said that the Self does everything that a self realized   
jnani does. It is an advaitic paradox. Sri Sankara did all the work,   
including pilgrimages (which Bhagavan Ramana did not do) with   
this Pure Mind or the Self. It is said in Tamil - Ninaiyamal ninainthu...  
thinking without thinking, sollaamal solli. .. telling   
without telling.... kaanaamal kandu....seeing without seeing.   
It is like doing acitivity in a dream. He has said this to Maurice   
Frydman in one of His conversations.   
Arunachala Siva.
 ---

and then you ask "find out who says this"... thats one more thought added to  
the list of thoughts !  
It did not arise automatically, it arose, because you were interested to see  
what the response for your question. You login here here because of some  
motive to feed your thought. More over don't all members who login here, will  
first check their own posts and then the other posts? You - 'I' \- Thoughts  
are here to feed the thoughts - Ego - Mind - I

## Re:[16]TAT TVAM ASI  How to watch the sense 'I am'  
Author: srkudai             Date: January 12, 2010, 02:32:38 PM  
---  
1\. The moment one does something if its lost. .. than Ramana was doing so  
many things! what do u intend to say?   
2.what kind of self inquiry are you talking about Nagaraj?   
When a thought came. ..   
and you remembered that you have to question to whom it has come...   
the original thought is already over. the thought now is this remembrance.   
while the illusion is created as if you are killing the previous thought!!   
and if u did not remember, you cannot ask the question either.   
so u sit for just be. .. and the thought arose. .. it did not ask u permission  
to arise. it just arose.... and nothing can be done about it! u try it  
tomorrow. just sit. thought arises. when you remembered your self inquiry and  
tried to use it to "resolve that thought". .. this remembrance is slow. by  
that time the thought has already passed away.   
infact the reason u r saying this always but not doing it is. .. u r not able  
to do it. .. coz its impractical!   
Love!   
Silence

## Re:[17] How to watch the sense 'I am'  
Author: Nagaraj             Date: January 12, 2010, 04:24:58 PM  
---  
Dear I,   
Quote from: silentgreen on January 12, 2010, 01:13:29 PM  
Is eating and drinking also part of effort and one requires to refrain from  
them to "Just Be"?   
What do you say?   
I am trying to understand whether it can be classified as a thoughtful or  
thoughtless activity.  
Why do you - 'I' want to know, whether eating and drinking also is part of  
effort and whether one has to refrain from them to "Just Be" \- please see,  
this very need is taking you - 'I' away from Just Being. This is what you -  
'I' \- Mind - Thought is doing. Questioning!   
Just for purposes of clarity, in a thoughtless (state) what matters to you -  
'I' ? why speculate about it now Thinking about it? what ever you think about  
it now, is going to be false as it falls in the realms of thoughts only!   
A honest answer thought can give is - "you - thought - 'I' will know answer  
for your question only in thought-less (state) {in reality you will never know  
for you - thoughts will never be there to know this answer}   
Ideally, Ramana Mahashi would say, first get to the thoughtless (state) and  
then ask this question.   
You - 'I' (as in - Thoughts) can never know Manonasham (state) what ever you  
know is just thought alone! Please see, it is you - 'I' \- Mind - thought that  
is just hungry for thinking - Thoughts, Mind just want to procreate for  
continuity for eternity.   
Please see, as I mentioned in other posts about the Sushupti (State), is there  
any hunger, thirst, life, Body, others, world, are you there? where are these  
questions about the effort and effortlessness, activity and inactivity!   
Salutations to Sri Ramana

## Re:[19] How to watch the sense 'I am'  
Author: Vladimir            Date: January 12, 2010, 08:19:10 PM  
---  
Quote  
How to watch the sense 'I am'  
Dear Snow,   
Sence of "I am" is what watches so called "you" all the time. Try to get rid  
of it and you will not succeed. When you are defeated in such a way, you'll  
see how to watch it.

## Re:[20] How to watch the sense 'I am'  
Author: matthias            Date: January 12, 2010, 09:52:26 PM  
---  
dear rideforever you said   
" Please help me understand. You say do not try. .. so you mean do nothing ?  
Or are you saying do something subtle ?"**   
try as you like, it is ok to meditate, to make effort..but know that all  
effort is contraproductive as a mental concentration activity..   
what we look for is eternal, everpresent concioussness...and it is simply the  
arising of htis moment..not a big thing..just this   
now tell me Who creates thsi moment...if you found a personality who makes  
this moment   
then tell me next who sustains this moment?   
if you can find someone then show me a person who transcends this moment...   
oyu will never find anything apart from this moment...no sustainer no creator  
no destroyer   
it simply is...and no one is there to make this...yo effor tis senseless...but  
still we need to make effort daily   
its a paradox but a very gentle and loving paradox..so make effort, hard  
effort and then more and more subtle but know deeply understand deeply that it  
is for nothing because there is no one to achive enlightment, enlightment is  
allready (primordially) the nature of htis moment...it is self arising,  
spontanious samadhi   
you cannot reach it, you cannot miss it, you can not grasp it hold it or  
whatever...so best thing is to relax...

## Re:[21] How to watch the sense 'I am'  
Author: rideforever         Date: January 12, 2010, 10:04:48 PM  
---  
Quote from: matthias on January 12, 2010, 09:52:26 PM  
what we look for. ..   
so best thing is to relax...   
If you are looking or if you are relaxing, you are doing something.   
"Is there any meaning in wanting to be a jnani ?", or does enlightenment just  
happen ?   
"Is it possible to make an effort to be a jnani ?"   
"Why did Sri Ramana write a book about jnana ? reading a book is gaining a  
vasana"   
Yes, I think, wanting to be a jnana might have some value. I am not saying  
definitely, I am saying there is a possibility that it would help to want to  
be a jnana.   
The instruction "hold onto the I-feeling". This is a vasana. Can it help you  
? Perhaps.   
Perhaps if you have a small amount of wanting, a small amount of doing, it can  
take you 95% on the path, and then you give that up and you are pulled from  
the other side 5%.   
If you think that any effort is against jnana, then stop being a jnana. Stop  
relaxing. Stop looking. Forget it.
 ---

## Re:[22] How to watch the sense 'I am'  
Author: Subramanian.R       Date: January 13, 2010, 05:45:58 AM  
---  
Bhagavan Ramana has said the following on the various points   
mentioned: 1. Desiring the Self is the only desire that one can have. If   
desire is meant as vasana, this is the only vasana that one can   
have.   
2. Bhagavan Ramana did write books, did have some thoughts,   
why only thoughts, He did have dreams too. He did drinking   
and sleeping. He has said that this is done by the Pure Mind   
or Suddha Manas, or Sattva Manas, which does not produce   
any prarabdha effect. It is from the Pure Mind, which is like   
the burnt rope. The burnt rope has only a form but of little   
use for any activity i.e. activity that we normally mean.   
He has also said that the Self does everything that a self realized   
jnani does. It is an advaitic paradox. Sri Sankara did all the work,   
including pilgrimages (which Bhagavan Ramana did not do) with   
this Pure Mind or the Self. It is said in Tamil - Ninaiyamal ninainthu...  
thinking without thinking, sollaamal solli. .. telling   
without telling.... kaanaamal kandu....seeing without seeing.   
It is like doing acitivity in a dream. He has said this to Maurice   
Frydman in one of His conversations.   
Arunachala Siva.
 ---  
Source:[http://web.archive.org/web/20100707045052/http://www.arunachala-ramana.org/forum/index.php?topic=4337.msg11098](http://web.archive.org/web/20100707045052/http://www.arunachala-ramana.org/forum/index.php?topic=4337.msg11098)   
---

questions about the effort and effortlessness, activity and inactivity!

How to watch the sense 'I am'  
Dear Snow,   
Sence of "I am" is what watches so called "you" all the time. Try to get rid  
of it and you will not succeed. When you are defeated in such a way, you'll  
see how to watch it.

## Re:[20] How to watch the sense 'I am'  
Author: matthias            Date: January 12, 2010, 09:52:26 PM  
---  
dear rideforever you said   
" Please help me understand. You say do not try. .. so you mean do nothing ?  
Or are you saying do something subtle ?"**   
try as you like, it is ok to meditate, to make effort..but know that all  
effort is contraproductive as a mental concentration activity..   
what we look for is eternal, everpresent concioussness...and it is simply the  
arising of htis moment..not a big thing..just this   
now tell me Who creates thsi moment...if you found a personality who makes  
this moment   
then tell me next who sustains this moment?   
if you can find someone then show me a person who transcends this moment...   
oyu will never find anything apart from this moment...no sustainer no creator  
no destroyer   
it simply is...and no one is there to make this...yo effor tis senseless...but  
still we need to make effort daily   
its a paradox but a very gentle and loving paradox..so make effort, hard  
effort and then more and more subtle but know deeply understand deeply that it  
is for nothing because there is no one to achive enlightment, enlightment is  
allready (primordially) the nature of htis moment...it is self arising,  
spontanious samadhi   
you cannot reach it, you cannot miss it, you can not grasp it hold it or  
whatever...so best thing is to relax...
 ---

## Re:[21] How to watch the sense 'I am'  
Author: rideforever         Date: January 12, 2010, 10:04:48 PM  
---  
Quote from: matthias on January 12, 2010, 09:52:26 PM  
what we look for. ..   
so best thing is to relax...   
If you are looking or if you are relaxing, you are doing something.   
"Is there any meaning in wanting to be a jnani ?", or does enlightenment just  
happen ?   
"Is it possible to make an effort to be a jnani ?"   
"Why did Sri Ramana write a book about jnana ? reading a book is gaining a  
vasana"   
Yes, I think, wanting to be a jnana might have some value. I am not saying  
definitely, I am saying there is a possibility that it would help to want to  
be a jnana.   
The instruction "hold onto the I-feeling". This is a vasana. Can it help you  
? Perhaps.   
Perhaps if you have a small amount of wanting, a small amount of doing, it can  
take you 95% on the path, and then you give that up and you are pulled from  
the other side 5%.   
If you think that any effort is against jnana, then stop being a jnana. Stop  
relaxing. Stop looking. Forget it.
 ---  
Source:[http://web.archive.org/web/20100707045031/http://www.arunachala-ramana.org/forum/index.php?topic=4337.msg11101](http://web.archive.org/web/20100707045031/http://www.arunachala-ramana.org/forum/index.php?topic=4337.msg11101)

## Re:[22] How to watch the sense 'I am'  
Author: Subramanian.R       Date: January 13, 2010, 05:45:58 AM  
---  
Bhagavan Ramana has said the following on the various points   
mentioned: 1. Desiring the Self is the only desire that one can have. If   
desire is meant as vasana, this is the only vasana that one can   
have.   
2. Bhagavan Ramana did write books, did have some thoughts,   
why only thoughts, He did have dreams too. He did drinking   
and sleeping. He has said that this is done by the Pure Mind   
or Suddha Manas, or Sattva Manas, which does not produce   
any prarabdha effect. It is from the Pure Mind, which is like   
the burnt rope. The burnt rope has only a form but of little   
use for any activity i.e. activity that we normally mean.   
He has also said that the Self does everything that a self realized   
jnani does. It is an advaitic paradox. Sri Sankara did all the work,   
including pilgrimages (which Bhagavan Ramana did not do) with   
this Pure Mind or the Self. It is said in Tamil - Ninaiyamal ninainthu...  
thinking without thinking, sollaamal solli. .. telling   
without telling.... kaanaamal kandu....seeing without seeing.   
It is like doing acitivity in a dream. He has said this to Maurice   
Frydman in one of His conversations.   
Arunachala Siva.
 ---  
Source:[http://web.archive.org/web/20100707045031/http://www.arunachala-ramana.org/forum/index.php?topic=4337.msg11101](http://web.archive.org/web/20100707045031/http://www.arunachala-ramana.org/forum/index.php?topic=4337.msg11101)   
---

## Re:[16]TAT TVAM ASI  How to watch the sense 'I am'

1\. The moment one does something if its lost. .. than Ramana was doing so  
many things! what do u intend to say?   
2.what kind of self inquiry are you talking about Nagaraj?   
When a thought came. ..   
and you remembered that you have to question to whom it has come...   
the original thought is already over. the thought now is this remembrance.   
while the illusion is created as if you are killing the previous thought!!   
and if u did not remember, you cannot ask the question either.   
so u sit for just be. .. and the thought arose. .. it did not ask u permission  
to arise. it just arose.... and nothing can be done about it! u try it  
tomorrow. just sit. thought arises. when you remembered your self inquiry and  
tried to use it to "resolve that thought". .. this remembrance is slow. by  
that time the thought has already passed away.   
infact the reason u r saying this always but not doing it is. .. u r not able  
to do it. .. coz its impractical!

Dear I,

Is eating and drinking also part of effort and one requires to refrain from

I am trying to understand whether it can be classified as a thoughtful or  
thoughtless activity.  
Why do you - 'I' want to know, whether eating and drinking also is part of  
effort and whether one has to refrain from them to "Just Be" \- please see,  
this very need is taking you - 'I' away from Just Being. This is what you -  
'I' \- Mind - Thought is doing. Questioning!   
Just for purposes of clarity, in a thoughtless (state) what matters to you -  
'I' ? why speculate about it now Thinking about it? what ever you think about  
it now, is going to be false as it falls in the realms of thoughts only!   
A honest answer thought can give is - "you - thought - 'I' will know answer  
for your question only in thought-less (state) {in reality you will never know  
for you - thoughts will never be there to know this answer}   
Ideally, Ramana Mahashi would say, first get to the thoughtless (state) and  
then ask this question.   
You - 'I' (as in - Thoughts) can never know Manonasham (state) what ever you  
know is just thought alone! Please see, it is you - 'I' \- Mind - thought that  
is just hungry for thinking - Thoughts, Mind just want to procreate for  
continuity for eternity.   
Please see, as I mentioned in other posts about the Sushupti (State), is there  
any hunger, thirst, life, Body, others, world, are you there? where are these  
questions about the effort and effortlessness, activity and inactivity!

## Re:[21] How to watch the sense 'I am'  
Author: rideforever         Date: January 12, 2010, 10:04:48 PM  
---  
Quote from: matthias on January 12, 2010, 09:52:26 PM  
what we look for. ..   
so best thing is to relax...   
If you are looking or if you are relaxing, you are doing something.   
"Is there any meaning in wanting to be a jnani ?", or does enlightenment just  
happen ?   
"Is it possible to make an effort to be a jnani ?"   
"Why did Sri Ramana write a book about jnana ? reading a book is gaining a  
vasana"   
Yes, I think, wanting to be a jnana might have some value. I am not saying  
definitely, I am saying there is a possibility that it would help to want to  
be a jnana.   
The instruction "hold onto the I-feeling". This is a vasana. Can it help you  
? Perhaps.   
Perhaps if you have a small amount of wanting, a small amount of doing, it can  
take you 95% on the path, and then you give that up and you are pulled from  
the other side 5%.   
If you think that any effort is against jnana, then stop being a jnana. Stop  
relaxing. Stop looking. Forget it.

## Re:[22] How to watch the sense 'I am'  
Author: Subramanian.R       Date: January 13, 2010, 05:45:58 AM  
---  
Bhagavan Ramana has said the following on the various points   
mentioned: 1. Desiring the Self is the only desire that one can have. If   
desire is meant as vasana, this is the only vasana that one can   
have.   
2. Bhagavan Ramana did write books, did have some thoughts,   
why only thoughts, He did have dreams too. He did drinking   
and sleeping. He has said that this is done by the Pure Mind   
or Suddha Manas, or Sattva Manas, which does not produce   
any prarabdha effect. It is from the Pure Mind, which is like   
the burnt rope. The burnt rope has only a form but of little   
use for any activity i.e. activity that we normally mean.   
He has also said that the Self does everything that a self realized   
jnani does. It is an advaitic paradox. Sri Sankara did all the work,   
including pilgrimages (which Bhagavan Ramana did not do) with   
this Pure Mind or the Self. It is said in Tamil - Ninaiyamal ninainthu...  
thinking without thinking, sollaamal solli. .. telling   
without telling.... kaanaamal kandu....seeing without seeing.   
It is like doing acitivity in a dream. He has said this to Maurice   
Frydman in one of His conversations.   
Arunachala Siva.
 ---  
Source:[http://web.archive.org/web/20100707045010/http://www.arunachala-ramana.org/forum/index.php?topic=4337.msg11102](http://web.archive.org/web/20100707045010/http://www.arunachala-ramana.org/forum/index.php?topic=4337.msg11102)   
---

## Re:[16]TAT TVAM ASI  How to watch the sense 'I am'  
Author: srkudai             Date: January 12, 2010, 02:32:38 PM

1\. The moment one does something if its lost. .. than Ramana was doing so  
many things! what do u intend to say?   
2.what kind of self inquiry are you talking about Nagaraj?   
When a thought came. ..   
and you remembered that you have to question to whom it has come...   
the original thought is already over. the thought now is this remembrance.   
while the illusion is created as if you are killing the previous thought!!   
and if u did not remember, you cannot ask the question either.   
so u sit for just be. .. and the thought arose. .. it did not ask u permission  
to arise. it just arose.... and nothing can be done about it! u try it  
tomorrow. just sit. thought arises. when you remembered your self inquiry and  
tried to use it to "resolve that thought". .. this remembrance is slow. by  
that time the thought has already passed away.   
infact the reason u r saying this always but not doing it is. .. u r not able  
to do it. .. coz its impractical!   
Love!

## Re:[17] How to watch the sense 'I am'

Dear I,   
Quote from: silentgreen on January 12, 2010, 01:13:29 PM  
Is eating and drinking also part of effort and one requires to refrain from  
them to "Just Be"?   
What do you say?   
I am trying to understand whether it can be classified as a thoughtful or  
thoughtless activity.  
Why do you - 'I' want to know, whether eating and drinking also is part of  
effort and whether one has to refrain from them to "Just Be" \- please see,  
this very need is taking you - 'I' away from Just Being. This is what you -  
'I' \- Mind - Thought is doing. Questioning!   
Just for purposes of clarity, in a thoughtless (state) what matters to you -  
'I' ? why speculate about it now Thinking about it? what ever you think about  
it now, is going to be false as it falls in the realms of thoughts only!   
A honest answer thought can give is - "you - thought - 'I' will know answer  
for your question only in thought-less (state) {in reality you will never know  
for you - thoughts will never be there to know this answer}   
Ideally, Ramana Mahashi would say, first get to the thoughtless (state) and  
then ask this question.   
You - 'I' (as in - Thoughts) can never know Manonasham (state) what ever you  
know is just thought alone! Please see, it is you - 'I' \- Mind - thought that  
is just hungry for thinking - Thoughts, Mind just want to procreate for  
continuity for eternity.   
Please see, as I mentioned in other posts about the Sushupti (State), is there  
any hunger, thirst, life, Body, others, world, are you there? where are these  
questions about the effort and effortlessness, activity and inactivity!   
Salutations to Sri Ramana

Quote  
How to watch the sense 'I am'  
Dear Snow,   
Sence of "I am" is what watches so called "you" all the time. Try to get rid  
of it and you will not succeed. When you are defeated in such a way, you'll  
see how to watch it.

## Re:[20] How to watch the sense 'I am'  
Author: matthias            Date: January 12, 2010, 09:52:26 PM  
---  
dear rideforever you said   
" Please help me understand. You say do not try. .. so you mean do nothing ?  
Or are you saying do something subtle ?"**   
try as you like, it is ok to meditate, to make effort..but know that all  
effort is contraproductive as a mental concentration activity..   
what we look for is eternal, everpresent concioussness...and it is simply the  
arising of htis moment..not a big thing..just this   
now tell me Who creates thsi moment...if you found a personality who makes  
this moment   
then tell me next who sustains this moment?   
if you can find someone then show me a person who transcends this moment...   
oyu will never find anything apart from this moment...no sustainer no creator  
no destroyer   
it simply is...and no one is there to make this...yo effor tis senseless...but  
still we need to make effort daily   
its a paradox but a very gentle and loving paradox..so make effort, hard  
effort and then more and more subtle but know deeply understand deeply that it  
is for nothing because there is no one to achive enlightment, enlightment is  
allready (primordially) the nature of htis moment...it is self arising,  
spontanious samadhi   
you cannot reach it, you cannot miss it, you can not grasp it hold it or  
whatever...so best thing is to relax...

## Re:[21] How to watch the sense 'I am'  
Author: rideforever         Date: January 12, 2010, 10:04:48 PM  
---  
Quote from: matthias on January 12, 2010, 09:52:26 PM  
what we look for. ..   
so best thing is to relax...   
If you are looking or if you are relaxing, you are doing something.   
"Is there any meaning in wanting to be a jnani ?", or does enlightenment just  
happen ?   
"Is it possible to make an effort to be a jnani ?"   
"Why did Sri Ramana write a book about jnana ? reading a book is gaining a  
vasana"   
Yes, I think, wanting to be a jnana might have some value. I am not saying  
definitely, I am saying there is a possibility that it would help to want to  
be a jnana.   
The instruction "hold onto the I-feeling". This is a vasana. Can it help you  
? Perhaps.   
Perhaps if you have a small amount of wanting, a small amount of doing, it can  
take you 95% on the path, and then you give that up and you are pulled from  
the other side 5%.   
If you think that any effort is against jnana, then stop being a jnana. Stop  
relaxing. Stop looking. Forget it.
 ---

## Re:[22] How to watch the sense 'I am'  
Author: Subramanian.R       Date: January 13, 2010, 05:45:58 AM  
---  
Bhagavan Ramana has said the following on the various points   
mentioned: 1. Desiring the Self is the only desire that one can have. If   
desire is meant as vasana, this is the only vasana that one can   
have.   
2. Bhagavan Ramana did write books, did have some thoughts,   
why only thoughts, He did have dreams too. He did drinking   
and sleeping. He has said that this is done by the Pure Mind   
or Suddha Manas, or Sattva Manas, which does not produce   
any prarabdha effect. It is from the Pure Mind, which is like   
the burnt rope. The burnt rope has only a form but of little   
use for any activity i.e. activity that we normally mean.   
He has also said that the Self does everything that a self realized   
jnani does. It is an advaitic paradox. Sri Sankara did all the work,   
including pilgrimages (which Bhagavan Ramana did not do) with   
this Pure Mind or the Self. It is said in Tamil - Ninaiyamal ninainthu...  
thinking without thinking, sollaamal solli. .. telling   
without telling.... kaanaamal kandu....seeing without seeing.   
It is like doing acitivity in a dream. He has said this to Maurice   
Frydman in one of His conversations.   
Arunachala Siva.
 ---

## Re:[16]TAT TVAM ASI  How to watch the sense 'I am'  
Author: srkudai             Date: January 12, 2010, 02:32:38 PM  
---  
1\. The moment one does something if its lost. .. than Ramana was doing so  
many things! what do u intend to say?   
2.what kind of self inquiry are you talking about Nagaraj?   
When a thought came. ..   
and you remembered that you have to question to whom it has come...   
the original thought is already over. the thought now is this remembrance.   
while the illusion is created as if you are killing the previous thought!!   
and if u did not remember, you cannot ask the question either.   
so u sit for just be. .. and the thought arose. .. it did not ask u permission  
to arise. it just arose.... and nothing can be done about it! u try it  
tomorrow. just sit. thought arises. when you remembered your self inquiry and  
tried to use it to "resolve that thought". .. this remembrance is slow. by  
that time the thought has already passed away.   
infact the reason u r saying this always but not doing it is. .. u r not able  
to do it. .. coz its impractical!   
Love!   
Silence

## Re:[17] How to watch the sense 'I am'  
Author: Nagaraj             Date: January 12, 2010, 04:24:58 PM  
---  
Dear I,   
Quote from: silentgreen on January 12, 2010, 01:13:29 PM  
Is eating and drinking also part of effort and one requires to refrain from  
them to "Just Be"?   
What do you say?   
I am trying to understand whether it can be classified as a thoughtful or  
thoughtless activity.  
Why do you - 'I' want to know, whether eating and drinking also is part of  
effort and whether one has to refrain from them to "Just Be" \- please see,  
this very need is taking you - 'I' away from Just Being. This is what you -  
'I' \- Mind - Thought is doing. Questioning!   
Just for purposes of clarity, in a thoughtless (state) what matters to you -  
'I' ? why speculate about it now Thinking about it? what ever you think about  
it now, is going to be false as it falls in the realms of thoughts only!   
A honest answer thought can give is - "you - thought - 'I' will know answer  
for your question only in thought-less (state) {in reality you will never know  
for you - thoughts will never be there to know this answer}   
Ideally, Ramana Mahashi would say, first get to the thoughtless (state) and  
then ask this question.   
You - 'I' (as in - Thoughts) can never know Manonasham (state) what ever you  
know is just thought alone! Please see, it is you - 'I' \- Mind - thought that  
is just hungry for thinking - Thoughts, Mind just want to procreate for  
continuity for eternity.   
Please see, as I mentioned in other posts about the Sushupti (State), is there  
any hunger, thirst, life, Body, others, world, are you there? where are these  
questions about the effort and effortlessness, activity and inactivity!   
Salutations to Sri Ramana

## Re:[19] How to watch the sense 'I am'  
Author: Vladimir            Date: January 12, 2010, 08:19:10 PM  
---  
Quote  
How to watch the sense 'I am'  
Dear Snow,   
Sence of "I am" is what watches so called "you" all the time. Try to get rid  
of it and you will not succeed. When you are defeated in such a way, you'll  
see how to watch it.

## Re:[20] How to watch the sense 'I am'  
Author: matthias            Date: January 12, 2010, 09:52:26 PM  
---  
dear rideforever you said   
" Please help me understand. You say do not try. .. so you mean do nothing ?  
Or are you saying do something subtle ?"**   
try as you like, it is ok to meditate, to make effort..but know that all  
effort is contraproductive as a mental concentration activity..   
what we look for is eternal, everpresent concioussness...and it is simply the  
arising of htis moment..not a big thing..just this   
now tell me Who creates thsi moment...if you found a personality who makes  
this moment   
then tell me next who sustains this moment?   
if you can find someone then show me a person who transcends this moment...   
oyu will never find anything apart from this moment...no sustainer no creator  
no destroyer   
it simply is...and no one is there to make this...yo effor tis senseless...but  
still we need to make effort daily   
its a paradox but a very gentle and loving paradox..so make effort, hard  
effort and then more and more subtle but know deeply understand deeply that it  
is for nothing because there is no one to achive enlightment, enlightment is  
allready (primordially) the nature of htis moment...it is self arising,  
spontanious samadhi   
you cannot reach it, you cannot miss it, you can not grasp it hold it or  
whatever...so best thing is to relax...

## Re:[21] How to watch the sense 'I am'  
Author: rideforever         Date: January 12, 2010, 10:04:48 PM  
---  
Quote from: matthias on January 12, 2010, 09:52:26 PM  
what we look for. ..   
so best thing is to relax...   
If you are looking or if you are relaxing, you are doing something.   
"Is there any meaning in wanting to be a jnani ?", or does enlightenment just  
happen ?   
"Is it possible to make an effort to be a jnani ?"   
"Why did Sri Ramana write a book about jnana ? reading a book is gaining a  
vasana"   
Yes, I think, wanting to be a jnana might have some value. I am not saying  
definitely, I am saying there is a possibility that it would help to want to  
be a jnana.   
The instruction "hold onto the I-feeling". This is a vasana. Can it help you  
? Perhaps.   
Perhaps if you have a small amount of wanting, a small amount of doing, it can  
take you 95% on the path, and then you give that up and you are pulled from  
the other side 5%.   
If you think that any effort is against jnana, then stop being a jnana. Stop  
relaxing. Stop looking. Forget it.
 ---

## Re:[22] How to watch the sense 'I am'  
Author: Subramanian.R       Date: January 13, 2010, 05:45:58 AM  
---  
Bhagavan Ramana has said the following on the various points   
mentioned: 1. Desiring the Self is the only desire that one can have. If   
desire is meant as vasana, this is the only vasana that one can   
have.   
2. Bhagavan Ramana did write books, did have some thoughts,   
why only thoughts, He did have dreams too. He did drinking   
and sleeping. He has said that this is done by the Pure Mind   
or Suddha Manas, or Sattva Manas, which does not produce   
any prarabdha effect. It is from the Pure Mind, which is like   
the burnt rope. The burnt rope has only a form but of little   
use for any activity i.e. activity that we normally mean.   
He has also said that the Self does everything that a self realized   
jnani does. It is an advaitic paradox. Sri Sankara did all the work,   
including pilgrimages (which Bhagavan Ramana did not do) with   
this Pure Mind or the Self. It is said in Tamil - Ninaiyamal ninainthu...  
thinking without thinking, sollaamal solli. .. telling   
without telling.... kaanaamal kandu....seeing without seeing.   
It is like doing acitivity in a dream. He has said this to Maurice   
Frydman in one of His conversations.   
Arunachala Siva.
 ---  
Source:[http://web.archive.org/web/20100707045205/http://www.arunachala-ramana.org/forum/index.php?topic=4337.msg11112](http://web.archive.org/web/20100707045205/http://www.arunachala-ramana.org/forum/index.php?topic=4337.msg11112)   
---

How to watch the sense 'I am'  
Dear Snow,   
Sence of "I am" is what watches so called "you" all the time. Try to get rid  
of it and you will not succeed. When you are defeated in such a way, you'll  
see how to watch it.

## Re:[20] How to watch the sense 'I am'

---  
dear rideforever you said   
" Please help me understand. You say do not try. .. so you mean do nothing ?  
Or are you saying do something subtle ?"**   
try as you like, it is ok to meditate, to make effort..but know that all  
effort is contraproductive as a mental concentration activity..   
what we look for is eternal, everpresent concioussness...and it is simply the  
arising of htis moment..not a big thing..just this   
now tell me Who creates thsi moment...if you found a personality who makes  
this moment   
then tell me next who sustains this moment?   
if you can find someone then show me a person who transcends this moment...   
oyu will never find anything apart from this moment...no sustainer no creator  
no destroyer   
it simply is...and no one is there to make this...yo effor tis senseless...but  
still we need to make effort daily   
its a paradox but a very gentle and loving paradox..so make effort, hard  
effort and then more and more subtle but know deeply understand deeply that it  
is for nothing because there is no one to achive enlightment, enlightment is  
allready (primordially) the nature of htis moment...it is self arising,  
spontanious samadhi   
you cannot reach it, you cannot miss it, you can not grasp it hold it or  
whatever...so best thing is to relax...

## Re:[21] How to watch the sense 'I am'  
Author: rideforever         Date: January 12, 2010, 10:04:48 PM  
---  
Quote from: matthias on January 12, 2010, 09:52:26 PM  
what we look for. ..   
so best thing is to relax...   
If you are looking or if you are relaxing, you are doing something.   
"Is there any meaning in wanting to be a jnani ?", or does enlightenment just  
happen ?   
"Is it possible to make an effort to be a jnani ?"   
"Why did Sri Ramana write a book about jnana ? reading a book is gaining a  
vasana"   
Yes, I think, wanting to be a jnana might have some value. I am not saying  
definitely, I am saying there is a possibility that it would help to want to  
be a jnana.   
The instruction "hold onto the I-feeling". This is a vasana. Can it help you  
? Perhaps.   
Perhaps if you have a small amount of wanting, a small amount of doing, it can  
take you 95% on the path, and then you give that up and you are pulled from  
the other side 5%.   
If you think that any effort is against jnana, then stop being a jnana. Stop  
relaxing. Stop looking. Forget it.
 ---  
Source:[http://web.archive.org/web/20100707045432/http://www.arunachala-ramana.org/forum/index.php?topic=4337.msg11124](http://web.archive.org/web/20100707045432/http://www.arunachala-ramana.org/forum/index.php?topic=4337.msg11124)

## Re:[22] How to watch the sense 'I am'  
Author: Subramanian.R       Date: January 13, 2010, 05:45:58 AM  
---  
Bhagavan Ramana has said the following on the various points   
mentioned: 1. Desiring the Self is the only desire that one can have. If   
desire is meant as vasana, this is the only vasana that one can   
have.   
2. Bhagavan Ramana did write books, did have some thoughts,   
why only thoughts, He did have dreams too. He did drinking   
and sleeping. He has said that this is done by the Pure Mind   
or Suddha Manas, or Sattva Manas, which does not produce   
any prarabdha effect. It is from the Pure Mind, which is like   
the burnt rope. The burnt rope has only a form but of little   
use for any activity i.e. activity that we normally mean.   
He has also said that the Self does everything that a self realized   
jnani does. It is an advaitic paradox. Sri Sankara did all the work,   
including pilgrimages (which Bhagavan Ramana did not do) with   
this Pure Mind or the Self. It is said in Tamil - Ninaiyamal ninainthu...  
thinking without thinking, sollaamal solli. .. telling   
without telling.... kaanaamal kandu....seeing without seeing.   
It is like doing acitivity in a dream. He has said this to Maurice   
Frydman in one of His conversations.   
Arunachala Siva.
 ---  
Source:[http://web.archive.org/web/20100707045432/http://www.arunachala-ramana.org/forum/index.php?topic=4337.msg11124](http://web.archive.org/web/20100707045432/http://www.arunachala-ramana.org/forum/index.php?topic=4337.msg11124)   
---

many things! what do u intend to say?   
2.what kind of self inquiry are you talking about Nagaraj?   
When a thought came. ..   
and you remembered that you have to question to whom it has come...   
the original thought is already over. the thought now is this remembrance.   
while the illusion is created as if you are killing the previous thought!!   
and if u did not remember, you cannot ask the question either.   
so u sit for just be. .. and the thought arose. .. it did not ask u permission  
to arise. it just arose.... and nothing can be done about it! u try it  
tomorrow. just sit. thought arises. when you remembered your self inquiry and  
tried to use it to "resolve that thought". .. this remembrance is slow. by  
that time the thought has already passed away.   
infact the reason u r saying this always but not doing it is. .. u r not able  
to do it. .. coz its impractical!

## Re:[17] How to watch the sense 'I am'  
Author: Nagaraj             Date: January 12, 2010, 04:24:58 PM

Dear I,   
Quote from: silentgreen on January 12, 2010, 01:13:29 PM  
Is eating and drinking also part of effort and one requires to refrain from  
them to "Just Be"?   
What do you say?   
I am trying to understand whether it can be classified as a thoughtful or  
thoughtless activity.  
Why do you - 'I' want to know, whether eating and drinking also is part of  
effort and whether one has to refrain from them to "Just Be" \- please see,  
this very need is taking you - 'I' away from Just Being. This is what you -  
'I' \- Mind - Thought is doing. Questioning!   
Just for purposes of clarity, in a thoughtless (state) what matters to you -  
'I' ? why speculate about it now Thinking about it? what ever you think about  
it now, is going to be false as it falls in the realms of thoughts only!   
A honest answer thought can give is - "you - thought - 'I' will know answer  
for your question only in thought-less (state) {in reality you will never know  
for you - thoughts will never be there to know this answer}   
Ideally, Ramana Mahashi would say, first get to the thoughtless (state) and  
then ask this question.   
You - 'I' (as in - Thoughts) can never know Manonasham (state) what ever you  
know is just thought alone! Please see, it is you - 'I' \- Mind - thought that  
is just hungry for thinking - Thoughts, Mind just want to procreate for  
continuity for eternity.   
Please see, as I mentioned in other posts about the Sushupti (State), is there  
any hunger, thirst, life, Body, others, world, are you there? where are these  
questions about the effort and effortlessness, activity and inactivity!   
Salutations to Sri Ramana

Quote from: matthias on January 12, 2010, 09:52:26 PM  
what we look for. ..   
so best thing is to relax...   
If you are looking or if you are relaxing, you are doing something.   
"Is there any meaning in wanting to be a jnani ?", or does enlightenment just  
happen ?   
"Is it possible to make an effort to be a jnani ?"   
"Why did Sri Ramana write a book about jnana ? reading a book is gaining a  
vasana"   
Yes, I think, wanting to be a jnana might have some value. I am not saying  
definitely, I am saying there is a possibility that it would help to want to  
be a jnana.   
The instruction "hold onto the I-feeling". This is a vasana. Can it help you  
? Perhaps.   
Perhaps if you have a small amount of wanting, a small amount of doing, it can  
take you 95% on the path, and then you give that up and you are pulled from  
the other side 5%.   
If you think that any effort is against jnana, then stop being a jnana. Stop  
relaxing. Stop looking. Forget it.

Bhagavan Ramana has said the following on the various points   
mentioned: 1. Desiring the Self is the only desire that one can have. If   
desire is meant as vasana, this is the only vasana that one can   
have.   
2. Bhagavan Ramana did write books, did have some thoughts,   
why only thoughts, He did have dreams too. He did drinking   
and sleeping. He has said that this is done by the Pure Mind   
or Suddha Manas, or Sattva Manas, which does not produce   
any prarabdha effect. It is from the Pure Mind, which is like   
the burnt rope. The burnt rope has only a form but of little   
use for any activity i.e. activity that we normally mean.   
He has also said that the Self does everything that a self realized   
jnani does. It is an advaitic paradox. Sri Sankara did all the work,   
including pilgrimages (which Bhagavan Ramana did not do) with   
this Pure Mind or the Self. It is said in Tamil - Ninaiyamal ninainthu...  
thinking without thinking, sollaamal solli. .. telling   
without telling.... kaanaamal kandu....seeing without seeing.   
It is like doing acitivity in a dream. He has said this to Maurice   
Frydman in one of His conversations.   
Arunachala Siva.
 ---  
Source:[http://web.archive.org/web/20100707045352/http://www.arunachala-ramana.org/forum/index.php?topic=4337.msg11128](http://web.archive.org/web/20100707045352/http://www.arunachala-ramana.org/forum/index.php?topic=4337.msg11128)

## Re:[32] How to watch the sense 'I am'  
Author: Subramanian.R       Date: January 13, 2010, 07:50:48 AM  
---  
Dear srkudai, Nagaraj,   
The sense of "I am" is simply experiencing. For seekers, they have   
to watch the sense of "I am". Thereafter, it is only experiencing   
not describable by thoughts and words and deeds. Bhagavan   
Ramana used to quote Saint Tayumanavar and another old song   
in this context.   
Tayumanavar: It is like a newly married girl, coming out of the nuptial room in   
the early morning. What shall she say about her experience?   
She will not talk or describe to anyone. Even to her mother who   
is waiting anxiously in the morning, she would simply give a small   
smile and rush to take bath! Imagine, a celibate saint poet has   
written this! A celibate Brahma Jnani has quoted this!   
The old song: (Which Devaraja Mudaliar quotes in his book   
"You are my mother and You are my father.": It is like a drunken fellow returning home at night. He does   
not know where his dhoti is, where is towel is, where his bed   
is. He does not want anything. He does not want even food.   
He simply wants to lie in bed with the experience.   
Arunachala Siva.
 ---  
Source:[http://web.archive.org/web/20100707040108/http://www.arunachala-ramana.org/forum/index.php?topic=4337.msg11130](http://web.archive.org/web/20100707040108/http://www.arunachala-ramana.org/forum/index.php?topic=4337.msg11130)   
---  

## Re:[33] How to watch the sense 'I am'  
Author: Nagaraj             Date: January 13, 2010, 05:35:22 PM  
---  
Dear I,   
There is really no sense of experiencing "I am". it is simply being. It  
remains experience so long the Self enquiry continues till the mind/I merges  
where the perfect Self emerges as 'I-I'   
The example quoted by Ramana Maharshi is the first (stage) in what he says: "First the Self sees itself as object, then the Self sees itself as Void, and  
finally it sees itiself as Self, here there is no seeing as seeing is being"   
Therefore,   
Experiencing the sense of "I am" is "First the Self sees itself as object"   
and   
in reality, "I am" is simply being - "and finally it sees itiself as Self,  
here there is no seeing as seeing is being"   
Which is why I have always stressed in my other posts that Bhagawan's answers  
to several questions were tailor made as per the Pakva of the Questioneer.  
Those answers and Dialogues recorded as books should not be taken at face  
value as his answers to our same question. We have seen several instances  
where Bhagawan has responded differently for same questions. But His grace  
shall take care of the devotee all through!   
Salutations to Sri Ramana.

## Re:[38] How to watch the sense 'I am'  
Author: Nagaraj             Date: March 15, 2010, 06:11:00 PM  
---  
Dear I,   
Quote from: Akira on March 15, 2010, 04:14:41 PM  
Quote from: snow on January 07, 2010, 03:06:33 PM  
Nisargadatta Maharaj said that it is very important to watch "I-am-ness" all  
the time.   
How is that possible?   
How can the subject watch the subject itself?  
Bhagavans explanation is given below -   
"First the Self sees itself as object, then the Self sees itself as Void, and  
finally it sees itiself as Self, here there is no seeing as seeing is being"   
The subject is ego, ego first begins watching itself, ego watching ego, and as  
a result of such an enquiry ego ceases to exist and Self shines and when this  
(occurs) the Subject will not be there, the ego will not be there, the very  
need to know that you are the Self has to end.   
Salutations to Sri Ramana

## Re:[41] How to watch the sense 'I am'  
Author: Nagaraj             Date: March 16, 2010, 05:25:56 AM  
---  
Dear I,   
All interpretations and understanding are correct. There is no need for a  
confirmation from 'anothers' expereience, for understanding. For, it is  
ultimately only an acknowledgement for knowledge what one already has, thats  
all. If 'anothers' experience matches with our existing understanding, mind or  
the ego or the little 'I' nods in confirmation and at the same time, if the  
'anothers' experience does not matches with our existing understanding, mind  
or the ego or the little 'I' nods in non confirmation and this leads to  
discussions, etc... anhd the Mind - ego - little 'I' goes on discussing so  
long the so called 'another' confirms to its own existing or preconceived  
knowledge.   
The 'one' that wants knowledge is the ego, the knowledge that is being created  
in the process is also the ego's. The Mind some how wants to be acknowledged  
as a 'Jnani' or it wants to be acknowledged as a super consciousness, or it  
wants to just enjoy, relish having the title of "Self" or acknowledgement for  
having 'Self-Realised'   
So in all these, who is the one that is wanting to get 'realised'? it is the  
ego - mind - little 'I'. Its like, as a stage drama is being enacted, you act  
as 'Ravana' character and forget that you are just the actor, and as a  
character - 'Ravana' tries to realise its Self as 'Rama' \- which eventually  
becomes another character in itself. The ego - mind - little 'I' gets lost in  
the character of 'Ravana' tries so hard to realised its Self as 'Rama' instead  
of just casting away just the character of Ravana and remain as the one who  
performed the character.   
Salutations to Sri Ramana
 ---  
Source:[http://web.archive.org/web/20100707040108/http://www.arunachala-ramana.org/forum/index.php?topic=4337.msg11130](http://web.archive.org/web/20100707040108/http://www.arunachala-ramana.org/forum/index.php?topic=4337.msg11130)

## Re:[42] How to watch the sense 'I am'  
Author: Nagaraj             Date: March 16, 2010, 06:15:28 AM  
---  
Dear I,   
that means, like Krishna says in the Gita, Uddaret Atmanaatmaanam, the Self is  
its own friend and foe, one has to lift Himself from his own higher Self and  
not let itself fall from its own lower Self.   
Mis-interpretaions and mis understandings are biggest grace in themselves,  
they bestow higher grace than 'Knowledge' itself. It is only because of Mis-  
interpretaions and mis understandings that we begin to enquire further.   
More over it is only the Mind that distinguishes between Misunderstanding and  
Understanding.   
Meditation, for is just being aware of ones own ego, till it gets dissolved  
into nothingness or everything ness.   
Meditation is for me, "Chumma Iru", "Just being" Let all move around you, Just  
Be.   
Bhagavan says - "To know and not to think"   
Salutations to Sri Ramana
 ---

## Re:[43] How to watch the sense 'I am'  
Author: Subramanian.R       Date: March 16, 2010, 06:33:11 AM  
---  
The non existent ego coming out of the non existent mind watches the Self.  
But   
in the beginning, it watches only the thoughts. In a thoughtless abandon, it  
watches   
the Self, in the sense it becomes the Self. The last stage, " watching the  
Self and   
being the Self" is through Guru's Grace. Bhagavan Ramana says in Sri  
Arunachala   
Akshara Mana Maalai: Do not show the mirror to this noseless person and makes  
him   
ashamed. Please lift me up and hug me. (AAMM 91)   
Arunachala Siva.
 ---
