## Re:[44]ఓం నమో భగవతే శ్రీ రమణాయ  How to watch the sense 'I am'  
Author: prasanth_ramana_maharshiDate: June 29, 2010, 11:28:40 AM  
---  
Nice discussion.   
Nice points raised by subramanian garu,nagaraj garu and udai garu.   
I agree with subramanian garu regarding Suddha Manas,or Sattva Manas, which  
does not produce any prarabdha effect. Bhagavan Ramana did write books, did  
have some thoughts,why only thoughts, He did have dreams too.   
I agree with udai garu regarding we cannot have control over our thoughts and  
it is not like we desire and hence we have thoughts.   
Only because we cannot have control over our thoughts several techniques like  
breath control,self enquiry.... are mentioned.   
In Bhagavad Gita Ch6 Text35 Lord Krishna says,   
The Blessed Lord said: O mighty-armed son of Kunti, **it is undoubtedly very  
difficult to curb the restless mind, but it is possible by constant practice  
and by detachment.**   
Here detachment means having strong conviction that ' i am not the  
mind,body,senses...' which reminds Adi sankara's Nirvana Satakam poem.   
Once bhagavan said   
If the outlook changes, the troubles of the world will not worry us. Are the  
waves different from the ocean? Why do the waves occur at all? If asked, what  
reply can we give? The troubles in the world also are like that. Waves come  
and go. If it is found out that they are not different from Atma this worry  
will not exist.

## Re:[33] How to watch the sense 'I am'  
Author: Nagaraj             Date: January 13, 2010, 05:35:22 PM  
---  
Dear I,   
There is really no sense of experiencing "I am". it is simply being. It  
remains experience so long the Self enquiry continues till the mind/I merges  
where the perfect Self emerges as 'I-I'   
The example quoted by Ramana Maharshi is the first (stage) in what he says: "First the Self sees itself as object, then the Self sees itself as Void, and  
finally it sees itiself as Self, here there is no seeing as seeing is being"   
Therefore,   
Experiencing the sense of "I am" is "First the Self sees itself as object"   
and   
in reality, "I am" is simply being - "and finally it sees itiself as Self,  
here there is no seeing as seeing is being"   
Which is why I have always stressed in my other posts that Bhagawan's answers  
to several questions were tailor made as per the Pakva of the Questioneer.  
Those answers and Dialogues recorded as books should not be taken at face  
value as his answers to our same question. We have seen several instances  
where Bhagawan has responded differently for same questions. But His grace  
shall take care of the devotee all through!   
Salutations to Sri Ramana.

## Re:[38] How to watch the sense 'I am'  
Author: Nagaraj             Date: March 15, 2010, 06:11:00 PM  
---  
Dear I,   
Quote from: Akira on March 15, 2010, 04:14:41 PM  
Quote from: snow on January 07, 2010, 03:06:33 PM  
Nisargadatta Maharaj said that it is very important to watch "I-am-ness" all  
the time.   
How is that possible?   
How can the subject watch the subject itself?  
Bhagavans explanation is given below -   
"First the Self sees itself as object, then the Self sees itself as Void, and  
finally it sees itiself as Self, here there is no seeing as seeing is being"   
The subject is ego, ego first begins watching itself, ego watching ego, and as  
a result of such an enquiry ego ceases to exist and Self shines and when this  
(occurs) the Subject will not be there, the ego will not be there, the very  
need to know that you are the Self has to end.   
Salutations to Sri Ramana

## Re:[41] How to watch the sense 'I am'  
Author: Nagaraj             Date: March 16, 2010, 05:25:56 AM  
---  
Dear I,   
All interpretations and understanding are correct. There is no need for a  
confirmation from 'anothers' expereience, for understanding. For, it is  
ultimately only an acknowledgement for knowledge what one already has, thats  
all. If 'anothers' experience matches with our existing understanding, mind or  
the ego or the little 'I' nods in confirmation and at the same time, if the  
'anothers' experience does not matches with our existing understanding, mind  
or the ego or the little 'I' nods in non confirmation and this leads to  
discussions, etc... anhd the Mind - ego - little 'I' goes on discussing so  
long the so called 'another' confirms to its own existing or preconceived  
knowledge.   
The 'one' that wants knowledge is the ego, the knowledge that is being created  
in the process is also the ego's. The Mind some how wants to be acknowledged  
as a 'Jnani' or it wants to be acknowledged as a super consciousness, or it  
wants to just enjoy, relish having the title of "Self" or acknowledgement for  
having 'Self-Realised'   
So in all these, who is the one that is wanting to get 'realised'? it is the  
ego - mind - little 'I'. Its like, as a stage drama is being enacted, you act  
as 'Ravana' character and forget that you are just the actor, and as a  
character - 'Ravana' tries to realise its Self as 'Rama' \- which eventually  
becomes another character in itself. The ego - mind - little 'I' gets lost in  
the character of 'Ravana' tries so hard to realised its Self as 'Rama' instead  
of just casting away just the character of Ravana and remain as the one who  
performed the character.   
Salutations to Sri Ramana
 ---  
Source:[http://web.archive.org/web/20100707040401/http://www.arunachala-ramana.org/forum/index.php?topic=4337.msg11132](http://web.archive.org/web/20100707040401/http://www.arunachala-ramana.org/forum/index.php?topic=4337.msg11132)   
---  

## Re:[42] How to watch the sense 'I am'  
Author: Nagaraj             Date: March 16, 2010, 06:15:28 AM  
---  
Dear I,   
that means, like Krishna says in the Gita, Uddaret Atmanaatmaanam, the Self is  
its own friend and foe, one has to lift Himself from his own higher Self and  
not let itself fall from its own lower Self.   
Mis-interpretaions and mis understandings are biggest grace in themselves,  
they bestow higher grace than 'Knowledge' itself. It is only because of Mis-  
interpretaions and mis understandings that we begin to enquire further.   
More over it is only the Mind that distinguishes between Misunderstanding and  
Understanding.   
Meditation, for is just being aware of ones own ego, till it gets dissolved  
into nothingness or everything ness.   
Meditation is for me, "Chumma Iru", "Just being" Let all move around you, Just  
Be.   
Bhagavan says - "To know and not to think"   
Salutations to Sri Ramana
 ---  
Source:[http://web.archive.org/web/20100707040401/http://www.arunachala-ramana.org/forum/index.php?topic=4337.msg11132](http://web.archive.org/web/20100707040401/http://www.arunachala-ramana.org/forum/index.php?topic=4337.msg11132)   
---  

## Re:[43] How to watch the sense 'I am'  
Author: Subramanian.R       Date: March 16, 2010, 06:33:11 AM  
---  
The non existent ego coming out of the non existent mind watches the Self.  
But   
in the beginning, it watches only the thoughts. In a thoughtless abandon, it  
watches   
the Self, in the sense it becomes the Self. The last stage, " watching the  
Self and   
being the Self" is through Guru's Grace. Bhagavan Ramana says in Sri  
Arunachala   
Akshara Mana Maalai: Do not show the mirror to this noseless person and makes  
him   
ashamed. Please lift me up and hug me. (AAMM 91)   
Arunachala Siva.
 ---  
Source:[http://web.archive.org/web/20100707040401/http://www.arunachala-ramana.org/forum/index.php?topic=4337.msg11132](http://web.archive.org/web/20100707040401/http://www.arunachala-ramana.org/forum/index.php?topic=4337.msg11132)

## Re:[44]ఓం నమో భగవతే శ్రీ రమణాయ  How to watch the sense 'I am'  
Author: prasanth_ramana_maharshiDate: June 29, 2010, 11:28:40 AM  
---  
Nice discussion.   
Nice points raised by subramanian garu,nagaraj garu and udai garu.   
I agree with subramanian garu regarding Suddha Manas,or Sattva Manas, which  
does not produce any prarabdha effect. Bhagavan Ramana did write books, did  
have some thoughts,why only thoughts, He did have dreams too.   
I agree with udai garu regarding we cannot have control over our thoughts and  
it is not like we desire and hence we have thoughts.   
Only because we cannot have control over our thoughts several techniques like  
breath control,self enquiry.... are mentioned.   
In Bhagavad Gita Ch6 Text35 Lord Krishna says,   
The Blessed Lord said: O mighty-armed son of Kunti, **it is undoubtedly very  
difficult to curb the restless mind, but it is possible by constant practice  
and by detachment.**   
Here detachment means having strong conviction that ' i am not the  
mind,body,senses...' which reminds Adi sankara's Nirvana Satakam poem.   
Once bhagavan said   
If the outlook changes, the troubles of the world will not worry us. Are the  
waves different from the ocean? Why do the waves occur at all? If asked, what  
reply can we give? The troubles in the world also are like that. Waves come  
and go. If it is found out that they are not different from Atma this worry  
will not exist.
 ---

## Re:[32] How to watch the sense 'I am'  
Author: Subramanian.R       Date: January 13, 2010, 07:50:48 AM  
---  
Dear srkudai, Nagaraj,   
The sense of "I am" is simply experiencing. For seekers, they have   
to watch the sense of "I am". Thereafter, it is only experiencing   
not describable by thoughts and words and deeds. Bhagavan   
Ramana used to quote Saint Tayumanavar and another old song   
in this context.   
Tayumanavar: It is like a newly married girl, coming out of the nuptial room in   
the early morning. What shall she say about her experience?   
She will not talk or describe to anyone. Even to her mother who   
is waiting anxiously in the morning, she would simply give a small   
smile and rush to take bath! Imagine, a celibate saint poet has   
written this! A celibate Brahma Jnani has quoted this!   
The old song: (Which Devaraja Mudaliar quotes in his book   
"You are my mother and You are my father.": It is like a drunken fellow returning home at night. He does   
not know where his dhoti is, where is towel is, where his bed   
is. He does not want anything. He does not want even food.   
He simply wants to lie in bed with the experience.   
Arunachala Siva.
 ---  
Source:[http://web.archive.org/web/20100707040543/http://www.arunachala-ramana.org/forum/index.php?topic=4337.msg11135](http://web.archive.org/web/20100707040543/http://www.arunachala-ramana.org/forum/index.php?topic=4337.msg11135)   
---

Nice discussion.   
Nice points raised by subramanian garu,nagaraj garu and udai garu.   
I agree with subramanian garu regarding Suddha Manas,or Sattva Manas, which  
does not produce any prarabdha effect. Bhagavan Ramana did write books, did

Here detachment means having strong conviction that ' i am not the  
mind,body,senses...' which reminds Adi sankara's Nirvana Satakam poem.   
Once bhagavan said   
If the outlook changes, the troubles of the world will not worry us. Are the  
waves different from the ocean? Why do the waves occur at all? If asked, what  
reply can we give? The troubles in the world also are like that. Waves come  
and go. If it is found out that they are not different from Atma this worry  
will not exist.
 ---

## Re:[32] How to watch the sense 'I am'  
Author: Subramanian.R       Date: January 13, 2010, 07:50:48 AM  
---  
Dear srkudai, Nagaraj,   
The sense of "I am" is simply experiencing. For seekers, they have   
to watch the sense of "I am". Thereafter, it is only experiencing   
not describable by thoughts and words and deeds. Bhagavan   
Ramana used to quote Saint Tayumanavar and another old song   
in this context.   
Tayumanavar: It is like a newly married girl, coming out of the nuptial room in   
the early morning. What shall she say about her experience?   
She will not talk or describe to anyone. Even to her mother who   
is waiting anxiously in the morning, she would simply give a small   
smile and rush to take bath! Imagine, a celibate saint poet has   
written this! A celibate Brahma Jnani has quoted this!   
The old song: (Which Devaraja Mudaliar quotes in his book   
"You are my mother and You are my father.": It is like a drunken fellow returning home at night. He does   
not know where his dhoti is, where is towel is, where his bed   
is. He does not want anything. He does not want even food.   
He simply wants to lie in bed with the experience.   
Arunachala Siva.
 ---  
Source:[http://web.archive.org/web/20100707040343/http://www.arunachala-ramana.org/forum/index.php?topic=4337.msg11156](http://web.archive.org/web/20100707040343/http://www.arunachala-ramana.org/forum/index.php?topic=4337.msg11156)   
---  

## Re:[33] How to watch the sense 'I am'  
Author: Nagaraj             Date: January 13, 2010, 05:35:22 PM  
---  
Dear I,   
There is really no sense of experiencing "I am". it is simply being. It  
remains experience so long the Self enquiry continues till the mind/I merges  
where the perfect Self emerges as 'I-I'   
The example quoted by Ramana Maharshi is the first (stage) in what he says: "First the Self sees itself as object, then the Self sees itself as Void, and  
finally it sees itiself as Self, here there is no seeing as seeing is being"   
Therefore,   
Experiencing the sense of "I am" is "First the Self sees itself as object"   
and   
in reality, "I am" is simply being - "and finally it sees itiself as Self,  
here there is no seeing as seeing is being"   
Which is why I have always stressed in my other posts that Bhagawan's answers  
to several questions were tailor made as per the Pakva of the Questioneer.  
Those answers and Dialogues recorded as books should not be taken at face  
value as his answers to our same question. We have seen several instances  
where Bhagawan has responded differently for same questions. But His grace  
shall take care of the devotee all through!   
Salutations to Sri Ramana.   
« _Last Edit: January 13, 2010, 05:38:10 PM by Nagaraj_

## Re:[38] How to watch the sense 'I am'  
Author: Nagaraj             Date: March 15, 2010, 06:11:00 PM  
---  
Dear I,   
Quote from: Akira on March 15, 2010, 04:14:41 PM  
Quote from: snow on January 07, 2010, 03:06:33 PM  
Nisargadatta Maharaj said that it is very important to watch "I-am-ness" all  
the time.   
How is that possible?   
How can the subject watch the subject itself?  
Bhagavans explanation is given below -   
"First the Self sees itself as object, then the Self sees itself as Void, and  
finally it sees itiself as Self, here there is no seeing as seeing is being"   
The subject is ego, ego first begins watching itself, ego watching ego, and as  
a result of such an enquiry ego ceases to exist and Self shines and when this  
(occurs) the Subject will not be there, the ego will not be there, the very  
need to know that you are the Self has to end.   
Salutations to Sri Ramana
 ---  
Source:[http://web.archive.org/web/20100707040343/http://www.arunachala-ramana.org/forum/index.php?topic=4337.msg11156](http://web.archive.org/web/20100707040343/http://www.arunachala-ramana.org/forum/index.php?topic=4337.msg11156)

## Re:[41] How to watch the sense 'I am'  
Author: Nagaraj             Date: March 16, 2010, 05:25:56 AM  
---  
Dear I,   
All interpretations and understanding are correct. There is no need for a  
confirmation from 'anothers' expereience, for understanding. For, it is  
ultimately only an acknowledgement for knowledge what one already has, thats  
all. If 'anothers' experience matches with our existing understanding, mind or  
the ego or the little 'I' nods in confirmation and at the same time, if the  
'anothers' experience does not matches with our existing understanding, mind  
or the ego or the little 'I' nods in non confirmation and this leads to  
discussions, etc... anhd the Mind - ego - little 'I' goes on discussing so  
long the so called 'another' confirms to its own existing or preconceived  
knowledge.   
The 'one' that wants knowledge is the ego, the knowledge that is being created  
in the process is also the ego's. The Mind some how wants to be acknowledged  
as a 'Jnani' or it wants to be acknowledged as a super consciousness, or it  
wants to just enjoy, relish having the title of "Self" or acknowledgement for  
having 'Self-Realised'   
So in all these, who is the one that is wanting to get 'realised'? it is the  
ego - mind - little 'I'. Its like, as a stage drama is being enacted, you act  
as 'Ravana' character and forget that you are just the actor, and as a  
character - 'Ravana' tries to realise its Self as 'Rama' \- which eventually  
becomes another character in itself. The ego - mind - little 'I' gets lost in  
the character of 'Ravana' tries so hard to realised its Self as 'Rama' instead  
of just casting away just the character of Ravana and remain as the one who  
performed the character.   
Salutations to Sri Ramana
 ---  
Source:[http://web.archive.org/web/20100707040343/http://www.arunachala-ramana.org/forum/index.php?topic=4337.msg11156](http://web.archive.org/web/20100707040343/http://www.arunachala-ramana.org/forum/index.php?topic=4337.msg11156)   
---  

## Re:[42] How to watch the sense 'I am'  
Author: Nagaraj             Date: March 16, 2010, 06:15:28 AM  
---  
Dear I,   
that means, like Krishna says in the Gita, Uddaret Atmanaatmaanam, the Self is  
its own friend and foe, one has to lift Himself from his own higher Self and  
not let itself fall from its own lower Self.   
Mis-interpretaions and mis understandings are biggest grace in themselves,  
they bestow higher grace than 'Knowledge' itself. It is only because of Mis-  
interpretaions and mis understandings that we begin to enquire further.   
More over it is only the Mind that distinguishes between Misunderstanding and  
Understanding.   
Meditation, for is just being aware of ones own ego, till it gets dissolved  
into nothingness or everything ness.   
Meditation is for me, "Chumma Iru", "Just being" Let all move around you, Just  
Be.   
Bhagavan says - "To know and not to think"   
Salutations to Sri Ramana
 ---  
Source:[http://web.archive.org/web/20100707040343/http://www.arunachala-ramana.org/forum/index.php?topic=4337.msg11156](http://web.archive.org/web/20100707040343/http://www.arunachala-ramana.org/forum/index.php?topic=4337.msg11156)

## Re:[43] How to watch the sense 'I am'  
Author: Subramanian.R       Date: March 16, 2010, 06:33:11 AM  
---  
The non existent ego coming out of the non existent mind watches the Self.  
But   
in the beginning, it watches only the thoughts. In a thoughtless abandon, it  
watches   
the Self, in the sense it becomes the Self. The last stage, " watching the  
Self and   
being the Self" is through Guru's Grace. Bhagavan Ramana says in Sri  
Arunachala   
Akshara Mana Maalai: Do not show the mirror to this noseless person and makes  
him   
ashamed. Please lift me up and hug me. (AAMM 91)   
Arunachala Siva.
 ---  
Source:[http://web.archive.org/web/20100707040343/http://www.arunachala-ramana.org/forum/index.php?topic=4337.msg11156](http://web.archive.org/web/20100707040343/http://www.arunachala-ramana.org/forum/index.php?topic=4337.msg11156)   
---  

## Re:[44]ఓం నమో భగవతే శ్రీ రమణాయ  How to watch the sense 'I am'  
Author: prasanth_ramana_maharshiDate: June 29, 2010, 11:28:40 AM  
---  
Nice discussion.   
Nice points raised by subramanian garu,nagaraj garu and udai garu.   
I agree with subramanian garu regarding Suddha Manas,or Sattva Manas, which  
does not produce any prarabdha effect. Bhagavan Ramana did write books, did  
have some thoughts,why only thoughts, He did have dreams too.   
I agree with udai garu regarding we cannot have control over our thoughts and  
it is not like we desire and hence we have thoughts.   
Only because we cannot have control over our thoughts several techniques like  
breath control,self enquiry.... are mentioned.   
In Bhagavad Gita Ch6 Text35 Lord Krishna says,   
The Blessed Lord said: O mighty-armed son of Kunti, **it is undoubtedly very  
difficult to curb the restless mind, but it is possible by constant practice  
and by detachment.**   
Here detachment means having strong conviction that ' i am not the  
mind,body,senses...' which reminds Adi sankara's Nirvana Satakam poem.   
Once bhagavan said   
If the outlook changes, the troubles of the world will not worry us. Are the  
waves different from the ocean? Why do the waves occur at all? If asked, what  
reply can we give? The troubles in the world also are like that. Waves come  
and go. If it is found out that they are not different from Atma this worry  
will not exist.
 ---

## Re:[42] How to watch the sense 'I am'  
Author: Nagaraj             Date: March 16, 2010, 06:15:28 AM  
---  
Dear I,   
that means, like Krishna says in the Gita, Uddaret Atmanaatmaanam, the Self is  
its own friend and foe, one has to lift Himself from his own higher Self and  
not let itself fall from its own lower Self.   
Mis-interpretaions and mis understandings are biggest grace in themselves,  
they bestow higher grace than 'Knowledge' itself. It is only because of Mis-  
interpretaions and mis understandings that we begin to enquire further.   
More over it is only the Mind that distinguishes between Misunderstanding and  
Understanding.   
Meditation, for is just being aware of ones own ego, till it gets dissolved  
into nothingness or everything ness.   
Meditation is for me, "Chumma Iru", "Just being" Let all move around you, Just  
Be.   
Bhagavan says - "To know and not to think"   
Salutations to Sri Ramana

## Re:[43] How to watch the sense 'I am'  
Author: Subramanian.R       Date: March 16, 2010, 06:33:11 AM  
---  
The non existent ego coming out of the non existent mind watches the Self.  
But   
in the beginning, it watches only the thoughts. In a thoughtless abandon, it  
watches   
the Self, in the sense it becomes the Self. The last stage, " watching the  
Self and   
being the Self" is through Guru's Grace. Bhagavan Ramana says in Sri  
Arunachala   
Akshara Mana Maalai: Do not show the mirror to this noseless person and makes  
him   
ashamed. Please lift me up and hug me. (AAMM 91)   
Arunachala Siva.

## Re:[44]ఓం నమో భగవతే శ్రీ రమణాయ  How to watch the sense 'I am'  
Author: prasanth_ramana_maharshiDate: June 29, 2010, 11:28:40 AM  
---  
Nice discussion.   
Nice points raised by subramanian garu,nagaraj garu and udai garu.   
I agree with subramanian garu regarding Suddha Manas,or Sattva Manas, which  
does not produce any prarabdha effect. Bhagavan Ramana did write books, did  
have some thoughts,why only thoughts, He did have dreams too.   
I agree with udai garu regarding we cannot have control over our thoughts and  
it is not like we desire and hence we have thoughts.   
Only because we cannot have control over our thoughts several techniques like  
breath control,self enquiry.... are mentioned.   
In Bhagavad Gita Ch6 Text35 Lord Krishna says,   
The Blessed Lord said: O mighty-armed son of Kunti, **it is undoubtedly very  
difficult to curb the restless mind, but it is possible by constant practice  
and by detachment.**   
Here detachment means having strong conviction that ' i am not the  
mind,body,senses...' which reminds Adi sankara's Nirvana Satakam poem.   
Once bhagavan said   
If the outlook changes, the troubles of the world will not worry us. Are the  
waves different from the ocean? Why do the waves occur at all? If asked, what  
reply can we give? The troubles in the world also are like that. Waves come  
and go. If it is found out that they are not different from Atma this worry  
will not exist.

## Re:[32] How to watch the sense 'I am'  
Author: Subramanian.R       Date: January 13, 2010, 07:50:48 AM  
---  
Dear srkudai, Nagaraj,   
The sense of "I am" is simply experiencing. For seekers, they have   
to watch the sense of "I am". Thereafter, it is only experiencing   
not describable by thoughts and words and deeds. Bhagavan   
Ramana used to quote Saint Tayumanavar and another old song   
in this context.   
Tayumanavar: It is like a newly married girl, coming out of the nuptial room in   
the early morning. What shall she say about her experience?   
She will not talk or describe to anyone. Even to her mother who   
is waiting anxiously in the morning, she would simply give a small   
smile and rush to take bath! Imagine, a celibate saint poet has   
written this! A celibate Brahma Jnani has quoted this!   
The old song: (Which Devaraja Mudaliar quotes in his book   
"You are my mother and You are my father.": It is like a drunken fellow returning home at night. He does   
not know where his dhoti is, where is towel is, where his bed   
is. He does not want anything. He does not want even food.   
He simply wants to lie in bed with the experience.   
Arunachala Siva.
 ---  
Source:[http://web.archive.org/web/20100707040523/http://www.arunachala-ramana.org/forum/index.php?topic=4337.msg11163](http://web.archive.org/web/20100707040523/http://www.arunachala-ramana.org/forum/index.php?topic=4337.msg11163)   
---  

## Re:[33] How to watch the sense 'I am'  
Author: Nagaraj             Date: January 13, 2010, 05:35:22 PM  
---  
Dear I,   
There is really no sense of experiencing "I am". it is simply being. It  
remains experience so long the Self enquiry continues till the mind/I merges  
where the perfect Self emerges as 'I-I'   
The example quoted by Ramana Maharshi is the first (stage) in what he says: "First the Self sees itself as object, then the Self sees itself as Void, and  
finally it sees itiself as Self, here there is no seeing as seeing is being"   
Therefore,   
Experiencing the sense of "I am" is "First the Self sees itself as object"   
and   
in reality, "I am" is simply being - "and finally it sees itiself as Self,  
here there is no seeing as seeing is being"   
Which is why I have always stressed in my other posts that Bhagawan's answers  
to several questions were tailor made as per the Pakva of the Questioneer.  
Those answers and Dialogues recorded as books should not be taken at face  
value as his answers to our same question. We have seen several instances  
where Bhagawan has responded differently for same questions. But His grace  
shall take care of the devotee all through!   
Salutations to Sri Ramana.   
« _Last Edit: January 13, 2010, 05:38:10 PM by Nagaraj_

neccessary...if you are totally confortabel with beeing bound then you are not

no-doer-that reality is the ever present **here and now** and no matter where  
oyu turn your attention to (sense object, inner feeling etc) all you find is  
blissfull open space..you may know, you may feel it but when the karmic jungle  
of thoughts can pull you out of htis "vision" then effor tis still important   
so thats I all I can say..and I know htat I want give oyu satisfactory  
answers....its not my job anyway   
matthias

## Re:[38] How to watch the sense 'I am'  
Author: Nagaraj             Date: March 15, 2010, 06:11:00 PM  
---  
Dear I,   
Quote from: Akira on March 15, 2010, 04:14:41 PM  
Quote from: snow on January 07, 2010, 03:06:33 PM  
Nisargadatta Maharaj said that it is very important to watch "I-am-ness" all  
the time.   
How is that possible?   
How can the subject watch the subject itself?  
Bhagavans explanation is given below -   
"First the Self sees itself as object, then the Self sees itself as Void, and  
finally it sees itiself as Self, here there is no seeing as seeing is being"   
The subject is ego, ego first begins watching itself, ego watching ego, and as  
a result of such an enquiry ego ceases to exist and Self shines and when this  
(occurs) the Subject will not be there, the ego will not be there, the very  
need to know that you are the Self has to end.   
Salutations to Sri Ramana
 ---  
Source:[http://web.archive.org/web/20100707040523/http://www.arunachala-ramana.org/forum/index.php?topic=4337.msg11163](http://web.archive.org/web/20100707040523/http://www.arunachala-ramana.org/forum/index.php?topic=4337.msg11163)

## Re:[41] How to watch the sense 'I am'  
Author: Nagaraj             Date: March 16, 2010, 05:25:56 AM  
---  
Dear I,   
All interpretations and understanding are correct. There is no need for a  
confirmation from 'anothers' expereience, for understanding. For, it is  
ultimately only an acknowledgement for knowledge what one already has, thats  
all. If 'anothers' experience matches with our existing understanding, mind or  
the ego or the little 'I' nods in confirmation and at the same time, if the  
'anothers' experience does not matches with our existing understanding, mind  
or the ego or the little 'I' nods in non confirmation and this leads to  
discussions, etc... anhd the Mind - ego - little 'I' goes on discussing so  
long the so called 'another' confirms to its own existing or preconceived  
knowledge.   
The 'one' that wants knowledge is the ego, the knowledge that is being created  
in the process is also the ego's. The Mind some how wants to be acknowledged  
as a 'Jnani' or it wants to be acknowledged as a super consciousness, or it  
wants to just enjoy, relish having the title of "Self" or acknowledgement for  
having 'Self-Realised'   
So in all these, who is the one that is wanting to get 'realised'? it is the  
ego - mind - little 'I'. Its like, as a stage drama is being enacted, you act  
as 'Ravana' character and forget that you are just the actor, and as a  
character - 'Ravana' tries to realise its Self as 'Rama' \- which eventually  
becomes another character in itself. The ego - mind - little 'I' gets lost in  
the character of 'Ravana' tries so hard to realised its Self as 'Rama' instead  
of just casting away just the character of Ravana and remain as the one who  
performed the character.   
Salutations to Sri Ramana
 ---  
Source:[http://web.archive.org/web/20100707040523/http://www.arunachala-ramana.org/forum/index.php?topic=4337.msg11163](http://web.archive.org/web/20100707040523/http://www.arunachala-ramana.org/forum/index.php?topic=4337.msg11163)   
---

## Re:[38] How to watch the sense 'I am'  
Author: Nagaraj             Date: March 15, 2010, 06:11:00 PM  
---  
Dear I,   
Quote from: Akira on March 15, 2010, 04:14:41 PM  
Quote from: snow on January 07, 2010, 03:06:33 PM  
Nisargadatta Maharaj said that it is very important to watch "I-am-ness" all  
the time.   
How is that possible?   
How can the subject watch the subject itself?  
Bhagavans explanation is given below -   
"First the Self sees itself as object, then the Self sees itself as Void, and  
finally it sees itiself as Self, here there is no seeing as seeing is being"   
The subject is ego, ego first begins watching itself, ego watching ego, and as  
a result of such an enquiry ego ceases to exist and Self shines and when this  
(occurs) the Subject will not be there, the ego will not be there, the very  
need to know that you are the Self has to end.   
Salutations to Sri Ramana

## Re:[41] How to watch the sense 'I am'  
Author: Nagaraj             Date: March 16, 2010, 05:25:56 AM  
---  
Dear I,   
All interpretations and understanding are correct. There is no need for a  
confirmation from 'anothers' expereience, for understanding. For, it is  
ultimately only an acknowledgement for knowledge what one already has, thats  
all. If 'anothers' experience matches with our existing understanding, mind or  
the ego or the little 'I' nods in confirmation and at the same time, if the  
'anothers' experience does not matches with our existing understanding, mind  
or the ego or the little 'I' nods in non confirmation and this leads to  
discussions, etc... anhd the Mind - ego - little 'I' goes on discussing so  
long the so called 'another' confirms to its own existing or preconceived  
knowledge.   
The 'one' that wants knowledge is the ego, the knowledge that is being created  
in the process is also the ego's. The Mind some how wants to be acknowledged  
as a 'Jnani' or it wants to be acknowledged as a super consciousness, or it  
wants to just enjoy, relish having the title of "Self" or acknowledgement for  
having 'Self-Realised'   
So in all these, who is the one that is wanting to get 'realised'? it is the  
ego - mind - little 'I'. Its like, as a stage drama is being enacted, you act  
as 'Ravana' character and forget that you are just the actor, and as a  
character - 'Ravana' tries to realise its Self as 'Rama' \- which eventually  
becomes another character in itself. The ego - mind - little 'I' gets lost in  
the character of 'Ravana' tries so hard to realised its Self as 'Rama' instead  
of just casting away just the character of Ravana and remain as the one who  
performed the character.   
Salutations to Sri Ramana
 ---  
Source:[http://web.archive.org/web/20100707040324/http://www.arunachala-ramana.org/forum/index.php?topic=4337.msg11178](http://web.archive.org/web/20100707040324/http://www.arunachala-ramana.org/forum/index.php?topic=4337.msg11178)   
---  

## Re:[42] How to watch the sense 'I am'  
Author: Nagaraj             Date: March 16, 2010, 06:15:28 AM  
---  
Dear I,   
that means, like Krishna says in the Gita, Uddaret Atmanaatmaanam, the Self is  
its own friend and foe, one has to lift Himself from his own higher Self and  
not let itself fall from its own lower Self.   
Mis-interpretaions and mis understandings are biggest grace in themselves,  
they bestow higher grace than 'Knowledge' itself. It is only because of Mis-  
interpretaions and mis understandings that we begin to enquire further.   
More over it is only the Mind that distinguishes between Misunderstanding and  
Understanding.   
Meditation, for is just being aware of ones own ego, till it gets dissolved  
into nothingness or everything ness.   
Meditation is for me, "Chumma Iru", "Just being" Let all move around you, Just  
Be.   
Bhagavan says - "To know and not to think"   
Salutations to Sri Ramana
 ---  
Source:[http://web.archive.org/web/20100707040324/http://www.arunachala-ramana.org/forum/index.php?topic=4337.msg11178](http://web.archive.org/web/20100707040324/http://www.arunachala-ramana.org/forum/index.php?topic=4337.msg11178)

## Re:[43] How to watch the sense 'I am'  
Author: Subramanian.R       Date: March 16, 2010, 06:33:11 AM  
---  
The non existent ego coming out of the non existent mind watches the Self.  
But   
in the beginning, it watches only the thoughts. In a thoughtless abandon, it  
watches   
the Self, in the sense it becomes the Self. The last stage, " watching the  
Self and   
being the Self" is through Guru's Grace. Bhagavan Ramana says in Sri  
Arunachala   
Akshara Mana Maalai: Do not show the mirror to this noseless person and makes  
him   
ashamed. Please lift me up and hug me. (AAMM 91)   
Arunachala Siva.
 ---

## Re:[44]ఓం నమో భగవతే శ్రీ రమణాయ  How to watch the sense 'I am'  
Author: prasanth_ramana_maharshiDate: June 29, 2010, 11:28:40 AM  
---  
Nice discussion.   
Nice points raised by subramanian garu,nagaraj garu and udai garu.   
I agree with subramanian garu regarding Suddha Manas,or Sattva Manas, which  
does not produce any prarabdha effect. Bhagavan Ramana did write books, did  
have some thoughts,why only thoughts, He did have dreams too.   
I agree with udai garu regarding we cannot have control over our thoughts and  
it is not like we desire and hence we have thoughts.   
Only because we cannot have control over our thoughts several techniques like  
breath control,self enquiry.... are mentioned.   
In Bhagavad Gita Ch6 Text35 Lord Krishna says,   
The Blessed Lord said: O mighty-armed son of Kunti, **it is undoubtedly very  
difficult to curb the restless mind, but it is possible by constant practice  
and by detachment.**   
Here detachment means having strong conviction that ' i am not the  
mind,body,senses...' which reminds Adi sankara's Nirvana Satakam poem.   
Once bhagavan said   
If the outlook changes, the troubles of the world will not worry us. Are the  
waves different from the ocean? Why do the waves occur at all? If asked, what  
reply can we give? The troubles in the world also are like that. Waves come  
and go. If it is found out that they are not different from Atma this worry  
will not exist.
 ---

## Re:[32] How to watch the sense 'I am'  
Author: Subramanian.R       Date: January 13, 2010, 07:50:48 AM  
---  
Dear srkudai, Nagaraj,   
The sense of "I am" is simply experiencing. For seekers, they have   
to watch the sense of "I am". Thereafter, it is only experiencing   
not describable by thoughts and words and deeds. Bhagavan   
Ramana used to quote Saint Tayumanavar and another old song   
in this context.   
Tayumanavar: It is like a newly married girl, coming out of the nuptial room in   
the early morning. What shall she say about her experience?   
She will not talk or describe to anyone. Even to her mother who   
is waiting anxiously in the morning, she would simply give a small   
smile and rush to take bath! Imagine, a celibate saint poet has   
written this! A celibate Brahma Jnani has quoted this!   
The old song: (Which Devaraja Mudaliar quotes in his book   
"You are my mother and You are my father.": It is like a drunken fellow returning home at night. He does   
not know where his dhoti is, where is towel is, where his bed   
is. He does not want anything. He does not want even food.   
He simply wants to lie in bed with the experience.   
Arunachala Siva.
 ---  
Source:[http://web.archive.org/web/20100707040638/http://www.arunachala-ramana.org/forum/index.php?topic=4337.msg12887](http://web.archive.org/web/20100707040638/http://www.arunachala-ramana.org/forum/index.php?topic=4337.msg12887)   
---  

## Re:[33] How to watch the sense 'I am'  
Author: Nagaraj             Date: January 13, 2010, 05:35:22 PM  
---  
Dear I,   
There is really no sense of experiencing "I am". it is simply being. It  
remains experience so long the Self enquiry continues till the mind/I merges  
where the perfect Self emerges as 'I-I'   
The example quoted by Ramana Maharshi is the first (stage) in what he says: "First the Self sees itself as object, then the Self sees itself as Void, and  
finally it sees itiself as Self, here there is no seeing as seeing is being"   
Therefore,   
Experiencing the sense of "I am" is "First the Self sees itself as object"   
and   
in reality, "I am" is simply being - "and finally it sees itiself as Self,  
here there is no seeing as seeing is being"   
Which is why I have always stressed in my other posts that Bhagawan's answers  
to several questions were tailor made as per the Pakva of the Questioneer.  
Those answers and Dialogues recorded as books should not be taken at face  
value as his answers to our same question. We have seen several instances  
where Bhagawan has responded differently for same questions. But His grace  
shall take care of the devotee all through!   
Salutations to Sri Ramana.   
« _Last Edit: January 13, 2010, 05:38:10 PM by Nagaraj_

shall take care of the devotee all through!

## Re:[38] How to watch the sense 'I am'  
Author: Nagaraj             Date: March 15, 2010, 06:11:00 PM  
---  
Dear I,   
Quote from: Akira on March 15, 2010, 04:14:41 PM  
Quote from: snow on January 07, 2010, 03:06:33 PM  
Nisargadatta Maharaj said that it is very important to watch "I-am-ness" all  
the time.   
How is that possible?   
How can the subject watch the subject itself?  
Bhagavans explanation is given below -   
"First the Self sees itself as object, then the Self sees itself as Void, and  
finally it sees itiself as Self, here there is no seeing as seeing is being"   
The subject is ego, ego first begins watching itself, ego watching ego, and as  
a result of such an enquiry ego ceases to exist and Self shines and when this  
(occurs) the Subject will not be there, the ego will not be there, the very  
need to know that you are the Self has to end.   
Salutations to Sri Ramana
 ---  
Source:[http://web.archive.org/web/20100707040149/http://www.arunachala-ramana.org/forum/index.php?topic=4337.msg12889](http://web.archive.org/web/20100707040149/http://www.arunachala-ramana.org/forum/index.php?topic=4337.msg12889)

## Re:[41] How to watch the sense 'I am'  
Author: Nagaraj             Date: March 16, 2010, 05:25:56 AM  
---  
Dear I,   
All interpretations and understanding are correct. There is no need for a  
confirmation from 'anothers' expereience, for understanding. For, it is  
ultimately only an acknowledgement for knowledge what one already has, thats  
all. If 'anothers' experience matches with our existing understanding, mind or  
the ego or the little 'I' nods in confirmation and at the same time, if the  
'anothers' experience does not matches with our existing understanding, mind  
or the ego or the little 'I' nods in non confirmation and this leads to  
discussions, etc... anhd the Mind - ego - little 'I' goes on discussing so  
long the so called 'another' confirms to its own existing or preconceived  
knowledge.   
The 'one' that wants knowledge is the ego, the knowledge that is being created  
in the process is also the ego's. The Mind some how wants to be acknowledged  
as a 'Jnani' or it wants to be acknowledged as a super consciousness, or it  
wants to just enjoy, relish having the title of "Self" or acknowledgement for  
having 'Self-Realised'   
So in all these, who is the one that is wanting to get 'realised'? it is the  
ego - mind - little 'I'. Its like, as a stage drama is being enacted, you act  
as 'Ravana' character and forget that you are just the actor, and as a  
character - 'Ravana' tries to realise its Self as 'Rama' \- which eventually  
becomes another character in itself. The ego - mind - little 'I' gets lost in  
the character of 'Ravana' tries so hard to realised its Self as 'Rama' instead  
of just casting away just the character of Ravana and remain as the one who  
performed the character.   
Salutations to Sri Ramana
 ---  
Source:[http://web.archive.org/web/20100707040149/http://www.arunachala-ramana.org/forum/index.php?topic=4337.msg12889](http://web.archive.org/web/20100707040149/http://www.arunachala-ramana.org/forum/index.php?topic=4337.msg12889)   
---  

## Re:[42] How to watch the sense 'I am'  
Author: Nagaraj             Date: March 16, 2010, 06:15:28 AM  
---  
Dear I,   
that means, like Krishna says in the Gita, Uddaret Atmanaatmaanam, the Self is  
its own friend and foe, one has to lift Himself from his own higher Self and  
not let itself fall from its own lower Self.   
Mis-interpretaions and mis understandings are biggest grace in themselves,  
they bestow higher grace than 'Knowledge' itself. It is only because of Mis-  
interpretaions and mis understandings that we begin to enquire further.   
More over it is only the Mind that distinguishes between Misunderstanding and  
Understanding.   
Meditation, for is just being aware of ones own ego, till it gets dissolved  
into nothingness or everything ness.   
Meditation is for me, "Chumma Iru", "Just being" Let all move around you, Just  
Be.   
Bhagavan says - "To know and not to think"   
Salutations to Sri Ramana
 ---  
Source:[http://web.archive.org/web/20100707040149/http://www.arunachala-ramana.org/forum/index.php?topic=4337.msg12889](http://web.archive.org/web/20100707040149/http://www.arunachala-ramana.org/forum/index.php?topic=4337.msg12889)   
---  

## Re:[43] How to watch the sense 'I am'  
Author: Subramanian.R       Date: March 16, 2010, 06:33:11 AM  
---  
The non existent ego coming out of the non existent mind watches the Self.  
But   
in the beginning, it watches only the thoughts. In a thoughtless abandon, it  
watches   
the Self, in the sense it becomes the Self. The last stage, " watching the  
Self and   
being the Self" is through Guru's Grace. Bhagavan Ramana says in Sri  
Arunachala   
Akshara Mana Maalai: Do not show the mirror to this noseless person and makes  
him   
ashamed. Please lift me up and hug me. (AAMM 91)   
Arunachala Siva.
 ---  
Source:[http://web.archive.org/web/20100707040149/http://www.arunachala-ramana.org/forum/index.php?topic=4337.msg12889](http://web.archive.org/web/20100707040149/http://www.arunachala-ramana.org/forum/index.php?topic=4337.msg12889)

## Re:[44]ఓం నమో భగవతే శ్రీ రమణాయ  How to watch the sense 'I am'  
Author: prasanth_ramana_maharshiDate: June 29, 2010, 11:28:40 AM  
---  
Nice discussion.   
Nice points raised by subramanian garu,nagaraj garu and udai garu.   
I agree with subramanian garu regarding Suddha Manas,or Sattva Manas, which  
does not produce any prarabdha effect. Bhagavan Ramana did write books, did  
have some thoughts,why only thoughts, He did have dreams too.   
I agree with udai garu regarding we cannot have control over our thoughts and  
it is not like we desire and hence we have thoughts.   
Only because we cannot have control over our thoughts several techniques like  
breath control,self enquiry.... are mentioned.   
In Bhagavad Gita Ch6 Text35 Lord Krishna says,   
The Blessed Lord said: O mighty-armed son of Kunti, **it is undoubtedly very  
difficult to curb the restless mind, but it is possible by constant practice  
and by detachment.**   
Here detachment means having strong conviction that ' i am not the  
mind,body,senses...' which reminds Adi sankara's Nirvana Satakam poem.   
Once bhagavan said   
If the outlook changes, the troubles of the world will not worry us. Are the  
waves different from the ocean? Why do the waves occur at all? If asked, what  
reply can we give? The troubles in the world also are like that. Waves come  
and go. If it is found out that they are not different from Atma this worry  
will not exist.
 ---

## Re:[32] How to watch the sense 'I am'  
Author: Subramanian.R       Date: January 13, 2010, 07:50:48 AM  
---  
Dear srkudai, Nagaraj,   
The sense of "I am" is simply experiencing. For seekers, they have   
to watch the sense of "I am". Thereafter, it is only experiencing   
not describable by thoughts and words and deeds. Bhagavan   
Ramana used to quote Saint Tayumanavar and another old song   
in this context.   
Tayumanavar: It is like a newly married girl, coming out of the nuptial room in   
the early morning. What shall she say about her experience?   
She will not talk or describe to anyone. Even to her mother who   
is waiting anxiously in the morning, she would simply give a small   
smile and rush to take bath! Imagine, a celibate saint poet has   
written this! A celibate Brahma Jnani has quoted this!   
The old song: (Which Devaraja Mudaliar quotes in his book   
"You are my mother and You are my father.": It is like a drunken fellow returning home at night. He does   
not know where his dhoti is, where is towel is, where his bed   
is. He does not want anything. He does not want even food.   
He simply wants to lie in bed with the experience.   
Arunachala Siva.
 ---  
Source:[http://web.archive.org/web/20100707040441/http://www.arunachala-ramana.org/forum/index.php?topic=4337.msg12892](http://web.archive.org/web/20100707040441/http://www.arunachala-ramana.org/forum/index.php?topic=4337.msg12892)   
---  

## Re:[33] How to watch the sense 'I am'  
Author: Nagaraj             Date: January 13, 2010, 05:35:22 PM  
---  
Dear I,   
There is really no sense of experiencing "I am". it is simply being. It  
remains experience so long the Self enquiry continues till the mind/I merges  
where the perfect Self emerges as 'I-I'   
The example quoted by Ramana Maharshi is the first (stage) in what he says: "First the Self sees itself as object, then the Self sees itself as Void, and  
finally it sees itiself as Self, here there is no seeing as seeing is being"   
Therefore,   
Experiencing the sense of "I am" is "First the Self sees itself as object"   
and   
in reality, "I am" is simply being - "and finally it sees itiself as Self,  
here there is no seeing as seeing is being"   
Which is why I have always stressed in my other posts that Bhagawan's answers  
to several questions were tailor made as per the Pakva of the Questioneer.  
Those answers and Dialogues recorded as books should not be taken at face  
value as his answers to our same question. We have seen several instances  
where Bhagawan has responded differently for same questions. But His grace  
shall take care of the devotee all through!   
Salutations to Sri Ramana.

## Re:[32] How to watch the sense 'I am'  
Author: Subramanian.R       Date: January 13, 2010, 07:50:48 AM  
---  
Dear srkudai, Nagaraj,   
The sense of "I am" is simply experiencing. For seekers, they have   
to watch the sense of "I am". Thereafter, it is only experiencing   
not describable by thoughts and words and deeds. Bhagavan   
Ramana used to quote Saint Tayumanavar and another old song   
in this context.   
Tayumanavar: It is like a newly married girl, coming out of the nuptial room in   
the early morning. What shall she say about her experience?   
She will not talk or describe to anyone. Even to her mother who   
is waiting anxiously in the morning, she would simply give a small   
smile and rush to take bath! Imagine, a celibate saint poet has   
written this! A celibate Brahma Jnani has quoted this!   
The old song: (Which Devaraja Mudaliar quotes in his book   
"You are my mother and You are my father.": It is like a drunken fellow returning home at night. He does   
not know where his dhoti is, where is towel is, where his bed   
is. He does not want anything. He does not want even food.   
He simply wants to lie in bed with the experience.   
Arunachala Siva.
 ---  
Source:[http://web.archive.org/web/20100707040050/http://www.arunachala-ramana.org/forum/index.php?topic=4337.msg12893](http://web.archive.org/web/20100707040050/http://www.arunachala-ramana.org/forum/index.php?topic=4337.msg12893)   
---  

## Re:[33] How to watch the sense 'I am'  
Author: Nagaraj             Date: January 13, 2010, 05:35:22 PM  
---  
Dear I,   
There is really no sense of experiencing "I am". it is simply being. It  
remains experience so long the Self enquiry continues till the mind/I merges  
where the perfect Self emerges as 'I-I'   
The example quoted by Ramana Maharshi is the first (stage) in what he says: "First the Self sees itself as object, then the Self sees itself as Void, and  
finally it sees itiself as Self, here there is no seeing as seeing is being"   
Therefore,   
Experiencing the sense of "I am" is "First the Self sees itself as object"   
and   
in reality, "I am" is simply being - "and finally it sees itiself as Self,  
here there is no seeing as seeing is being"   
Which is why I have always stressed in my other posts that Bhagawan's answers  
to several questions were tailor made as per the Pakva of the Questioneer.  
Those answers and Dialogues recorded as books should not be taken at face  
value as his answers to our same question. We have seen several instances  
where Bhagawan has responded differently for same questions. But His grace  
shall take care of the devotee all through!   
Salutations to Sri Ramana.   
« _Last Edit: January 13, 2010, 05:38:10 PM by Nagaraj_

## Re:[38] How to watch the sense 'I am'  
Author: Nagaraj             Date: March 15, 2010, 06:11:00 PM  
---  
Dear I,   
Quote from: Akira on March 15, 2010, 04:14:41 PM  
Quote from: snow on January 07, 2010, 03:06:33 PM  
Nisargadatta Maharaj said that it is very important to watch "I-am-ness" all  
the time.   
How is that possible?   
How can the subject watch the subject itself?  
Bhagavans explanation is given below -   
"First the Self sees itself as object, then the Self sees itself as Void, and  
finally it sees itiself as Self, here there is no seeing as seeing is being"   
The subject is ego, ego first begins watching itself, ego watching ego, and as  
a result of such an enquiry ego ceases to exist and Self shines and when this  
(occurs) the Subject will not be there, the ego will not be there, the very  
need to know that you are the Self has to end.   
Salutations to Sri Ramana
 ---  
Source:[http://web.archive.org/web/20100707040050/http://www.arunachala-ramana.org/forum/index.php?topic=4337.msg12893](http://web.archive.org/web/20100707040050/http://www.arunachala-ramana.org/forum/index.php?topic=4337.msg12893)

## Re:[41] How to watch the sense 'I am'  
Author: Nagaraj             Date: March 16, 2010, 05:25:56 AM  
---  
Dear I,   
All interpretations and understanding are correct. There is no need for a  
confirmation from 'anothers' expereience, for understanding. For, it is  
ultimately only an acknowledgement for knowledge what one already has, thats  
all. If 'anothers' experience matches with our existing understanding, mind or  
the ego or the little 'I' nods in confirmation and at the same time, if the  
'anothers' experience does not matches with our existing understanding, mind  
or the ego or the little 'I' nods in non confirmation and this leads to  
discussions, etc... anhd the Mind - ego - little 'I' goes on discussing so  
long the so called 'another' confirms to its own existing or preconceived  
knowledge.   
The 'one' that wants knowledge is the ego, the knowledge that is being created  
in the process is also the ego's. The Mind some how wants to be acknowledged  
as a 'Jnani' or it wants to be acknowledged as a super consciousness, or it  
wants to just enjoy, relish having the title of "Self" or acknowledgement for  
having 'Self-Realised'   
So in all these, who is the one that is wanting to get 'realised'? it is the  
ego - mind - little 'I'. Its like, as a stage drama is being enacted, you act  
as 'Ravana' character and forget that you are just the actor, and as a  
character - 'Ravana' tries to realise its Self as 'Rama' \- which eventually  
becomes another character in itself. The ego - mind - little 'I' gets lost in  
the character of 'Ravana' tries so hard to realised its Self as 'Rama' instead  
of just casting away just the character of Ravana and remain as the one who  
performed the character.   
Salutations to Sri Ramana
 ---  
Source:[http://web.archive.org/web/20100707040050/http://www.arunachala-ramana.org/forum/index.php?topic=4337.msg12893](http://web.archive.org/web/20100707040050/http://www.arunachala-ramana.org/forum/index.php?topic=4337.msg12893)   
---  

## Re:[42] How to watch the sense 'I am'  
Author: Nagaraj             Date: March 16, 2010, 06:15:28 AM  
---  
Dear I,   
that means, like Krishna says in the Gita, Uddaret Atmanaatmaanam, the Self is  
its own friend and foe, one has to lift Himself from his own higher Self and  
not let itself fall from its own lower Self.   
Mis-interpretaions and mis understandings are biggest grace in themselves,  
they bestow higher grace than 'Knowledge' itself. It is only because of Mis-  
interpretaions and mis understandings that we begin to enquire further.   
More over it is only the Mind that distinguishes between Misunderstanding and  
Understanding.   
Meditation, for is just being aware of ones own ego, till it gets dissolved  
into nothingness or everything ness.   
Meditation is for me, "Chumma Iru", "Just being" Let all move around you, Just  
Be.   
Bhagavan says - "To know and not to think"   
Salutations to Sri Ramana
 ---  
Source:[http://web.archive.org/web/20100707040050/http://www.arunachala-ramana.org/forum/index.php?topic=4337.msg12893](http://web.archive.org/web/20100707040050/http://www.arunachala-ramana.org/forum/index.php?topic=4337.msg12893)   
---  

## Re:[43] How to watch the sense 'I am'  
Author: Subramanian.R       Date: March 16, 2010, 06:33:11 AM  
---  
The non existent ego coming out of the non existent mind watches the Self.  
But   
in the beginning, it watches only the thoughts. In a thoughtless abandon, it  
watches   
the Self, in the sense it becomes the Self. The last stage, " watching the  
Self and   
being the Self" is through Guru's Grace. Bhagavan Ramana says in Sri  
Arunachala   
Akshara Mana Maalai: Do not show the mirror to this noseless person and makes  
him   
ashamed. Please lift me up and hug me. (AAMM 91)   
Arunachala Siva.
 ---  
Source:[http://web.archive.org/web/20100707040050/http://www.arunachala-ramana.org/forum/index.php?topic=4337.msg12893](http://web.archive.org/web/20100707040050/http://www.arunachala-ramana.org/forum/index.php?topic=4337.msg12893)

## Re:[44]ఓం నమో భగవతే శ్రీ రమణాయ  How to watch the sense 'I am'  
Author: prasanth_ramana_maharshiDate: June 29, 2010, 11:28:40 AM  
---  
Nice discussion.   
Nice points raised by subramanian garu,nagaraj garu and udai garu.   
I agree with subramanian garu regarding Suddha Manas,or Sattva Manas, which  
does not produce any prarabdha effect. Bhagavan Ramana did write books, did  
have some thoughts,why only thoughts, He did have dreams too.   
I agree with udai garu regarding we cannot have control over our thoughts and  
it is not like we desire and hence we have thoughts.   
Only because we cannot have control over our thoughts several techniques like  
breath control,self enquiry.... are mentioned.   
In Bhagavad Gita Ch6 Text35 Lord Krishna says,   
The Blessed Lord said: O mighty-armed son of Kunti, **it is undoubtedly very  
difficult to curb the restless mind, but it is possible by constant practice  
and by detachment.**   
Here detachment means having strong conviction that ' i am not the  
mind,body,senses...' which reminds Adi sankara's Nirvana Satakam poem.   
Once bhagavan said   
If the outlook changes, the troubles of the world will not worry us. Are the  
waves different from the ocean? Why do the waves occur at all? If asked, what  
reply can we give? The troubles in the world also are like that. Waves come  
and go. If it is found out that they are not different from Atma this worry  
will not exist.
 ---

## Re:[43] How to watch the sense 'I am'  
Author: Subramanian.R       Date: March 16, 2010, 06:33:11 AM  
---  
The non existent ego coming out of the non existent mind watches the Self.  
But   
in the beginning, it watches only the thoughts. In a thoughtless abandon, it  
watches   
the Self, in the sense it becomes the Self. The last stage, " watching the  
Self and   
being the Self" is through Guru's Grace. Bhagavan Ramana says in Sri  
Arunachala   
Akshara Mana Maalai: Do not show the mirror to this noseless person and makes  
him   
ashamed. Please lift me up and hug me. (AAMM 91)   
Arunachala Siva.

## Re:[44]ఓం నమో భగవతే శ్రీ రమణాయ  How to watch the sense 'I am'  
Author: prasanth_ramana_maharshiDate: June 29, 2010, 11:28:40 AM  
---  
Nice discussion.   
Nice points raised by subramanian garu,nagaraj garu and udai garu.   
I agree with subramanian garu regarding Suddha Manas,or Sattva Manas, which  
does not produce any prarabdha effect. Bhagavan Ramana did write books, did  
have some thoughts,why only thoughts, He did have dreams too.   
I agree with udai garu regarding we cannot have control over our thoughts and  
it is not like we desire and hence we have thoughts.   
Only because we cannot have control over our thoughts several techniques like  
breath control,self enquiry.... are mentioned.   
In Bhagavad Gita Ch6 Text35 Lord Krishna says,   
The Blessed Lord said: O mighty-armed son of Kunti, **it is undoubtedly very  
difficult to curb the restless mind, but it is possible by constant practice  
and by detachment.**   
Here detachment means having strong conviction that ' i am not the  
mind,body,senses...' which reminds Adi sankara's Nirvana Satakam poem.   
Once bhagavan said   
If the outlook changes, the troubles of the world will not worry us. Are the  
waves different from the ocean? Why do the waves occur at all? If asked, what  
reply can we give? The troubles in the world also are like that. Waves come  
and go. If it is found out that they are not different from Atma this worry  
will not exist.

## Re:[32] How to watch the sense 'I am'  
Author: Subramanian.R       Date: January 13, 2010, 07:50:48 AM  
---  
Dear srkudai, Nagaraj,   
The sense of "I am" is simply experiencing. For seekers, they have   
to watch the sense of "I am". Thereafter, it is only experiencing   
not describable by thoughts and words and deeds. Bhagavan   
Ramana used to quote Saint Tayumanavar and another old song   
in this context.   
Tayumanavar: It is like a newly married girl, coming out of the nuptial room in   
the early morning. What shall she say about her experience?   
She will not talk or describe to anyone. Even to her mother who   
is waiting anxiously in the morning, she would simply give a small   
smile and rush to take bath! Imagine, a celibate saint poet has   
written this! A celibate Brahma Jnani has quoted this!   
The old song: (Which Devaraja Mudaliar quotes in his book   
"You are my mother and You are my father.": It is like a drunken fellow returning home at night. He does   
not know where his dhoti is, where is towel is, where his bed   
is. He does not want anything. He does not want even food.   
He simply wants to lie in bed with the experience.   
Arunachala Siva.
 ---  
Source:[http://web.archive.org/web/20100707040501/http://www.arunachala-ramana.org/forum/index.php?topic=4337.msg12896](http://web.archive.org/web/20100707040501/http://www.arunachala-ramana.org/forum/index.php?topic=4337.msg12896)   
---  

## Re:[33] How to watch the sense 'I am'  
Author: Nagaraj             Date: January 13, 2010, 05:35:22 PM  
---  
Dear I,   
There is really no sense of experiencing "I am". it is simply being. It  
remains experience so long the Self enquiry continues till the mind/I merges  
where the perfect Self emerges as 'I-I'   
The example quoted by Ramana Maharshi is the first (stage) in what he says: "First the Self sees itself as object, then the Self sees itself as Void, and  
finally it sees itiself as Self, here there is no seeing as seeing is being"   
Therefore,   
Experiencing the sense of "I am" is "First the Self sees itself as object"   
and   
in reality, "I am" is simply being - "and finally it sees itiself as Self,  
here there is no seeing as seeing is being"   
Which is why I have always stressed in my other posts that Bhagawan's answers  
to several questions were tailor made as per the Pakva of the Questioneer.  
Those answers and Dialogues recorded as books should not be taken at face  
value as his answers to our same question. We have seen several instances  
where Bhagawan has responded differently for same questions. But His grace  
shall take care of the devotee all through!   
Salutations to Sri Ramana.   
« _Last Edit: January 13, 2010, 05:38:10 PM by Nagaraj_

## Re:[38] How to watch the sense 'I am'  
Author: Nagaraj             Date: March 15, 2010, 06:11:00 PM  
---  
Dear I,   
Quote from: Akira on March 15, 2010, 04:14:41 PM  
Quote from: snow on January 07, 2010, 03:06:33 PM  
Nisargadatta Maharaj said that it is very important to watch "I-am-ness" all  
the time.   
How is that possible?   
How can the subject watch the subject itself?  
Bhagavans explanation is given below -   
"First the Self sees itself as object, then the Self sees itself as Void, and  
finally it sees itiself as Self, here there is no seeing as seeing is being"   
The subject is ego, ego first begins watching itself, ego watching ego, and as  
a result of such an enquiry ego ceases to exist and Self shines and when this  
(occurs) the Subject will not be there, the ego will not be there, the very  
need to know that you are the Self has to end.   
Salutations to Sri Ramana
 ---  
Source:[http://web.archive.org/web/20100707040501/http://www.arunachala-ramana.org/forum/index.php?topic=4337.msg12896](http://web.archive.org/web/20100707040501/http://www.arunachala-ramana.org/forum/index.php?topic=4337.msg12896)

## Re:[41] How to watch the sense 'I am'  
Author: Nagaraj             Date: March 16, 2010, 05:25:56 AM  
---  
Dear I,   
All interpretations and understanding are correct. There is no need for a  
confirmation from 'anothers' expereience, for understanding. For, it is  
ultimately only an acknowledgement for knowledge what one already has, thats  
all. If 'anothers' experience matches with our existing understanding, mind or  
the ego or the little 'I' nods in confirmation and at the same time, if the  
'anothers' experience does not matches with our existing understanding, mind  
or the ego or the little 'I' nods in non confirmation and this leads to  
discussions, etc... anhd the Mind - ego - little 'I' goes on discussing so  
long the so called 'another' confirms to its own existing or preconceived  
knowledge.   
The 'one' that wants knowledge is the ego, the knowledge that is being created  
in the process is also the ego's. The Mind some how wants to be acknowledged  
as a 'Jnani' or it wants to be acknowledged as a super consciousness, or it  
wants to just enjoy, relish having the title of "Self" or acknowledgement for  
having 'Self-Realised'   
So in all these, who is the one that is wanting to get 'realised'? it is the  
ego - mind - little 'I'. Its like, as a stage drama is being enacted, you act  
as 'Ravana' character and forget that you are just the actor, and as a  
character - 'Ravana' tries to realise its Self as 'Rama' \- which eventually  
becomes another character in itself. The ego - mind - little 'I' gets lost in  
the character of 'Ravana' tries so hard to realised its Self as 'Rama' instead  
of just casting away just the character of Ravana and remain as the one who  
performed the character.   
Salutations to Sri Ramana
 ---  
Source:[http://web.archive.org/web/20100707040501/http://www.arunachala-ramana.org/forum/index.php?topic=4337.msg12896](http://web.archive.org/web/20100707040501/http://www.arunachala-ramana.org/forum/index.php?topic=4337.msg12896)   
---  

## Re:[42] How to watch the sense 'I am'  
Author: Nagaraj             Date: March 16, 2010, 06:15:28 AM  
---  
Dear I,   
that means, like Krishna says in the Gita, Uddaret Atmanaatmaanam, the Self is  
its own friend and foe, one has to lift Himself from his own higher Self and  
not let itself fall from its own lower Self.   
Mis-interpretaions and mis understandings are biggest grace in themselves,  
they bestow higher grace than 'Knowledge' itself. It is only because of Mis-  
interpretaions and mis understandings that we begin to enquire further.   
More over it is only the Mind that distinguishes between Misunderstanding and  
Understanding.   
Meditation, for is just being aware of ones own ego, till it gets dissolved  
into nothingness or everything ness.   
Meditation is for me, "Chumma Iru", "Just being" Let all move around you, Just  
Be.   
Bhagavan says - "To know and not to think"   
Salutations to Sri Ramana
 ---

Author: Nagaraj             Date: March 16, 2010, 05:25:56 AM  
---  
Dear I,   
All interpretations and understanding are correct. There is no need for a  
confirmation from 'anothers' expereience, for understanding. For, it is  
ultimately only an acknowledgement for knowledge what one already has, thats  
all. If 'anothers' experience matches with our existing understanding, mind or  
the ego or the little 'I' nods in confirmation and at the same time, if the  
'anothers' experience does not matches with our existing understanding, mind  
or the ego or the little 'I' nods in non confirmation and this leads to  
discussions, etc... anhd the Mind - ego - little 'I' goes on discussing so  
long the so called 'another' confirms to its own existing or preconceived  
knowledge.   
The 'one' that wants knowledge is the ego, the knowledge that is being created  
in the process is also the ego's. The Mind some how wants to be acknowledged  
as a 'Jnani' or it wants to be acknowledged as a super consciousness, or it  
wants to just enjoy, relish having the title of "Self" or acknowledgement for  
having 'Self-Realised'   
So in all these, who is the one that is wanting to get 'realised'? it is the  
ego - mind - little 'I'. Its like, as a stage drama is being enacted, you act  
as 'Ravana' character and forget that you are just the actor, and as a  
character - 'Ravana' tries to realise its Self as 'Rama' \- which eventually  
becomes another character in itself. The ego - mind - little 'I' gets lost in  
the character of 'Ravana' tries so hard to realised its Self as 'Rama' instead  
of just casting away just the character of Ravana and remain as the one who  
performed the character.   
Salutations to Sri Ramana
 ---  
Source:[http://web.archive.org/web/20100707040208/http://www.arunachala-ramana.org/forum/index.php?topic=4337.msg12899](http://web.archive.org/web/20100707040208/http://www.arunachala-ramana.org/forum/index.php?topic=4337.msg12899)   
---  

## Re:[42] How to watch the sense 'I am'  
Author: Nagaraj             Date: March 16, 2010, 06:15:28 AM  
---  
Dear I,   
that means, like Krishna says in the Gita, Uddaret Atmanaatmaanam, the Self is  
its own friend and foe, one has to lift Himself from his own higher Self and  
not let itself fall from its own lower Self.   
Mis-interpretaions and mis understandings are biggest grace in themselves,  
they bestow higher grace than 'Knowledge' itself. It is only because of Mis-  
interpretaions and mis understandings that we begin to enquire further.   
More over it is only the Mind that distinguishes between Misunderstanding and  
Understanding.   
Meditation, for is just being aware of ones own ego, till it gets dissolved  
into nothingness or everything ness.   
Meditation is for me, "Chumma Iru", "Just being" Let all move around you, Just  
Be.   
Bhagavan says - "To know and not to think"   
Salutations to Sri Ramana
 ---

## Re:[43] How to watch the sense 'I am'  
Author: Subramanian.R       Date: March 16, 2010, 06:33:11 AM  
---  
The non existent ego coming out of the non existent mind watches the Self.  
But   
in the beginning, it watches only the thoughts. In a thoughtless abandon, it  
watches   
the Self, in the sense it becomes the Self. The last stage, " watching the  
Self and   
being the Self" is through Guru's Grace. Bhagavan Ramana says in Sri  
Arunachala   
Akshara Mana Maalai: Do not show the mirror to this noseless person and makes  
him   
ashamed. Please lift me up and hug me. (AAMM 91)   
Arunachala Siva.
 ---

## Re:[44]ఓం నమో భగవతే శ్రీ రమణాయ  How to watch the sense 'I am'  
Author: prasanth_ramana_maharshiDate: June 29, 2010, 11:28:40 AM  
---  
Nice discussion.   
Nice points raised by subramanian garu,nagaraj garu and udai garu.   
I agree with subramanian garu regarding Suddha Manas,or Sattva Manas, which  
does not produce any prarabdha effect. Bhagavan Ramana did write books, did  
have some thoughts,why only thoughts, He did have dreams too.   
I agree with udai garu regarding we cannot have control over our thoughts and  
it is not like we desire and hence we have thoughts.   
Only because we cannot have control over our thoughts several techniques like  
breath control,self enquiry.... are mentioned.   
In Bhagavad Gita Ch6 Text35 Lord Krishna says,   
The Blessed Lord said: O mighty-armed son of Kunti, **it is undoubtedly very  
difficult to curb the restless mind, but it is possible by constant practice  
and by detachment.**   
Here detachment means having strong conviction that ' i am not the  
mind,body,senses...' which reminds Adi sankara's Nirvana Satakam poem.   
Once bhagavan said   
If the outlook changes, the troubles of the world will not worry us. Are the  
waves different from the ocean? Why do the waves occur at all? If asked, what  
reply can we give? The troubles in the world also are like that. Waves come  
and go. If it is found out that they are not different from Atma this worry  
will not exist.

## Re:[32] How to watch the sense 'I am'  
Author: Subramanian.R       Date: January 13, 2010, 07:50:48 AM  
---  
Dear srkudai, Nagaraj,   
The sense of "I am" is simply experiencing. For seekers, they have   
to watch the sense of "I am". Thereafter, it is only experiencing   
not describable by thoughts and words and deeds. Bhagavan   
Ramana used to quote Saint Tayumanavar and another old song   
in this context.   
Tayumanavar: It is like a newly married girl, coming out of the nuptial room in   
the early morning. What shall she say about her experience?   
She will not talk or describe to anyone. Even to her mother who   
is waiting anxiously in the morning, she would simply give a small   
smile and rush to take bath! Imagine, a celibate saint poet has   
written this! A celibate Brahma Jnani has quoted this!   
The old song: (Which Devaraja Mudaliar quotes in his book   
"You are my mother and You are my father.": It is like a drunken fellow returning home at night. He does   
not know where his dhoti is, where is towel is, where his bed   
is. He does not want anything. He does not want even food.   
He simply wants to lie in bed with the experience.   
Arunachala Siva.
 ---  
Source:[http://web.archive.org/web/20100707040602/http://www.arunachala-ramana.org/forum/index.php?topic=4337.msg12903](http://web.archive.org/web/20100707040602/http://www.arunachala-ramana.org/forum/index.php?topic=4337.msg12903)   
---  

## Re:[33] How to watch the sense 'I am'  
Author: Nagaraj             Date: January 13, 2010, 05:35:22 PM  
---  
Dear I,   
There is really no sense of experiencing "I am". it is simply being. It  
remains experience so long the Self enquiry continues till the mind/I merges  
where the perfect Self emerges as 'I-I'   
The example quoted by Ramana Maharshi is the first (stage) in what he says: "First the Self sees itself as object, then the Self sees itself as Void, and  
finally it sees itiself as Self, here there is no seeing as seeing is being"   
Therefore,   
Experiencing the sense of "I am" is "First the Self sees itself as object"   
and   
in reality, "I am" is simply being - "and finally it sees itiself as Self,  
here there is no seeing as seeing is being"   
Which is why I have always stressed in my other posts that Bhagawan's answers  
to several questions were tailor made as per the Pakva of the Questioneer.  
Those answers and Dialogues recorded as books should not be taken at face  
value as his answers to our same question. We have seen several instances  
where Bhagawan has responded differently for same questions. But His grace  
shall take care of the devotee all through!   
Salutations to Sri Ramana.

## Re:[38] How to watch the sense 'I am'  
Author: Nagaraj             Date: March 15, 2010, 06:11:00 PM  
---  
Dear I,   
Quote from: Akira on March 15, 2010, 04:14:41 PM  
Quote from: snow on January 07, 2010, 03:06:33 PM  
Nisargadatta Maharaj said that it is very important to watch "I-am-ness" all  
the time.   
How is that possible?   
How can the subject watch the subject itself?  
Bhagavans explanation is given below -   
"First the Self sees itself as object, then the Self sees itself as Void, and  
finally it sees itiself as Self, here there is no seeing as seeing is being"   
The subject is ego, ego first begins watching itself, ego watching ego, and as  
a result of such an enquiry ego ceases to exist and Self shines and when this  
(occurs) the Subject will not be there, the ego will not be there, the very  
need to know that you are the Self has to end.   
Salutations to Sri Ramana
 ---

are arising to"   
Salutations to Sri Ramana

## Re:[38] How to watch the sense 'I am'  
Author: Nagaraj             Date: March 15, 2010, 06:11:00 PM  
---  
Dear I,   
Quote from: Akira on March 15, 2010, 04:14:41 PM  
Quote from: snow on January 07, 2010, 03:06:33 PM  
Nisargadatta Maharaj said that it is very important to watch "I-am-ness" all  
the time.   
How is that possible?   
How can the subject watch the subject itself?  
Bhagavans explanation is given below -   
"First the Self sees itself as object, then the Self sees itself as Void, and  
finally it sees itiself as Self, here there is no seeing as seeing is being"   
The subject is ego, ego first begins watching itself, ego watching ego, and as  
a result of such an enquiry ego ceases to exist and Self shines and when this  
(occurs) the Subject will not be there, the ego will not be there, the very  
need to know that you are the Self has to end.   
Salutations to Sri Ramana
 ---

## Re:[41] How to watch the sense 'I am'  
Author: Nagaraj             Date: March 16, 2010, 05:25:56 AM  
---  
Dear I,   
All interpretations and understanding are correct. There is no need for a  
confirmation from 'anothers' expereience, for understanding. For, it is  
ultimately only an acknowledgement for knowledge what one already has, thats  
all. If 'anothers' experience matches with our existing understanding, mind or  
the ego or the little 'I' nods in confirmation and at the same time, if the  
'anothers' experience does not matches with our existing understanding, mind  
or the ego or the little 'I' nods in non confirmation and this leads to  
discussions, etc... anhd the Mind - ego - little 'I' goes on discussing so  
long the so called 'another' confirms to its own existing or preconceived  
knowledge.   
The 'one' that wants knowledge is the ego, the knowledge that is being created  
in the process is also the ego's. The Mind some how wants to be acknowledged  
as a 'Jnani' or it wants to be acknowledged as a super consciousness, or it  
wants to just enjoy, relish having the title of "Self" or acknowledgement for  
having 'Self-Realised'   
So in all these, who is the one that is wanting to get 'realised'? it is the  
ego - mind - little 'I'. Its like, as a stage drama is being enacted, you act  
as 'Ravana' character and forget that you are just the actor, and as a  
character - 'Ravana' tries to realise its Self as 'Rama' \- which eventually  
becomes another character in itself. The ego - mind - little 'I' gets lost in  
the character of 'Ravana' tries so hard to realised its Self as 'Rama' instead  
of just casting away just the character of Ravana and remain as the one who  
performed the character.   
Salutations to Sri Ramana
 ---  
Source:[http://web.archive.org/web/20100707040233/http://www.arunachala-ramana.org/forum/index.php?topic=4337.msg16250](http://web.archive.org/web/20100707040233/http://www.arunachala-ramana.org/forum/index.php?topic=4337.msg16250)   
---  

## Re:[42] How to watch the sense 'I am'  
Author: Nagaraj             Date: March 16, 2010, 06:15:28 AM  
---  
Dear I,   
that means, like Krishna says in the Gita, Uddaret Atmanaatmaanam, the Self is  
its own friend and foe, one has to lift Himself from his own higher Self and  
not let itself fall from its own lower Self.   
Mis-interpretaions and mis understandings are biggest grace in themselves,  
they bestow higher grace than 'Knowledge' itself. It is only because of Mis-  
interpretaions and mis understandings that we begin to enquire further.   
More over it is only the Mind that distinguishes between Misunderstanding and  
Understanding.   
Meditation, for is just being aware of ones own ego, till it gets dissolved  
into nothingness or everything ness.   
Meditation is for me, "Chumma Iru", "Just being" Let all move around you, Just  
Be.   
Bhagavan says - "To know and not to think"   
Salutations to Sri Ramana
